### [1] [Imaginary Gauge Field and Non-Hermitian Topological Transition Emerging Through Attenuation-Gauge Duality in Conservative Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17557)
*Haoran Nie,Chaoran Jiang,Xiangying Shen,Lei Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种衰减-规范对偶（attenuation-gauge duality）范式，使非厄米拓扑（non-Hermitian topology）能够在完全被动、保守的系统中通过耦合到结构化储层（structured reservoir）而出现，避免了传统方法所需的主动增益-损耗调制或非互易耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统非厄米物理（non-Hermitian physics）依赖于主动增益-损耗调制或非互易耦合，这些方法通常引入显著复杂性、损害稳定性，且在保守系统中可扩展性非常有限。因此需要一种新范式来在被动保守系统中实现非厄米拓扑。

Method: 提出衰减-规范对偶（attenuation-gauge duality）范式，其中空间变化的储层（spatially varying reservoir）可以建立这种对偶关系，使空间变化表现为有效动力学中的涌现虚规范场（emergent imaginary gauge field）。该方法类似于量子开放系统中的Feshbach投影（Feshbach projection）。

Result: 通过宏观机械超材料（macroscopic mechanical metamaterials）验证了这一普适波动范式，证明通过调节单个被动耦合参数t⊥可以逆转趋肤效应（skin effect）的方向，这一过程由谱缠绕数（spectral winding number）表征的拓扑相变驱动。该框架还允许非线性扩展，其中振幅依赖耦合可以诱导本征拓扑转变。

Conclusion: 该衰减-规范对偶范式使非厄米拓扑能够在完全被动、保守的系统中实现，同时保持能量守恒，为在被动系统中实现拓扑趋肤效应（topological skin effect）提供了新途径，并具有非线性扩展潜力。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian physics traditionally relies on active gain--loss modulation or non-reciprocal couplings, which often introduce significant complexity, compromise stability, and offer very limited scalability in conservative systems. Here we propose an attenuation-gauge duality paradigm in which non-Hermitian topology emerges within fully passive, conservative systems through coupling to a structured reservoir. We derive that a spatially varying reservoir can establish an attenuation-gauge duality, where the spatial variation manifests as an emergent imaginary gauge field in the effective dynamics. It drives the boundary accumulation of skin modes while preserving energy conservation, analogous to Feshbach projection in quantum open systems. We validate this universal wave paradigm via macroscopic mechanical metamaterials, demonstrating that the direction of the skin effect can be reversed by tuning a single passive coupling parameter$t_\perp$, driven by a topological phase transition characterized by the spectral winding number. This framework also allows for a nonlinear extension, where amplitude-dependent coupling can induce intrinsic topological transitions.

</details>


<div id='astro-ph.IM'></div>

# astro-ph.IM [[Back]](#toc)

### [2] [Quantifying the Scientific Potential of Intermediate and Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals with the Laser Interferometer Space Antenna](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17072)
*Lorenzo Speri,Francisco Duque,Susanna Barsanti,Alessandro Santini,Shubham Kejriwal,Ollie Burke,Christian E. A. Chapman-Bird*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 该研究评估了LISA空间引力波探测器对极端质量比旋近（EMRIs）和中等质量比旋近（IMRIs）的探测能力，量化了仪器性能对探测视界和参数测量精度的影响，并开发了相关软件工具供社区使用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光干涉空间天线（Laser Interferometer Space Antenna, LISA）将实现对极端质量比旋近（Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals, EMRIs）和中等质量比旋近（Intermediate Mass Ratio Inspirals, IMRIs）的精确研究，为星系核天体物理环境和强场引力提供独特探测手段。研究旨在量化仪器性能对这些系统探测能力的影响。

Method: 采用完全相对论性（fully relativistic）分析流程，覆盖主质量$m_1 \in [5\times10^4, 10^7]\,M_\odot$和次质量$m_2 \in [1, 10^4]\,M_\odot$的范围。通过将仪器性能直接映射到探测视界（detection horizons）和参数测量精度，评估不同质量比系统的灵敏度。

Result: EMRIs（$m_1 = 10^7\,M_\odot$, $m_2 \sim 1\,M_\odot$）对仪器性能退化最敏感，红移视界（redshift horizons）仅$z \sim 0.01$；而IMRIs对退化最不敏感，可达$z \sim 1-3$。所有顺行（prograde）系统在三个月观测内可实现亚百分比的旋转精度测量。完整4.5年任务将$m_1 = 10^7\,M_\odot$系统的视界提高约4倍，天空定位（sky localization）精度提升1-2个数量级至$ < 10\,\mathrm{deg}^2$。

Conclusion: IMRI探测对仪器退化具有鲁棒性，但其参数估计因波段内周期较少而更易受影响。完整基线观测下，EMRI观测可将标量偶极辐射（scalar dipole emission）和Kerr四极矩偏差（Kerr quadrupole deviations）的约束比地基界限低1-2个数量级。研究发布了配套软件和交互式网站，使社区能快速量化EMRIs和IMRIs的科学潜力。

Abstract: The Laser Interferometer Space Antenna (LISA) will enable precision studies of Extreme and Intermediate Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs/IMRIs), providing unique probes of astrophysical environments of galactic nuclei and strong-field gravity. Using a fully relativistic pipeline across primary masses $m_1 \in [5\times10^4, 10^7]\,M_\odot$ and secondary masses $m_2 \in [1, 10^4]\,M_\odot$, we map instrumental performance directly to detection horizons and parameter measurement precision. EMRIs with $m_1 = 10^7\,M_\odot$ and $m_2 \sim 1\,M_\odot$ are the most sensitive to instrument degradation, with redshift horizons at $z \sim 0.01$, while IMRIs are the least sensitive to degradation and reach redshifts $z \sim 1-3$. All prograde systems considered achieve sub-percent spin precision within three months of observation. The full 4.5-year mission increases the horizon of systems with $m_1 = 10^7\,M_\odot$ and $m_2 \sim 1\,M_\odot$ by a factor of $\sim 4$ and improves sky localization by one to two orders of magnitude reaching $ < 10\,\mathrm{deg}^2$. IMRI detection is robust against degradation, but their parameter estimation is more vulnerable due to fewer cycles in band. With the full baseline, EMRI observations constrain scalar dipole emission and Kerr quadrupole deviations below ground-based bounds by one to two orders of magnitude. We release the accompanying software and an interactive website to enable the community to rapidly quantify the scientific potential of EMRIs and IMRIs.

</details>

# quant-ph [[Back]](#toc)

### [3] [Chiral and bond-ordered phases in a triangular-ladder superconducting-qubit quantum simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16993)
*Matthew Molinelli,Joshua C. Wang,Jeronimo G. C. Martinez,Sonny Lowe,Andrew Osborne,Rhine Samajdar,Andrew A. Houck*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究利用超导量子比特（superconducting qubits）模拟三角梯子晶格上的玻色-哈伯德模型（Bose-Hubbard model），通过调控合成磁通（synthetic magnetic flux）表征了不同参数区域下的半填充基态，观测到手性超流体（chiral superfluids）、迈斯纳超流体（Meissner superfluids）和键序绝缘体（bond-ordered insulators）等量子相的特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强相互作用多体系统（many-body systems）常展现出单粒子或非相互作用极限中不存在的宏观行为。晶格哈伯德模型（lattice Hubbard models）中相互作用、几何阻挫（geometric frustration）和磁通（magnetic flux）的相互作用产生了丰富的物理现象，而超导量子比特为模拟玻色-哈伯德模型提供了可调参数、位点分辨控制和快速实验重复率的平台。

Method: 研究使用超导量子比特器件实现三角梯子晶格（triangular-ladder lattice）上的玻色-哈伯德模型。通过调控耦合的大小和符号，工程化合成磁通以表征不同参数区域下的半填充基态（half-filling ground state）。测量了类似于电流-电流关联器（current-current correlators）和键动能（bond kinetic energies）的观测量。

Result: 实验观测到与手性超流体、迈斯纳超流体和键序绝缘体一致的特征信号。这些结果表明超导电路能够稳健地探测阻挫玻色-哈伯德系统中的量子相（quantum phases of matter），即使在强关联（strongly correlated）和无能隙（gapless）区域也是如此。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了超导电路作为研究阻挫玻色-哈伯德系统中量子物质相（quantum phases of matter）的稳健平台，特别是在强关联和无能隙区域，为探索多体系统的涌现现象（emergent phenomena）提供了新的实验途径。

Abstract: Many-body systems with strong interactions often exhibit macroscopic behavior markedly absent in single-particle or noninteracting limits. Such emergent phenomena are well exemplified in lattice Hubbard models, where the interplay between interactions, geometric frustration, and magnetic flux gives rise to rich physics. Superconducting qubits naturally enable analog quantum simulation of Bose-Hubbard models, while offering tunable parameters, site-resolved control, and rapid experimental repetition rates. Here, we study a superconducting-qubit device that realizes the Bose-Hubbard model on a triangular-ladder lattice. By tuning the magnitude and sign of couplings, we engineer a synthetic magnetic flux to characterize the resulting half-filling ground state for various parameter regimes. We measure observables analogous to current-current correlators and bond kinetic energies, finding signatures consistent with chiral superfluids, Meissner superfluids, and bond-ordered insulators. Our results establish superconducting circuits as a platform for robustly probing quantum phases of matter in frustrated Bose-Hubbard systems, even in strongly correlated and gapless regimes.

</details>


### [4] [Generation of many-body Bell correlations with short-range interactions in analog and digital quantum simulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17071)
*Marcin Płodzień,Jan Chwedeńczuk*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文展示了两种自旋链模型（交错最近邻XXX链和长程XXZ链）在对称子空间投影下能有效实现单轴扭曲动力学，从而生成可用于量子计量学的自旋压缩态和违反多体贝尔不等式的量子关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子资源（如多体纠缠或贝尔关联）的动态生成通常需要全连接的单轴扭曲动力学，但当前数字和模拟量子仿真平台仅提供短程或幂律衰减耦合，无法满足这一需求。

Method: 研究两种自旋-1/2链模型：交错最近邻XXX链（staggered nearest-neighbor XXX chain）和长程XXZ链（long-range XXZ chain）。通过将动力学投影到对称子空间（symmetric sector），展示这些系统能有效实现单轴扭曲非线性（OAT nonlinearity）。

Result: 这些动力学能生成计量学上有用的自旋压缩态（spin-squeezed states）和Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger相干性，确保违反多体贝尔不等式（many-body Bell inequalities）。通过与精确动力学比较验证了映射的准确性，并证明生成的关联可通过单个探测量子比特读出。

Conclusion: 所实现的动力学可在模拟和数字量子仿真器上进行模拟，为在现有量子平台上实现量子资源生成提供了可行方案。

Abstract: The dynamical generation of quantum resources, such as many-body entanglement or Bell correlations, can be achieved via one-axis twisting (OAT) dynamics, which require all-to-all couplings. However, current digital and analog quantum simulation platforms natively provide short-range or power-law couplings that decay too quickly for this purpose. We demonstrate that two spin-$\tfrac12$ chain models -- a staggered nearest-neighbor XXX chain and a long-range XXZ chain -- develop an effective OAT nonlinearity when projected onto the symmetric sector. We show that these dynamics generate metrologically useful spin-squeezed states and Greenberger-Horne-Zeilinger coherences that ensure violation of many-body Bell inequalities. We confirm the accuracy of this mapping by comparing it to the exact dynamics and demonstrate that the generated correlations can be read out using a single probe qubit. The resulting dynamics can be simulated with analog and digital quantum simulators

</details>


### [5] [Die to wafer direct bonding of (100) single-crystal diamond thin films for quantum optoelectronics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17140)
*Dominic Lepage,Amin Yaghoobi,Heidi Tremblay,Dominique Drouin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一种半导体兼容的工艺，能够将多个高质量超薄单晶金刚石（SCD）薄膜直接键合到载体晶圆上，为纳米光子量子系统的大规模制造提供了可扩展的解决方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在解决纳米光子量子系统制造中的关键挑战，即如何利用单晶金刚石（single-crystal diamond, SCD）的独特材料特性进行大规模制造。传统方法受限于金刚石材料的加工难度和集成限制。

Method: 研究引入了一种新的金刚石表面制备方法，避免了沸腾三酸混合物处理，能够生产出极其洁净的20微米薄单晶。这些薄片被并排键合到100毫米二氧化硅晶圆上，实现了范德华（van der Waals）相互作用主导的键合机制。

Result: 该方法实现了(100)取向金刚石45.1 MPa的创纪录剪切强度，超越了所有先前报道的键合尝试。异质结构在液体浸泡和标准纳米加工步骤中保持稳定，且该工艺主要依赖于表面清洁度和粗糙度，可广泛适用于不同晶圆材料。

Conclusion: 将超薄单晶金刚石薄膜并行键合到大面积衬底上的能力，为纳米光子量子技术、高功率电子学、微机电系统（MEMS）和生物技术等领域的高性能平台提供了可扩展的制造路径。

Abstract: This work unlocks the manufacturing of nanophotonic quantum systems that exploit the unique material properties of single-crystal diamond (SCD). We achieve this by introducing a semiconductor-compatible process for the direct bonding of multiple high-quality, ultrathin diamond films onto a carrier wafer, enabling the subsequent parallel nanofabrication of optoelectronic integrated circuits. Central to this approach is a new diamond surface-preparation method that avoids boiling tri-acid mixtures while producing exceptionally clean 20 um thin single crystals. These platelets are bonded side-by-side to 100 mm silica wafers and exhibit a record shear strength of 45.1 MPa for (100)-oriented diamond, surpassing all previously reported bonding attempts. Evidence indicates that the bonding is dominated by van der Waals interactions, likely arising from mismatched protonation mechanisms between Si-OH and C-OH surface terminations, rather than from covalent-bond-driven mechanisms. Despite this non-molecular nature, the heterostructures remain stable through liquid immersions and standard nanofabrication steps. Because the method depends primarily on surface cleanliness and roughness rather than specific chemistries, it is broadly transferable across wafer materials. This capability to parallel-bond ultrathin SCD films onto large-area substrates provides a scalable route to high-performance platforms spanning nanophotonic quantum technologies, high-power electronics, MEMS, and biotechnology.

</details>


### [6] [Engineering strong coupling with molecular coatings in optical nanocavities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17269)
*Athul S. Rema,Adrián E. Rubio López,Felipe Herrera*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 通过在银纳米颗粒表面涂覆J-聚集体分子层，形成核壳结构，可以重构局域电磁真空场，使量子发射体从弱耦合转变为强耦合，实现拉比振荡。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 银纳米颗粒表面的量子发射体通常只能与近场多极模式发生强耦合，而低频偶极模式虽然具有辐射性但耦合强度不足，这限制了强耦合现象的观测。

Method: 采用宏观量子电动力学理论，在非马尔可夫相互作用核的洛伦兹赝模近似下，研究涂覆J-聚集体分子层的银纳米球核壳结构。具体分析半径为20纳米的银纳米球近场中量子点发射体与2纳米J-聚集体壳层的相互作用。

Result: 核壳结构的plexciton共振在偶极模式频率下重构了局域电磁真空场，使原本仅经历指数衰减的量子发射体能够实现拉比振荡。J-聚集体壳层成功诱导了弱耦合到强耦合的转变。

Conclusion: 分子聚集体具有在深亚波长尺度上结构化真空场的潜力，为在光学纳米腔中观测相干量子动力学提供了新途径。

Abstract: Quantum emitters near the surface of silver nanoparticles undergo Rabi oscillations in electronic population dynamics due to strong coupling with near-field multipole modes that are not radiative. Low-frequency nanoparticle dipole modes are radiative but do not couple strong enough to quantum emitters. These features limit the observation of strong coupling. Using macroscopic quantum electrodynamics theory within a Lorentzian pseudo-mode approximation for the non-Markovian interaction kernel, we demonstrate that by coating spherical silver nanoparticles with a thin molecular J-aggregate layer, the resulting core-shell plexciton resonance restructures the local electromagnetic vacuum at dipole-mode frequencies to enable Rabi oscillations for quantum emitters that otherwise would only undergo exponential population decay. Specifically, we show for quantum dot emitters in the near field of silver nanospheres of 20 nm radius, that weak-to-strong coupling crossovers can be induced using 2 nm J-aggregate shells. Our work demonstrates the potential of molecular aggregates to enable deep sub-wavelength structuring of the vacuum field for the observation of coherent quantum dynamics in optical nanocavities.

</details>


### [7] [Geometry and restoration of the quantum Mpemba effect beyond weak-coupling regime in the spin-boson model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17565)
*P. Chirico,G. Di Bello,G. De Filippis,C. A. Perroni*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了开放量子系统中自旋-玻色子模型的量子姆潘巴效应（quantum Mpemba effect），发现该效应的出现强烈依赖于距离度量的选择，并揭示了系统-环境关联和几何结构在反常量子弛豫中的作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解开放量子系统中的弛豫动力学是非平衡量子物理的核心问题。研究旨在探索自旋-玻色子模型中的量子姆潘巴效应，该效应描述了某些初始状态比更接近平衡态的状态更快弛豫的反常现象。

Method: 在弱耦合马尔可夫（weak-coupling Markovian）区域分析不同距离度量的影响，并超越弱耦合近似，对完整系统-浴（system-bath）动力学进行数值精确模拟。研究还分析了在布洛赫球（Bloch sphere）上的几何结构。

Result: 量子姆潘巴效应在低温下强烈依赖于距离度量的选择：在迹距离（trace distance）中出现，但在量子相对熵（quantum relative entropy）中可能消失。增强耦合会增强迹距离中的效应，并在量子相对熵中恢复该效应。在去局域化-局域化量子相变（delocalized-localized quantum phase transition）之前的所有自旋-浴耦合中，激发态半球内通过旋转相关的状态对普遍表现出弛豫顺序反转。

Conclusion: 这些结果突显了几何结构和系统-环境关联在反常量子弛豫中的关键作用，为理解开放量子系统的弛豫动力学提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Understanding relaxation dynamics in open quantum systems is a central problem in nonequilibrium quantum physics. Here we investigate the quantum Mpemba effect in the spin-boson model. In the weak-coupling Markovian regime we show that the occurrence of the effect strongly depends on the choice of distance measure at low temperature: while it appears in the trace distance, it can disappear in the quantum relative entropy. Going beyond the weak-coupling approximation, numerically exact simulations of the full system-bath dynamics reveal that increasing coupling enhances the effect in the trace distance and restores it in the quantum relative entropy. For all spin-bath couplings prior to delocalized-localized quantum phase transition, we uncover a simple geometric structure of the effect on the Bloch sphere: within the excited-state hemisphere, pairs of states related by rotations generically exhibit relaxation-order inversion. These results highlight the role of geometry and system-environment correlations in anomalous quantum relaxation.

</details>


### [8] [Implementation of non-local arbitrary two-qubit controlled gates via geometric quantum computation with Rydberg anti-blockade](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17656)
*Le-Jiang Yu,Jia Zheng,Kun Pu,Chao Gao*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于里德堡反阻塞（Rydberg anti-blockade）和非绝热几何量子计算（non-adiabatic holonomic quantum computation）的高保真度受控酉门（controlled-unitary gate）方案。该方案通过脉冲参数逆向工程（reverse engineering）实现合适的演化路径，并在自发辐射和激光强度误差下保持高保真度，可扩展至非局域门（non-local gates）并应用于四量子比特纠缠态转换。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在里德堡反阻塞（Rydberg anti-blockade）背景下，本文旨在提出一种高保真度受控酉门（controlled-unitary gate）的新方案。该方案基于非绝热几何量子计算（non-adiabatic holonomic quantum computation），旨在实现复杂量子信息处理任务中的高精度量子门操作。

Method: 在特定失谐（detuning）和相互作用条件下，通过脉冲参数逆向工程（reverse engineering）实现非绝热几何量子计算（non-adiabatic holonomic quantum computation）的合适演化路径。该方法考虑了自发辐射（spontaneous radiation）和激光强度误差（laser intensity errors）等实际因素。

Result: 数值模拟（numerical simulations）显示，几何门（geometric gate）在自发辐射（spontaneous radiation）和激光强度误差（laser intensity errors）存在时仍能保持高保真度（high fidelity）。该方案可扩展至非局域门（non-local gates），并应用于四量子比特纠缠态（four-qubit entangled states）的转换。

Conclusion: 该方案展示了在里德堡反阻塞（Rydberg anti-blockade）系统中实现高保真度几何量子门的可行性。研究结果表明该方案具有应用于复杂量子信息处理任务（complex quantum information processing tasks）的潜在适用性。

Abstract: In the context of Rydberg anti-blockade, this paper proposes a new scheme for a high-fidelity controlled-unitary gate based on non-adiabatic holonomic quantum computation. Under specific detuning and interaction conditions, the scheme achieves a suitable evolution path for non-adiabatic holonomic quantum computation through reverse engineering of pulse parameters. Numerical simulations show that the geometric gate maintains high fidelity even in the presence of spontaneous radiation and laser intensity errors. Finally,we extend our designed quantum gates to non-local gates and investigate their use in converting four-qubit entangled states. This finding indicates the potential applicability of our scheme to complex quantum information processing tasks.

### [9] [CaRBM: A Fixed-Depth Quantum Algorithm with Partial Correction for Thermal State Preparation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17971)
*Omar Alsheikh,A. F. Kemper,Ermal Rrapaj,Goksu C. Toga*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: CaRBM算法用于固定深度热态制备，基于热态纯化和受限玻尔兹曼机块编码方案，通过Cartan分解实现虚时传播子。算法在高温下表现最佳，通过校正方案扩展温度范围，应用于XXZ模型配分函数零点和Gross-Neveu模型相图计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在解决固定深度热态制备问题，特别是在量子电路中实现虚时传播子$e^{-βH}$的高效实现。需要开发能够在量子电路中以固定深度方式执行热态制备的算法。

Method: CaRBM算法基于热态纯化（thermal state purification）和受限玻尔兹曼机块编码方案（Restricted Boltzmann Machine block-encoding scheme），通过Cartan分解在量子电路中以固定深度方式实现虚时传播子。设计了块编码校正方案以提高成功概率。

Result: 算法在高温下表现最佳，块编码成功概率随温度降低而下降。校正方案成功扩展了算法可靠探测的温度范围。通过计算XXZ模型的配分函数零点和Gross-Neveu模型的相图验证了算法有效性。

Conclusion: CaRBM算法为固定深度热态制备提供了有效解决方案，特别适用于高温区域。校正方案增强了算法的温度适用范围，使其能够可靠探测更广泛的温度范围，并在强相互作用相对论费米子模型中展示了应用潜力。

Abstract: We introduce the CaRBM algorithm for fixed-depth thermal state preparation. Our algorithm is based on thermal state purification and uses the Restricted Boltzmann Machine (RBM) block-encoding scheme to implement the imaginary-time propagator $e^{-βH}$, which is implemented in the quantum circuit in a fixed-depth manner via Cartan decomposition. Our algorithm performs best at high temperatures, with the success probability of the block encoding decreasing as the temperature decreases. To increase the success probability, we have devised a correction scheme for the block-encoding that increases the temperature range our algorithm reliably probes. We demonstrate our algorithm by calculating the partition function zeros of the XXZ model and the phase diagram of the Gross-Neveu model, which is a model of strongly interacting relativistic fermions.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在精确测量相干弹性中微子-核散射（coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering, CEνNS）截面，这是标准模型预测但实验验证具有挑战性的基本过程。精确测量对于检验标准模型和探索超出标准模型的新物理至关重要。

Method: 研究使用COHERENT合作组的锗探测器阵列（Ge-Mini），在美国橡树岭国家实验室的散裂中子源（Spallation Neutron Source）进行测量。通过累积4.68×10²²个靶上质子（protons on target）的曝光量，观测到124个事件，并利用中微子源的精确能量和时间分布特性，独立测量了μ子中微子和电子中微子的散射率。

Result: 测量得到的总观测计数为124⁺¹⁴₋₁₂，通量平均截面为1.00±0.10（统计误差）±0.10（系统误差），相对于标准模型预期值5.9×10⁻³⁹ cm²。该结果与标准模型预测一致，是目前最精确的CEνNS截面测量。

Conclusion: 该精确测量结果不仅验证了标准模型对相干弹性中微子-核散射的预测，还利用μ子中微子和电子中微子散射率的独立测量信息，显著改进了对重粒子介导的非标准中微子相互作用（non-standard neutrino interactions）的限制。

Abstract: The COHERENT collaboration reports the most precise measurement of the coherent elastic neutrino-nucleus scattering cross section to date. This measurement was performed with COHERENT's germanium detector array, Ge-Mini, at the Spallation Neutron Source at Oak Ridge National Laboratory. A cumulative exposure of $4.68\times10^{22}$ protons on target yielded a total number of observed counts of $124^{+14}_{-12}$ and a flux-averaged cross section of $1.00 \pm 0.10 \mathrm{(statistical)} \pm 0.10 \mathrm{(systematic)}$ relative to the standard-model expectation of $5.9\times10^{-39} \mathrm{cm}^2$. The well-understood energy and timing distributions of the neutrino source allow for independent measurements of muon- and electron-neutrino scattering rates. This information is used to improve constraints on non-standard neutrino interactions mediated by heavy particles.

### [12] [Machine intelligence supports the full chain of 2D dendrite synthesis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16959)
*Wenqiang Huang,Susu Fang,Xuhang Gu,Shen'ao Xue,Huanhuan Xing,Junjie Jiang,Junying Zhang,Shen Zhou,Zheng Luo,Jin Zhang,Fangping Ouyang,Shanshan Wang*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维树枝状晶体的化学气相沉积生长具有催化应用潜力，但面临参数密集、数据稀缺和反应过程复杂的挑战，需要开发高效的方法来支持材料合成的全链条研究。

Method: 首先将主动学习（active learning）整合到实验工作流中，通过60次实验（4次迭代）优化工艺参数；然后开发预测精度引导的数据增强策略，结合基于树的机器学习算法；最后构建数据-知识双驱动的机理模型，整合跨尺度表征、可解释ML模型以及热力学和动力学领域知识。

Result: 该方法仅通过60次实验（占总可能参数组合的1.3%）就找到了高分支、电催化活性ReSe2树枝状晶体的最优配方；通过仅增加9次实验揭示了5个工艺变量与分形维度（fractal dimension）的非线性关系，并实现了用户定义分形维度的定制合成；解析了多个工艺参数对产物形貌的协同贡献机制。

Conclusion: 该工作展示了机器学习在转变研究范式方面的潜力，所开发的框架可适应更广泛的材料合成领域，为参数密集、数据稀缺的复杂材料合成问题提供了有效的解决方案。

Abstract: Exemplified by the chemical vapor deposition growth of two-dimensional dendrites, which has potential applications in catalysis and presents a parameter-intensive, data-scarce and reaction process-complex model problem, we devise a machine intelligence-empowered framework for the full chain support of material synthesis, encompassing rapid process optimization, accurate customized synthesis, and comprehensive mechanism deciphering.First, active learning is integrated into the experimental workflow, identifying an optimal recipe for the growth of highly-branched, electrocatalytically-active ReSe2 dendrites through 60 experiments (4 iterations), which account for less than 1.3% of the numerous possible parameter combinations.Then, a prediction accuracy-guided data augmentation strategy is developed combined with a tree-based machine learning (ML) algorithm, unveiling a non-linear correlation between 5 process variables and fractal dimension (DF) of ReSe2 dendrites with only 9 experiment additions, which guides the synthesis of various user-defined DF. Finally, we construct a data-knowledge dual-driven mechanism model by integration of cross-scale characterizations, interpretable ML models, and domain knowledge in thermodynamics and kinetics, unraveling synergistic contributions of multiple process parameters to the product morphology. This work demonstrates the ML potential to transform the research paradigm and is adaptable to broader material synthesis.

### [13] [From pore collapse to crystal growth: ultrafast laser-induced stishovite formation in nanoporous silica](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16968)
*Aram Yedigaryan,Mohamed Yaseen Noor,Elena Kachan,Gabriel Calderon,Jinwoo Hwang,Enam Chowdhury,Jean-Philippe Colombier*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过多尺度模拟揭示了纳米孔界面在超快激光辐照下作为电磁热点（electromagnetic hotspots）催化非晶态二氧化硅向高压相stishovite晶体转变的机制，证明了纳米孔能显著加速相变过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索超快激光辐照下非晶态固体结晶这一非平衡相变（non-equilibrium phase transitions）过程中，电磁能量局域化（electromagnetic energy localization）与原子尺度动力学之间的相互作用机制。

Method: 采用多尺度框架（multiscale framework），将非线性光传播的时域有限差分（Finite-Difference Time-Domain, FDTD）模拟与原子响应的分子动力学（Molecular Dynamics, MD）模拟相耦合，研究含纳米孔的二氧化硅结构。

Result: 纳米孔界面处的场增强（field enhancement）局域化激光能量，驱动周围基质的快速塌陷；2纳米孔径（孔隙率约7%）系统的局域电磁场使最终平衡温度比1纳米孔径（孔隙率1%）高16%，比均匀介质高20%；异质性能量局域化在致密玻璃网络中形成优先成核位点，导致stishovite（高压SiO2晶相）在亚纳秒时间尺度上超快形成。

Conclusion: 加速的结晶过程使相变能够超越压力弛豫（pressure relaxation），从而在相同热载荷下实现stishovite的形成；纳米孔可作为通过定制电磁热点（electromagnetic hotspots）控制固态转变的有效催化剂，这与受限几何结构中激光诱导结晶的实验观察一致。

Abstract: The crystallization of amorphous solids under ultrafast laser irradiation represents a paradigm of non-equilibrium phase transitions, where the interplay between electromagnetic energy localization and atomic-scale dynamics remains largely uncharted. By using a multiscale framework that couples Finite-Difference Time-Domain simulations of nonlinear light propagation with Molecular Dynamics of the atomic response, we demonstrate that field enhancement at nanopore interfaces confines laser energy and drives a rapid collapse of the surrounding matrix. In the silica structure containing a nanopore of 2 nm radius, corresponding to a porosity of approximately 7%, the enhanced local electromagnetic field led to a final equilibrium temperature 16% higher than for the 1-nm pore (1% porosity), and 20% higher than for the homogeneous medium. Particularly, the heterogeneous energy localization in the 2-nm-pore system created a preferential nucleation site within the dense glass network and led to the ultrafast formation of stishovite, a high-pressure crystalline phase of SiO2, on a sub-nanosecond timescale, significantly faster than in homogeneous silica at the same equilibrium temperature. Such accelerated crystallization enables the phase transition to outpace pressure relaxation, which would otherwise inhibit stishovite formation under identical thermal loading. These predictions align with experimental observations of laser-induced crystallization in confined geometries and establish nanopores as potent catalysts for controlling solid-state transformations via tailored electromagnetic hotspots.

### [14] [Accelerating Structure-Property Relationship Discovery with Multimodal Machine Learning and Self-Driving Microscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17028)
*Jiawei Gong,Danqing Ma,Ralph Bulanadi,Robert Moore,Rama Vasudevan,Lianfeng Zhao,Yongtao Liu*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 该框架整合了自主显微镜、双新颖性深度核学习（dual-novelty deep kernel learning, DN-DKL）用于自适应数据采集，以及双变分自编码器（dual variational autoencoder, dual-VAE）用于表示学习。DN-DKL主动引导显微镜探索结构和光谱学上新颖的区域，而dual-VAE将局部结构和光谱响应嵌入共享的潜在流形。

Result: 应用该框架于卤化物钙钛矿薄膜的导电原子力显微镜（conductive atomic force microscopy）研究，揭示了与特定纳米尺度结构基元相关的独特滞后行为。具体包括在不同偏压条件下显示滞后的晶界连接点，以及抑制电荷传输的不对称晶界。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了一种通用策略，利用自主显微镜、机器学习和人类专业知识的互补优势，加速功能材料领域的科学发现。它能够高效收集大型光谱数据集，并建立结构-性能关系图谱。

Abstract: Microscopy combined with local spectroscopy is widely used to correlate nanoscale structure with functional properties in materials, but conventional measurements rely heavily on human-selected sampling locations and predefined targets, limiting dataset diversity and the potential for discovery. Here, we present a framework that integrates autonomous microscopy with a dual-novelty deep kernel learning (DN-DKL) for adaptive data acquisition and a dual variational autoencoder (VAE) for representation learning. DN-DKL actively guides the microscopy toward structurally and spectroscopically novel regions, enabling efficient collection of large spectral datasets. Dual-VAE embeds local structure and spectroscopic responses into a shared latent manifold that serves as a structure-property relationship map. We applied this framework for the investigation of halide perovskite films using conductive atomic force microscopy. The results reveal distinct hysteresis behaviors that are linked to specific nanoscale structural motifs, including grain boundary junction points that show hysteresis under different bias conditions and asymmetric grain boundaries that suppress charge transport. This framework establishes a general strategy that leverages the complementary strengths of self-driving microscopy, machine learning, and human expertise to accelerate scientific discovery in functional materials.

### [15] [Engineering Quantum Phases in Two Dimensions via Vacancy-Induced Electronic Reconstruction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17122)
*Emmanuel V. C. Lopes,Felipe Crasto de Lima,Caio Lewenkopf,Adalberto Fazzio*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 原子空位（vacancies）可诱导二维半导体发生拓扑相变，将原本平庸的绝缘体转变为量子自旋霍尔、量子反常霍尔或外尔半金属等拓扑量子物态，为缺陷工程拓扑器件提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实材料中结构缺陷（structural defects）天然结合了晶体对称性、自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling）和无序驱动的电子重整化（electronic renormalization）两种拓扑相形成机制。本研究旨在探索原子空位作为主动设计元素，而非仅仅是微扰，诱导拓扑相变的普遍机制。

Method: 采用紧束缚模型（tight-binding framework）结合大规模密度泛函理论计算（large-scale density functional theory calculations），分析空位产生的局域悬挂键态（dangling-bond states）及其通过空间分布和相互耦合形成的长程无序（long-range disorder）。

Result: 随着空位浓度增加，缺陷态杂化形成涌现电子子空间（emergent electronic subspace），该子空间经历拓扑相变。根据对称性破缺（symmetry breaking）和自旋极化（spin polarization）条件，空位诱导的电子重构（electronic reconstruction）可稳定产生量子自旋霍尔（quantum spin Hall）、量子反常霍尔（quantum anomalous Hall）和外尔半金属（Weyl semimetal）相。

Conclusion: 原子空位不仅是微扰，而是能够将平庸绝缘体转变为拓扑量子物质（topological quantum matter）的主动设计元素。这一发现为缺陷工程拓扑器件（defect-engineered topological devices）开辟了现实可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Topological phases of matter are commonly understood as emerging either from crystalline symmetry and intrinsic spin-orbit coupling or from disorder-driven electronic renormalization. In realistic materials, however, structural defects naturally combine both ingredients. Here, we demonstrate a general and material-independent mechanism by which atomic vacancies can induce topological phase transitions in two-dimensional semiconductors that are otherwise topologically trivial. Vacancies generate locally ordered dangling-bond states governed by well-defined hopping and spin-orbit interactions, while their spatial distribution and mutual coupling introduce long-range disorder. As vacancy concentration increases, the hybridization of these defect states forms an emergent electronic subspace that undergoes a topological transition. Using a tight-binding framework supported by large-scale density functional theory calculations, we show that this vacancy-induced electronic reconstruction can robustly stabilize quantum spin Hall, quantum anomalous Hall, and Weyl semimetal phases, depending on symmetry breaking and spin polarization. Our results establish vacancies not merely as perturbations, but as active design elements capable of transforming trivial insulators into topological quantum matter, opening realistic routes for defect-engineered topological devices.

</details>

Conclusion: 该研究通过冲击压缩实验获得了FeO在极端条件下的自旋状态数据，为（系外）行星内部的地球物理模型提供了关键实验依据，特别是揭示了高自旋状态在深部行星环境中的持续存在。

Abstract: FeO (wüstite), which exhibits complex electronic and structural properties with increasing pressure and temperature, is a key mineralogical phase for understanding deep planetary interiors. However, direct measurements of its spin state at high-pressure and temperature remain challenging in static compression experiments. Here, we employ laser-driven shock compression to extend the FeO principal Hugoniot up to $\sim$900 GPa and perform in situ X-ray diffraction and X-ray emission spectroscopy up to 250 GPa, probing FeO's crystal structure and spin state. We demonstrate a continuous spin crossover of iron in FeO over a broad pressure range, with the high-spin state persisting beyond Earth's core-mantle boundary (CMB) conditions. These observations provide new experimental constraints on iron spin state at extreme conditions essential for geophysical models of (exo)planetary interiors.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 无序岩盐（DRX）阴极材料在锂离子电池中具有高能量密度和低成本潜力，但其功率密度和循环稳定性需要优化。合成条件（如退火温度和时间）决定了成分和颗粒尺寸/形貌，这促使研究者需要理解LMTO岩盐相空间的相图，特别是通过量化有序-无序转变温度（T_disord）来理解DRX的稳定性。

Method: 研究结合第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）和X射线衍射实验（X-ray diffraction experiments），建立了位于LiMnO₂-Li₂MnO₃-Li₂TiO₃赝三元体系内的LMTO相图。

Conclusion: 特定DRX成分的有序-无序转变温度（T_disord）显著低于传统合成温度，这为降低合成温度提供了可能性。研究建立的相图为优化LMTO DRX材料的成分和合成条件提供了重要指导。

Abstract: Disordered rock-salt with Li-excess (DRX) cathode phases within the Li-Mn-Ti-O (LMTO) composition space have recently been extensively studied, as they promise to deliver exceptional energy density at low cost in Li-ion batteries. The continued development of LMTO DRX with improved power density and cycling stability requires optimization of the composition and particle size/morphology, which are determined by synthesis conditions such as annealing temperatures and hold times. Importantly, a significant range of LMTO compositions containing small to moderate fractions of Li-excess and Ti doping (relative to LiMnO$_2$) have $T_\text{disord}$ spanning $700 - 900$ C. These temperatures are substantially lower than conventional DRX synthesis temperatures ($\geq 1000$ C), suggesting the promise of decreasing synthesis temperatures for specific DRX compositions. Here, we demonstrate a general strategy for the purely electrical switching of the SkHE in two-dimensional altermagnets. Crucially, we show that an external electric field can strongly modulate these interaction parameters by inversing the altermagnetic symmetry, allowing for the reversible inversion of the anisotropic SkHE.   <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过系统分类所有1651个磁空间群（magnetic space groups, MSGs），分析无自旋轨道耦合（spin-orbit coupling, SOC）和有SOC条件下的兼容性。对于非磁性晶体，特别关注手性空间群92和96的自旋极限情况。

Here, by systematically classifying all 1651 magnetic space groups (MSGs), we reveal that only 14 MSGs without spin-orbit coupling (SOC) and 10 MSGs with SOC are compatible with this exotic state. Furthermore, for nonmagnetic crystals, this configuration is uniquely realized in the spinless limit of chiral space groups 92 and 96. Guided by this principle, we predict an ideal realization in chiral three-dimensional boron allotropes (SDHBN-B$_{28}$ enantiomers). First-principles calculations unveil a $|C|=2$ WP at the $Γ$ point and a $|C|=2$ DP at the $A$ point, which constitute the only fermions near the Fermi level within a large $2$ eV energy window. Motivation: 高压实验中，H2O样品通常直接接触金刚石压砧，但界面效应对测量性质（包括冰相共存线）的影响程度未知。研究旨在阐明界面如何影响高压冰相的各种性质，包括超离子态、固-固相变和熔化。

Method: 结合人工神经网络方法和主动学习方案，进行大规模分子动力学模拟，以研究金刚石压砧界面对高压冰相性质的影响。

Result: 界面显著降低氢超离子转变温度，并可通过逆贝恩机制（inverse Bain mechanism）诱导bcc到fcc冰的自发转变。研究重新定义了bcc和fcc冰在熔化线以下的稳定场，并预测fcc冰可在比先前认为低得多的压力下存在。

Conclusion: 界面效应对于理解高压冰实验研究中报告的各种现象（包括理论与实验结果之间的不一致性）至关重要，强调了在高压实验研究中考虑界面影响的重要性。

Abstract: High-pressure experiments using diamond anvils have revealed novel properties and phase behavior of H2O under extreme conditions. When contained in diamond-anvil cells, the H2O samples are usually in direct contact with the diamond anvil. However, the extent to which this interface affects measured pressure-induced properties and behavior, including coexistence lines of ice phases, remains unknown. Combining artificial neural network methods and active learning schemes with large-scale molecular dynamics simulations, we elucidate the interfacial effects on various properties of high-pressure ice phases, including superionic states, solid-solid phase transitions, and melting. The results reveal that the presence of this interface can significantly lower the hydrogen superionic transition temperature. Remarkably, the interface can also induce a spontaneous transition from bcc- to fcc-based ice following the inverse Bain mechanism. Further, we redefined a stability field of bcc and fcc ice below the melting line and predicted the existence of fcc ice at much lower pressures than previously thought. More broadly, the results emphasize the importance of interface effects in understanding a wide range of phenomena reported in experimental studies of ice under pressure, including inconsistencies between theoretical and experimental results of this fundamental system.

### [24] [Identification of sub-angstrom many-body localization in quantum materials by Bragg scattering phase breaking and ultrafast structural dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17591)
*Yingpeng Qi,Jianmin Yang,Zhihui Zhou,Qing Xu,Yang Lv,Xiao Zou,Tao Jiang,Pengfei Zhu,Dongxue Chen,Zhenrong Sun,Lin Xie,Dao Xiang,Jiaqing He*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究提出基于光激发超快结构响应的布拉格散射相位破缺机制，用于识别量子材料中亚埃尺度的局域关联结构。在AgCrSe2中成功识别出多体相互作用驱动的静态局域关联结构，揭示了其与奇特量子性质的内在联系。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 缺陷、涨落、简并态和关联相互作用在凝聚态系统中诱导出偏离平均长程有序的原子尺度局域关联结构，但由于缺乏直接识别这些结构的方法，从该视角建立结构-性质关系仍存在模糊性和争议。

Method: 基于光激发超快结构响应，提出布拉格散射相位破缺机制（Bragg scattering phase breaking regime）来识别量子材料中的亚埃尺度局域关联结构。采用最先进的密度泛函理论（density functional theory）模拟验证实验结果。

Result: 在AgCrSe2的低温基态中明确识别出多体相互作用驱动的局域关联结构，其中Ag原子存在0-0.5埃的静态偏离中心位移。温度升高时，这些静态结构转变为热涨落主导的动态态，表明局域结构具有强非谐性。

Conclusion: 这些独特的局域关联结构首次在真实材料系统中证明了具有拓扑序特征的多体局域化，为AgCrSe2单晶的多种量子性质提供了统一解释。该方法不仅为广泛量子材料中亚埃尺度局域关联结构的表征提供了通用途径，还从原子尺度局域关联结构视角深化了对奇特性质基本机制的理解。

Abstract: Defects, fluctuations, degenerate states and correlated interactions facilitate the emergence of exotic properties in condensed matter systems while also inducing atomic-scale local correlated structures that deviate from the average long-range order. Establishing the structure-property relationship from the perspective of these atomic-scale local correlated structures remains ambiguous and controversial due to the lack of direct methods for identifying such local correlated structures. In this work, based on the photoexcited ultrafast structural response, we propose a Bragg scattering phase breaking regime to identify the sub-angstrom local correlated structures in quantum materials. With this regime, we unambiguously identify the many-body-interaction driven local correlated structures with static off-center Ag displacements of 0 to 0.5 angstrom in the low temperature ground state of AgCrSe2. As temperature rising, these static local correlated structures transform to a dynamic state where the thermal fluctuations overwhelm the multiple localized quantum states, signifying the strong anharmonicity of the local structures. The state-of-the-art density functional theory simulation well reproduces the intrinsic many-body-interaction driven local correlated structures. These unique local correlated structures evidence the first many-body localization with topological order characteristic in real material systems and provide a unified scenario for the versatile quantum properties in single crystalline AgCrSe2. Our work not only offers a universal approach to characterize sub-angstrom local correlated structures across a wide range of quantum materials but also deepens our understanding of the fundamental mechanism behind exotic properties from the perspective of atomic-scale local correlated structures.

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）研究单层MnPS₃中极化子的形成，并计算由此产生的磁交换相互作用（magnetic exchange interactions）变化。

Using first-principles calculations, we investigate polaron formation in monolayer MnPS$_3$ and compute the resulting changes in magnetic exchange interactions. ### [26] [Chiral-Induced Spin Selectivity Effect in a 1 nm Thin 1,1'-Binaphthyl-2,2'-diyl Hydrogenphosphate Self-Assembled Monolayer on Nickel Oxide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17707)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 手性诱导自旋选择性（CISS）效应通常基于多纳米长的螺旋手性生物分子，但需要更稳定的金属氧化物表面耦合。本研究旨在探索低分子量、轴向手性的有机磷酸衍生物作为CISS应用的新型候选材料。

Method: 采用芳香族低分子量轴向手性有机磷酸衍生物1,1'-联萘-2,2'-二基氢磷酸酯（BNP），在NiOx/Ni基底上生长约1纳米厚的自组装单层膜，通过磁导原子力显微镜测量其CISS响应。

Result: 薄膜保持了手性特征，显示出强圆二色性信号。磁阻测量显示50-80%的高自旋极化率，偏压高于0.5V时磁阻曲线符合Fowler-Nordheim隧穿模型，特定自旋方向的电子面临的有效隧穿势垒比相反自旋方向高80%或低40%。

Abstract: The chiral-induced spin selectivity (CISS) effect describes an observed correlation between the orientation of an electron spin transported or transferred through a molecule and that molecule's chirality. Suitable molecules are usually arranged as self-assembled monolayers (SAMs), and the primary CISS systems are based on multiple nanometer-long biomolecules exhibiting helical chirality. Aside from these typically thiolate-anchored molecules, phosphonic and phosphoric acid SAMs may well become significant for those CISS applications that require a more robust molecular coupling to metal oxide surfaces. In this work, we report on our studies, employing the aromatic, low-molecular-mass, axially chiral organophosphoric acid derivative 1,1'-binaphthyl-2,2'-diyl hydrogenphosphate (BNP). Grown as a roughly 1 nm thin SAM on top of a NiOx/Ni substrate, a strong circular dichroism signal indicates that the thin films preserved chirality. The CISS response exhibits a high magnetoresistance with a spin polarization of 50-80% when measured using magnetic-conductive atomic force microscopy. For biases above 0.5 V, the magnetoresistance curves could be well fitted to the Fowler-Nordheim (FN) tunneling model. Using a minimal FN model, we determined that, depending on the magnetization direction and the handedness of the molecules, electrons of a certain spin direction face an effective tunneling barrier at high bias, which is either 80 % higher or 40 % lower compared to the barrier for electrons of the opposite spin direction. Due to the small size of the molecules, their compatibility with oxide materials, and their commercial availability, they are excellent candidates for the realization of novel (nanoscale) organic spintronic devices.

### [27] [Simulating the influence of stoichiometry on the spectral emissivity of Mo$_x$Si$_y$ thin films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17801)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Mo$_x$Si$_y$化合物不同晶相的光学性质，特别是其薄膜形式的发射率特性，以理解材料结构与光学性能之间的关系。

Method: 采用密度泛函微扰理论（density functional perturbation theory, DFPT）计算各晶相的介电函数（包括电子和离子贡献），并利用获得的体性质模拟约20nm薄膜的光学吸收谱。

Result: 大多数Mo$_x$Si$_y$薄膜呈金属性，但其发射率与Mo含量无简单相关性；在约900K温度下，预测金属薄膜在5-10nm厚度时达到最大发射率；六方MoSi$_2$发射率显著低于四方相，这与小带隙（六方相）和低费米能级态密度（四方相）有关；缺陷MoSi$_2$计算表明引入缺陷可大幅提高薄膜红外发射率。

Conclusion: 研究结果与实验定性吻合良好，证实了晶相结构对MoSi$_2$发射率的重要影响，并揭示了通过缺陷工程调控薄膜红外发射率的可能性。

Abstract: In this work, we simulate the spectral emissivity of various stoichiometric crystal phases of Mo$_x$Si$_y$ compounds using density functional perturbation theory. The dielectric function, including electronic and ionic contributions, is calculated for each phase. We use the bulk properties obtained to simulate the optical absorption spectrum originating from the compound in thin film ($\sim$20 nm) form. We find that most thin films of Mo$_x$Si$_y$ are metallic, however, our results indicate that their emissivity is not simply correlated with the Mo content. For hot metallic films at around 900 K, we predict a maximal emissivity between 5-10 nm thickness. Our results are in good qualitative agreement with experiments, confirming that the emissivity of hexagonal MoSi$_2$ is much lower than in the tetragonal phase. This is related to the small band gap (hexagonal MoSi$_2$) and low density of states at the Fermi level (tetragonal MoSi$_2$). Furthermore, test calculations on defected MoSi$_2$ demonstrate that the infrared emissivity of MoSi$_2$ thin films can be substantially increased by introducing defects.

### [28] [Substrate-controlled nucleation and growth kinetics in ultrathin Bi$_2$Te$_3$ films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17868)
*Damian Brzozowski,Sander R. Hønnås,Egil Y. Tokle,Jørgen A. Arnesen,Ingrid G. Hallsteinsen*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究通过脉冲激光沉积在不同基底上生长超薄Bi2Te3薄膜，发现基底粗糙度和成核密度是控制缺陷形成、影响拓扑表面态传输的关键因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属硫族化合物是重要的层状拓扑材料，但其电子性能常因缺陷导致的寄生体传导而受限。控制早期生长和缺陷形成对于抑制体传导、增强表面态传导至关重要。

Method: 采用脉冲激光沉积（pulsed laser deposition）在范德华（van der Waals）、晶格匹配和基底上生长超薄Bi2Te3薄膜，研究基底依赖的成核途径如何影响缺陷形成和电子传输。

Result: 所有基底上均形成相纯、c轴取向的Bi2Te3，但生长形貌差异显著。基底粗糙度而非晶格匹配主导层状生长：原子级平滑的云母和阶梯状SrTiO3产生连续阶地，而粗糙的BaF2和非晶Si3N4形成岛状结构。SrTiO3的高表面能增强吸附原子吸附和成核密度，导致快速垂直生长和早期Te耗尽。

Conclusion: 基底粗糙度和成核密度为控制Bi2Te3薄膜中缺陷形成、增强拓扑表面传输提供了关键调控手段。传输测量显示n型传导，最高载流子密度出现在SrTiO3基底上，与高密度成核期间的缺陷形成一致。

Abstract: Metal chalcogenides are promising layered topological materials, yet their electronic performance is often limited by parasitic bulk conduction arising from defects that introduce excess carriers and shift the Fermi level out of the topological regime. Controlling early-stage growth and defect formation is therefore essential for suppressing bulk transport and enhancing surface-state conduction. Here we investigate ultrathin Bi2Te3 films grown by pulsed laser deposition on substrates spanning van der Waals, lattice-matched, and amorphous regimes to determine how substrate-dependent nucleation pathways influence defect formation and electronic transport.
  Phase-pure, c-axis-oriented Bi2Te3 forms on all substrates, but the growth morphology varies strongly. Layered growth with well-defined quintuple-layer terraces is governed primarily by substrate roughness rather than lattice match: atomically smooth mica and step-terraced SrTiO3 yield continuous terraces, whereas rougher BaF2 and amorphous Si3N4 produce island-structured films. Between the two smooth substrates, the higher surface energy of SrTiO3 enhances adatom adsorption and nucleation density, promoting rapid vertical growth and early Te depletion.
  Transport measurements reveal n-type conduction with carrier densities of 10e19-10e20 cm-3. The highest carrier density occurs for films on SrTiO3, consistent with defect formation during high-density nucleation, whereas mobility correlates with structural coherence and terrace formation. Weak anti-localization signatures confirm phase-coherent transport in films on mica and SrTiO3. These results show that substrate roughness and nucleation density provide key levers for controlling defect formation and strengthening topological surface transport in Bi2Te3 thin films.

### [29] [Mechanistic Insights into Enhanced Alkaline Oxygen Evolution on Zn-Al Alloy Electrodes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17904)
*Abdul Ahad Mamun,Rokon Uddin Mahmud,Shahin Aziz,Muhammad Shahriar Bashar,Ahmed Sharif,Muhammad Anisuzzaman Talukder*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 碱性水电解（alkaline water electrolysis）作为生产清洁能源载体以减少碳排放的技术，缺乏低成本且高效的析氧反应（OER）电极。本研究旨在开发适合的Zn-Al合金电极以解决这一挑战。

Method: 采用粉末冶金法（powder metallurgy method）制备不同Al含量（最高20 wt.%）的Zn-Al合金电极，并进行碱性溶液中的电化学测量以评估其OER催化性能。同时进行第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）以研究其热力学相稳定性和电子结构。

Result: 实验和理论结果表明：Al含量≥20 wt.%时导致热力学相不稳定和富Al区二次相偏析，限制了反应动力学；5 wt.% Al合金虽具有良好热力学和电子特性，但表面反应活性位点不足导致电化学性能差；10 wt.%和15 wt.% Al合金表现出最佳性能，阳极交换电流密度分别比纯Zn提高约3倍和2倍，过电位显著降低（Zn₀.₉Al₀.₁为0.240 V，Zn₀.₈₅Al₀.₁₅为0.5603 V，纯Zn为1.086 V）。

Conclusion: Zn-Al合金电极中Al含量对OER催化性能有显著影响，10 wt.% Al含量的Zn₀.₉Al₀.₁合金表现出最优异的反应动力学和最低过电位，其性能优于其他过渡金属基催化剂如Fe-Co-Ni-Mo合金和Fe掺杂CuO。

Abstract: Electrochemical water electrolysis, which produces clean energy carriers to mitigate carbon emissions, lacks suitable, low-cost electrodes for efficient oxygen evolution reaction (OER) in alkaline water splitting. To address this challenge, we developed Zn-Al alloy electrodes with varying Al contents up to 20 wt.% via powder metallurgy method and conducted electrochemical measurements of the OER in alkaline solution to investigate their catalytic performance. We also performed first-principles calculations to examine their thermodynamic phase stability and electronic structures. Both theoretical and experimental results indicated that incorporating $\geq 20$ wt.% Al into Zn led to thermodynamic phase instability and secondary-phase segregation in Al-rich regions, limiting reaction kinetics and reducing catalytic efficiency. Although the Al content of 5 wt.% into Zn exhibited favorable thermodynamic and electronic characteristics, but its electrochemical performance was inefficient and poor due to inadequate reaction active sites on the surface. In contrast, the 10 wt.% and 15 wt.% Al into Zn showed approximately three- and two-fold increases in anodic exchange current density relative to pure Zn, respectively. Additionally, the anodic overpotential losses ($η_{0,a}$) measured at a current density of 12 mAcm$^{-2}$ were 0.240 V for Zn$_{0.9}$Al$_{0.1}$ and 0.5603 V for Zn$_{0.85}$Al$_{0.15}$, significantly lower than that of pure Zn ($η_{0,a} = 1.086$ V). While Zn$_{0.9}$Al$_{0.1}$ and Zn$_{0.85}$Al$_{0.15}$ showed similar charge transfer resistance ($R_{\rm CT}$), Zn$_{0.9}$Al$_{0.1}$ demonstrated superior reaction kinetics and lower $η_{0,a}$ across all samples tested. Furthermore, the improved kinetics and reduced overpotential of the Zn-Al alloys favorably compare with those of other transition-metal-based catalysts, including Fe-Co-Ni-Mo alloys and Fe-doped CuO.

### [30] [Real-space microscopic description of laser-pulse induced melting of superconductivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17073)
*Karl Bergson Hallberg,Jacob Linder,Guillermo Nava Antonio,Chiara Ciccarelli*

TL;DR: 该研究通过微观实空间模型模拟超导体在强激光脉冲后的时间动力学，重现了实验观测到的临界慢化现象，并预测了类似反向波的异常电流流动模式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 激光淬灭量子序已成为研究非平衡强扰动系统中奇异物理效应的有效工具，但现有理论建模通常采用唯象方法或平移不变性假设，缺乏对微观实空间动力学的精确描述。

Method: 采用微观实空间模型（microscopic real-space model）求解超导体在强激光脉冲后的时间动力学，利用模型的实空间分辨率分析系统相涨落和电流的时空行为。

Result: 成功重现了近期实验中观察到的临界慢化现象（critical slowing-down），即接近凝聚能（condensation energy）的激光通量下序参量熔化的临界慢化；预测了脉冲后超导体中类似反向波（backward waves）的异常电流流动模式。

Abstract: Quenching quantum order via laser pulses has proven a useful tool to access exotic physical effects in systems that are strongly perturbed out of equilibrium. However, theoretical modelling of experimental measurements is typically done phenomenologically or by assuming translational invariance due to the complexity of the problem. Here, we solve a microscopic real-space model of the time dynamics of a superconductor following an intense laser-pulse. We are able to reproduce recent experimental findings displaying a critical slowing-down of the melting of the order parameter for laser fluences close to the condensation energy. Moreover, we leverage the real-space resolution of our model to predict how phase fluctuations and currents in the system behave both spatially and temporally. We discover an unusual current flow in the superconductor after the pulse has subsided, resembling backward waves that normally require special engineering in metamaterials or wave guides. Our results predict a rich behavior of the superconducting order parameter at a microscopic level which is manifested in current textures that can be probed using radiation detection.

### [31] [Interplay of superconductivity and ferromagnetism in ferromagnetic semiconductor-based Josephson junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17101)

### [32] [$\textit{Ab initio}$ Identification of Hydrogen Tunneling as Two-Level Systems in Nb$_2$O$_5$ and Ta$_2$O$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17194)

Hydrogen is the only light interstitial with barrier-distance combinations near the $\sim0.1-10$ GHz tunneling regime, and its ensemble statistics in amorphous oxides produce effective TLS densities and loss estimates consistent with the experimentally observed higher loss in Nb oxide than in Ta oxide. Our results point to H tunneling as a plausible microscopic TLS source in these materials.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用双平行超导纳米线（Dayem环）结构，利用Little-Parks效应和量子干涉现象。分析包括通用立方电流-相位关系以及更现实的微观CPR（具有高阶非线性），并提出适用于极低温度（超导量子比特工作温度）的幂律唯象近似。

The inclusion of two nanowires instead of one leads to the Little-Parks effect, which provides an oscillator behavior for the qubit frequency as well as anharmonicity. Our key result is that even if the nanowires have an increasingly linear CPR at low supercurrents, the quantum interference between two condensates, induced by a magnetic field, leads to a restoration of cubic nonlinearity, which is predicted to be sufficient to create a functional transmon qubit based on thin superconducting wires. We consider both generic (cubic) current-phase relationships (CPR) as well as more realistic microscopic CPR, having higher-order nonlinearities.   <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究提供了普通带内输运揭示扭曲费米面的直接证据，并计算了霍尔电阻率的磁场角度依赖性以供进一步实验验证。这证实了费米面几何结构对UTe₂正常态输运性质的关键影响。

Abstract: We theoretically study angle-resolved magnetoresistance under rotated magnetic field in the normal state of a spin-triplet superconductor UTe$_2$. The Wannier model derived from a GGA+$U$ calculation shows quasi-two-dimensional Fermi surfaces with warping in the $k_z$ direction, consistent with quantum oscillation measurements in the high magnetic field regime. Solving the semiclassical Boltzmann equation, we show that the Fermi surface geometry gives rise to oscillations in the magnetoresistance when the field is tilted from the $c$ axis toward the $a$ or $b$ axis. By assuming a band-dependent relaxation time, the calculated angle-resolved magnetoresistance is in good agreement with the recent transport experiment. This is direct evidence for the warped Fermi surface revealed by ordinary intraband transport. It suggests that the hole band with long relaxation time dominates electron transport. The field angle dependence of the Hall resistivity is calculated for further experimental verification.

### [35] [Extended Hubbard model on fractals: d-Wave superconductivity and competing pairing channels](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17362)
*Robert Canyellas,Mikhail I. Katsnelson,Andrey Bagrov*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究预测谢尔宾斯基垫片（Sierpiński gasket）等分形结构能增强s波超导的临界温度，同时保持库珀对（Cooper pairs）的宏观相位相干性。本研究旨在将分析扩展到具有非平凡对称性的序参数，探究分形几何对不同配对对称性的选择性影响。

Method: 采用扩展哈伯德模型（extended Hubbard model）研究具有最近邻吸引作用的分形晶格。使用博戈留波夫-德热纳平均场理论（Bogoliubov-de Gennes mean-field theory）分析不同配对通道的竞争关系。

Result: 谢尔宾斯基地毯（Sierpiński carpet）显著改变了配对通道的竞争格局：在方形晶格半填充时占主导的d波超导圆顶（d-wave superconducting dome）在地毯结构中变得不稳定，而在高填充和低填充区域扩展s波配对（extended s-wave pairing）得到强烈增强。在三角谢尔宾斯基垫片上，混合s+d+id态（hybrid s+d+id states）显示出与先前观察到的纯s波配对相当的临界温度增强效应。

Conclusion: 分形几何作为配对对称性的选择性滤波器，序参数结构与晶格拓扑之间的兼容性决定了哪些通道被稳定或抑制。分形边界结构通过几何阻挫（geometric frustration）影响符号变化的序参数，从而调控不同超导配对对称性的稳定性。

Abstract: Fractal structures such as the Sierpiński gasket have been predicted to enhance the critical tem- perature of s-wave superconductivity compared to regular crystals while maintaining macroscopic phase coherence of Cooper pairs. Here we extend this analysis to order parameters with non-trivial symmetry by studying the extended Hubbard model with nearest-neighbor attraction on fractal lattices. Using Bogoliubov-de Gennes mean-field theory, we find that the Sierpiński carpet dramat- ically alters the competition between pairing channels: the predominant d-wave superconducting dome at half filling of the square lattice becomes unstable for the carpet, while at high and low fillings extended s-wave pairing gets strongly enhanced. We attribute this to geometric frustration of sign-changing order parameters by the fractal boundary structure. On the triangular Sierpiński gasket, hybrid s+d+id states show critical temperature enhancement comparable to that previously observed for pure s-wave pairing. Our results demonstrate that fractal geometry acts as a selective filter for pairing symmetries, with the compatibility between order parameter structure and lattice topology determining which channels are stabilized or suppressed.

Abstract: In 2023, superconductivity in La$_3$Ni$_2$O$_7$ was discovered under high pressures above approximately 14 GPa. In addition to its high transition temperature ($T_{\mathrm{c}} \simeq 80$ K), the structural resemblance to high-$T_{\mathrm{c}}$ cuprates has strongly stimulated research, soon followed by the discovery of superconductivity in La$_4$Ni$_3$O$_{10}$. These compounds belong to the Ruddlesden--Popper phases, comprising double- and triple-layered NiO$_2$ square lattices separated by LaO rock-salt slabs.
  Research on these systems has rapidly developed along three major directions, as in other prominent families of superconductors such as the cuprates and iron arsenides: expanding the chemical variety of compounds, enhancing $T_{\mathrm{c}}$ through elemental substitution, and elucidating the superconducting mechanism. These challenges, being closely interconnected, continue to drive the field. The clarification of the pairing mechanism encounters a particular difficulty, since the key experiments must be performed under high pressures. This situation highlights the significance of developing nickel oxides that exhibit superconductivity at much lower pressures, ideally at ambient pressure, which would in turn broaden the scope of chemical tuning and detailed physical characterization.
  In this context, it is timely and meaningful to summarize the present state of knowledge. Here, we emphasize sample synthesis and characterization, which are already well established and often decisive for progress in unconventional superconductors, while providing a brief overview of the currently available electronic properties.

### [38] [Electron-Hole Scattering Dichotomy and Anisotropic Warping in Quasi-Two-Dimensional Fermi Surfaces of UTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17710)
*Motoi Kimata,Jun Ishizuka,Freya Husstedt,Yusei Shimizu,Ai Nakamura,Dexin Li,Yoshiya Homma,Atsushi Miyake,Yoshinori Haga,Hironori Sakai,Yoshifumi Tokiwa,Shinsaku Kambe,Yo Tokunaga,Dai Aoki,Toni Helm,Youichi Yanase*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验与理论结合，揭示了UTe2重费米子超导体的费米面几何结构及其与磁涨落、准粒子寿命的关联，为理解其自旋三重态配对机制提供了关键依据。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 研究发现准二维费米面呈现矩形截面形状，具有强烈各向异性扭曲，源于两个正交准一维能带的杂化。实验揭示了显著的电子-空穴散射二分性：电子费米面上的准粒子寿命明显短于空穴费米面。这种二分性可由各向异性、低维反铁磁涨落解释，其选择性地增强电子费米面上的散射。

Conclusion: 研究阐明了费米面几何、磁涨落和动量依赖准粒子寿命之间的直接关系，为微观理解配对机制提供了关键基础。结果表明电子口袋对超导的出现起主导作用，并对UTe2中自旋三重态超导性的能隙对称性施加了严格约束。

Abstract: We present a combined experimental and theoretical study of the detailed Fermi-surface (FS) geometry of UTe2, a heavy-fermion superconductor that has recently attracted considerable attention as a promising candidate for spin-triplet pairing. Using angle-dependent magnetoresistance oscillations, a bulk- and low-energy-sensitive transport probe for quasi-two-dimensional (Q2D) electronic structures, we directly determine the in-plane FS geometry. We found that the Q2D FS exhibits a rectangular cross-sectional shape with strongly anisotropic warping, originating from the hybridization of two orthogonal quasi-one-dimensional bands. Through a quantitative comparison between experiment and theoretical calculations, we further reveal a large electron-hole scattering dichotomy: the quasiparticle lifetime on the electron FS is substantially shorter than that on the hole FS. This dichotomy is naturally explained by anisotropic, low-dimensional antiferromagnetic fluctuations, which selectively enhance scattering on the electron FS. This suggests a dominant role of the electron pockets for the emergence of superconductivity. Our results clarify a direct relation between FS geometry, magnetic fluctuations, and momentum-dependent quasiparticle lifetimes, and thus providing a crucial basis for the microscopic understanding of pairing mechanism, and impose stringent constraints on the gap symmetry of spin-triplet superconductivity in UTe2.

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Remeika系列超导体(Ca_xSr_{1-x})_3Rh_4Sn_{13}中与连续电荷密度波（CDW）和结构转变相关的非磁性量子临界点（QCP），探索无序（disorder）作为非热调控参数驱动系统达到量子临界区域的可能性。

Method: 采用2.5 MeV电子辐照引入非磁性点状无序，通过调控无序剂量来抑制电荷密度波（CDW）有序；分析温度依赖电阻率ρ(T)的演化，观察从费米液体（Fermi liquid）到非费米液体（non-Fermi liquid）行为的转变。

Result: 随着无序增加，电阻率ρ(T)中的线性项逐渐增大而二次项减小，在CDW长程有序被完全抑制时观察到近乎完美的T-线性依赖关系；将量子临界点（QCP）位置精确定位在x=0.75至0.85之间，证实无序可以将系统调控至量子临界区域甚至超越该点。

Conclusion: 无序（disorder）可作为新颖的非热调控参数驱动系统达到量子临界区域，支持了Imry和Ma关于淬火无序（quenched disorder）破坏有序相稳定性的论点，该方法可能适用于多种不同系统。

Abstract: The Remeika series superconductor, $(\text{Ca}_x\text{Sr}_{1-x})_3\text{Rh}_4\text{Sn}_{13}$, shows a rare nonmagnetic quantum critical point (QCP) associated with the continuous charge-density wave (CDW) and structural transition under the ``dome'' of superconductivity achieved by tuning composition and applying pressure. Here we use a nonmagnetic point-like disorder induced by 2.5 MeV electron irradiation to suppress the CDW and drive the system to and even beyond the QCP. This conclusion is based on a clear evolution of temperature-dependent resistivity, $ρ\left(T\right)$, from the Fermi liquid to the non-Fermi liquid regime with increasing amount of disorder. Starting on the CDW side, below the suggested QCP concentration of $x_c=0.9$, added disorder resulted in a progressively larger linear term and a reduced quadratic term in $ρ\left(T\right)$. Nearly perfect $T-$linear dependence is observed at the dose at which long-range CDW order is suppressed to $T=$0, consistent with the expectations. We refine the QCP location in this system and place it in the interval between $x=$0.75 and 0.85. Our results strongly support the concept that the disorder can tune the system to the quantum critical regime and even beyond. It follows from the argument by Imry and Ma that any ordered phase is unstable toward quenched disorder. Introduced in a controlled way, this disorder becomes a novel non-thermal tuning parameter likely applicable to a variety of different systems.

</details>


### [40] [Pressure-induced Superconductivity in AgSbTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17846)
*Sudaice Kazibwe,Bishnu Karki,Wencheng Lu,Zhongxin Liang,Minghong Sui,Melissa Gooch,Zhifeng Ren,Pavan Hosur,Timothy A. Strobel,Ching-Wu Chu,Liangzi Deng*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: AgSbTe₂在高压下展现出超导性，起始临界温度（Tc）为3.2K（0.38GPa），随压力增加至6.9K（31.9GPa），并在卸压过程中达到峰值7.4K。该材料在21.7GPa以上失去长程结构有序性，但卸压后完全恢复。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AgSbTe₂作为已知热电材料具有高塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和本征低热导率，但其在高压下的行为尚未充分探索。本研究旨在系统探究非化学计量比AgSbTe₂在高压下的结构、电子和输运性质。

Method: 采用高压实验系统研究非化学计量比AgSbTe₂的结构、电子和输运性质。结合磁场依赖输运测量和电子结构计算，分析超导态的演化机制。

Result: 在0.38GPa极低压力下即出现超导性，起始临界温度（Tc）为3.2K。Tc随压力增加而升高，在31.9GPa达到6.9K，卸压过程中峰值达7.4K。材料在21.7GPa以上失去长程结构有序性，但卸压后晶体结构完全恢复。

Conclusion: 研究揭示了AgSbTe₂中的压力诱导超导性，证明压力可有效调控热电材料的电子基态，将其功能扩展到热电能量转换之外。超导态的演化由压缩下费米能级（Fermi level）处增强的电子态密度驱动。

Abstract: AgSbTe2 is a well-known thermoelectric material with a high Seebeck coefficient and intrinsically low thermal conductivity, but its behavior under pressure remains largely unexplored. Here we report a systematic investigation of the structural, electronic, and transport properties of non-stoichiometric AgSbTe2 under high pressure. At ambient pressure, the material can be described as having a cubic crystal structure that remains stable up to 21.7 GPa beyond which it loses long-range structural order, while its crystal system fully recovers upon decompression. Remarkably, superconductivity emerges at a very low pressure of 0.38 GPa with an onset superconducting critical temperature (Tc) of 3.2 K. Tc increases with increasing pressure, reaching 6.9 K at 31.9 GPa, and peaks at 7.4 K during decompression. Magnetic-field-dependent transport measurements and electronic structure calculations reveal an evolution of the superconducting state driven by an enhanced electronic density of states at the Fermi level under compression. Our findings uncover pressure-induced superconductivity in AgSbTe2 and demonstrate that pressure can effectively tune the electronic ground state of thermoelectric materials, extending their functionality beyond thermoelectric energy conversion.

### [41] [Thermodynamic Discovery of Tetracriticality and Emergent Multicomponent Superconductivity in UTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17905)
*Sahas Kamat,Jared Dans,Shanta Saha,Artem D. Kokovin,Johnpierre Paglione,Jörg Schmalian,B. J. Ramshaw*

TL;DR: 通过脉冲回波超声测量发现UTe₂中新的相边界和重入相变，揭示了两个超导序参量之间的强竞争导致多分量超导态的形成，建立了完整的热力学相图。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: UTe₂作为候选拓扑超导体（candidate topological superconductor）具有复杂的相图，其中两个二阶相边界在压力-温度相图中"三相点"处的明显相交在热力学上是被禁止的，这表明存在隐藏的相变或对UTe₂超导性的根本误解。

Method: 使用脉冲回波超声（pulse-echo ultrasound）技术，通过发现一个具有独特"向上跳跃"声速特征的新相边界，获得了重入相变（re-entrant phase transition）的直接热力学证据。

Result: 研究结果确立了(P*,T*)为四临界点（tetracritical point），超过该点后常压诱导和压力诱导的超导序参量形成多分量态（multi-component state）。测量得到的相图被用于构建金兹堡-朗道理论（Ginzburg-Landau theory），显示两个超导序参量之间的强竞争驱动了重入现象并导致相锁定，从而抑制了超导涨落。

Conclusion: 这些发现提供了确定的磁场-温度-压力相图，并为UTe₂中的多分量（以及潜在的拓扑）超导性建立了热力学基础。

Abstract: The candidate topological superconductor UTe$_2$ exhibits a complex phase diagram with multiple superconducting states, yet the nature of their coexistence has remained a central mystery. In particular, the apparent intersection of two second-order phase boundaries at a ``triple point'' in the pressure-temperature phase diagram is thermodynamically forbidden, suggesting hidden phase transitions or a fundamental misunderstanding of the superconductivity in UTe$_2$. Here, we use pulse-echo ultrasound to resolve this puzzle by discovering a new phase boundary that is characterized by a unique ``upward jump" in the sound velocity -- direct thermodynamic evidence for a re-entrant phase transition. Our results establish $\left(P^{\star},T^{\star}\right)$ as a tetracrtical point, beyond which the ambient and pressure-induced superconducting order parameters form a multi-component state. We use the measured phase diagram to construct a Ginzburg-Landau theory that shows that strong competition between the two superconducting order parameters drives the re-entrance and leads to phase locking that suppress superconducting fluctuations. These findings provide the definitive magnetic field-temperature-pressure phase diagram and establish a thermodynamic foundation for multi-component -- and potentially topological -- superconductivity in UTe$_2$.

### [42] [Quantum-Material Josephson Junctions: Unconventional Barriers, Emerging Functionality](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17921)
*Kathryn A. Pitton,Michiel P. Dubbelman,Trent M. Kyrk,Houssam El Mrabet Haje,Yaozu Tang,Roald J. H. van der Kolk,Yarslov M. Blanter,Mazhar N Ali*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文综述了量子材料约瑟夫森结（quantum-material Josephson junctions, QMJJ）的研究进展，重点关注磁性、强关联和铁电/多铁性三类势垒材料，这些材料将约瑟夫森效应转变为探测对称性和多体物理的灵敏探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统约瑟夫森结（Josephson junctions）中的势垒主要作为被动弱连接，而量子材料势垒具有内部自由度（如磁性、强关联或可切换极化），能将约瑟夫森效应转变为探测对称性和多体物理（many-body physics）的灵敏探针。

Method: 采用综述研究方法，系统回顾量子材料约瑟夫森结（QMJJ）的进展，重点分析三类势垒材料：磁性势垒（magnetic barriers）、关联势垒（correlated barriers）以及铁电/多铁性势垒（ferroelectric and multiferroic barriers）。

Result: 在磁性势垒中，交换作用、非共线性和自旋活性散射实现了0-π-φ基态、单重态-三重态转换和非互易输运；在关联势垒中，邻近效应呈现多体特征，范德华Kagome莫特绝缘层表现出无场约瑟夫森二极管行为；在铁电/多铁性势垒中，非易失极化提供了内部控制手段，可实现超导存储和忆阻动力学。

Conclusion: 量子材料约瑟夫森结通过势垒的内部自由度（磁性、关联性、极化）将传统被动弱连接转变为主动功能单元，为探索对称性、多体物理以及开发新型超导器件（如超导存储、约瑟夫森二极管）提供了重要平台。

Abstract: Josephson junctions translate quantum phase coherence into an electrical response and underpin superconducting sensors and quantum circuits. In conventional junctions, the barrier acts primarily as a passive weak link, however, when the barrier is a quantum material with its own internal degrees of freedom like magnetism, strong correlations, or switchable polarization, the Josephson effect becomes a sensitive probe of symmetry and many-body physics in the interlayer. Here we review progress in quantum-material Josephson junctions, (QMJJ) focusing on three rapidly advancing barrier families: 1. magnetic barriers, where exchange, noncollinearity, and spin-active scattering enable 0-π-φ ground states, singlet-triplet conversion, and nonreciprocal transport, 2. correlated barriers, where proximity effects acquire many-body character and recent van der Waals Kagome Mott interlayers exhibit field-free Josephson diode behavior, and 3. ferroelectric and multiferroic barriers, where nonvolatile polarization provides an internal control knob and can produce superconducting memory and memristive dynamics.

### [43] [How Spontaneous Electrowetting and Surface Charge affect Drop Motion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2602.03362)
*Chirag Hinduja,Benjamin Leibauer,Rishi Chaurasia,Nikolaus Knorr,Aaron D. Ratschow,Shalini Singh,Hans-Jürgen Butt,Rüdiger Berger*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 水滴在疏水表面滑动时，其后缘会发生自发电荷分离。研究发现这种电荷分离通过两种机制影响接触角：自发电润湿效应降低接触角，同时沉积电荷的表面电荷效应也降低接触角。两种效应在后退接触线处相互补偿，导致滑动水滴的后退接触角变化不显著。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 水滴在疏水表面滑动时，其后缘会发生自发电荷分离，但尚不清楚这种电荷分离如何影响滑动水滴的接触角。研究旨在探究电荷分离对接触角的影响机制。

Method: 在低毛细数（≤10⁻⁴）条件下，分别研究接地和绝缘水滴在疏水表面的滑动行为。通过对比两种状态下的接触角变化，分析电荷分离对润湿行为的影响。

Result: 水滴电荷导致自发电润湿（spontaneous electrowetting），从而降低接触角。同时，沉积电荷产生表面电荷效应，同样降低接触角。两种现象在后退接触线处相互补偿，导致滑动水滴的后退接触角变化不显著。

Conclusion: 水滴滑动过程中的电荷分离通过两种相互补偿的机制影响接触角：自发电润湿效应和表面电荷效应。这种补偿作用解释了为何滑动水滴的后退接触角变化不明显。

Abstract: Water drops sliding on hydrophobic surfaces spontaneously separate charges at their rear. It is unclear how this charge separation affects the contact angles of a sliding drop. We slide grounded and insulated drops on hydrophobic surfaces at low capillary numbers (\leq 10^{-4}). We find that drop charge leads to spontaneous electrowetting, which decreases the contact angles. Additionally, the deposited charges lead to a surface charge effect and decrease the contact angle. Both phenomena compensate each other at the receding contact line, resulting in an insignificant change in the receding contact angle of a sliding drop.

### [45] [Higher-point Energy Correlators: Factorization in the Back-to-Back Limit & Non-perturbative Effects](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16996)
*Ankita Budhraja,Isabelle Pels,Wouter J. Waalewijn*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该论文通过引入新的参数化方法，系统研究了N点能量关联子（N-point energy correlators）在背对背极限下的因子化定理和共线极限下的领头非微扰效应，为强耦合常数α_s提取和喷注物理研究提供了新工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: N点能量关联子（N-point energy correlators）是研究强相互作用的重要可观测量，可用于提取强耦合常数α_s、探测重离子碰撞中的喷注修正以及确定顶夸克质量。然而，大N情况下的复杂相空间限制了其实际应用。

Method: 采用新引入的参数化方法简化相空间结构，研究投影N点关联子在两个极限区域：背对背极限下的因子化和共线极限下的领头非微扰效应。计算了次次领头对数重求和所需的新成分——单圈喷注函数（one-loop jet function）。

Result: 推导出任意N的因子化定理，确定了领头非微扰幂次修正的解析结构及其对质心能量Q、N值和角标度x的依赖关系。首次得到非整数N<1的结果，发现经典x标度获得N依赖修正，并出现新的非微扰矩阵元$\tildeΩ^{[N]}$。在特定近似下，$\tildeΩ^{[N]}$可与标准参数$Ω_1$关联。

Conclusion: 解析预测与Pythia中的强子化模型符合良好，证明了新参数化方法在能量关联子研究中的显著进展，为未来具有互补系统误差的α_s提取奠定了基础。

Abstract: N-point energy correlators are powerful observables for studying strong interactions, with applications ranging from extractions of the strong coupling $α_s$ to probes of jet modification in heavy-ion collisions and determination of the top-quark mass. Their practical use has, however, been limited by the complicated phase space for large N. Using a recently introduced parametrization that simplifies this structure, we study projected N-point correlators in two regimes: factorization in the back-to-back limit and leading non-perturbative effects in the collinear limit. While results in the back-to-back regime were previously limited to the energy-energy correlator, our approach allows us to derive the factorization theorem for arbitrary N. We compute the new ingredient, a one-loop jet function, needed for the next-to-next-to-leading-logarithmic resummation, which enables future $α_s$ extractions with complementary systematics. We further determine the analytic structure of leading non-perturbative power corrections for arbitrary N, including their dependence on the center-of-mass energy Q, the value of N, and the angular scale $x$. We present the first results for non-integer N<1, finding that the classical scaling in $x$ acquires an N-dependent modification, and that a new non-perturbative matrix element $\tildeΩ^{[N]}$ appears. In a certain approximation, $\tildeΩ^{[N]}$ can be related to the standard parameter $Ω_1$ relevant for N>1. Our analytic predictions are tested against the hadronization model in Pythia, finding good agreement. The results presented in this paper demonstrate the significant advancements enabled through our new parametrization of energy correlators.

Abstract: Motivated by the DAMA/LIBRA annual modulation signal, the dark matter community has invested heavily in ultra-clean underground NaI detectors to search for light WIMPs. We point out a new target of opportunity for these detectors -- axions produced by the carbon-burning stars within our galaxy. These stars synthesize large quantities of $^{23}$Na, keeping it at temperatures $\sim 10^9$K for periods up to tens of thousands of years. Under these conditions, $^{23}$Na radiates 440 keV axions through repeated photo-excitation and axio-deexcitation of its first excited state. Upon reaching a NaI detector, the process is reversed: the axion is resonantly absorbed, producing a 440 keV deexcitation photon. NaI thus serves as both $γ$ source and $γ$ detector. We find that existing NaI detectors can probe axion-nucleon couplings $|g_{aNN}^\mathrm{eff~^{23}Na}| \approx g_{app} \sim 10^{-6}$--$10^{-2}$, including QCD axions with $m_a \gtrsim 10$ eV. While there are several astrophysical constraints on axions with these couplings, our re-examination of these bounds shows that substantial gaps remain, providing strong motivation for the proposed searches.

### [47] [A Continuum Schwinger Method to Study the Pion's Generalized Parton Distribution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17496)
*J. M. Morgado-Chávez,J. Segovia,F. de Soto,J. Rodríguez-Quintero,V. Bertone,M. Defurne,C. Mezrag,H. Moutarde*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种满足所有QCD约束的π介子广义部分子分布（GPDs）建模新策略，通过简单代数模型计算了深度虚康普顿散射（DVCS）康普顿形状因子，发现在电子离子对撞机运动学下胶子主导π介子响应。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义部分子分布（Generalised Parton Distributions, GPDs）为强子结构提供了多维视角，对π介子尤为重要，因其动力学与手征对称性破缺（chiral symmetry breaking）密切相关。现有模型需要满足所有QCD约束条件。

Method: 提出了一种新颖的π介子GPDs建模策略，该策略在构造上满足所有QCD约束：支撑性（support）、多项式性（polynomiality）、正定性（positivity）和软π定理（soft-pion theorem）。通过一个简单的代数模型进行说明，并进行了演化计算。

Result: 使用该模型计算了次领头阶（next-to-leading order）的深度虚康普顿散射（deeply virtual Compton scattering, DVCS）康普顿形状因子（Compton Form Factors）。结果表明，在电子离子对撞机（Electron Ion Collider）运动学下，胶子（gluons）主导π介子响应。

Conclusion: 提出的建模策略成功构建了满足所有QCD约束的π介子GPDs模型，计算结果显示在电子离子对撞机运动学条件下，胶子对π介子响应起主导作用，这为理解π介子内部结构提供了重要见解。

Abstract: Generalised Parton Distributions (GPDs) provide multidimensional insight into hadron structure and are particularly relevant for the pion, whose dynamics are intimately linked to chiral symmetry breaking. We introduce a novel modelling strategy for pion GPDs that satisfies all QCD constraints by construction: support, polynomiality, positivity, and the soft-pion theorem. The approach is illustrated with a simple algebraic model, which is evolved and used to compute deeply virtual Compton scattering (DVCS) Compton Form Factors at next-to-leading order. Our results indicate that gluons dominate the pion response at the Electron Ion Collider kinematics.

</details>


### [48] [Pseudoscalar and vector toponia in a Dyson--Schwinger--Bethe--Salpeter framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17503)
*H. -R. Zhang,Z. -F. Cui,J. Segovia*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究采用Dyson-Schwinger和Bethe-Salpeter方程的彩虹-梯阶（rainbow-ladder）截断，结合Qin-Chang有效相互作用，计算了顶夸克-反顶夸克（toponium）系统的伪标量（pseudoscalar）和矢量（vector）态性质。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于将Poincaré协变的非微扰量子色动力学（QCD）框架扩展到极端重夸克极限下的顶夸克系统，探索QCD在此极限下产生的强关联束缚态性质。

Method: 方法基于Dyson-Schwinger方程和Bethe-Salpeter方程的彩虹-梯阶（rainbow-ladder）截断，采用Qin-Chang有效相互作用。研究首先在粲偶素（charmonium）和底偶素（bottomonium）领域验证框架，然后一致性地扩展到顶夸克系统，并考虑了流夸克质量的重整化群（renormalisation-group）跑动和活跃味夸克数的处理。

Result: 计算得到顶偶素（toponium）质量在344-346 GeV附近，超精细劈裂（hyperfine splittings）低于0.14-0.17 GeV。衰变常数较大（6-7 GeV），并表现出预期的重夸克标度行为。结果对重整化标度（renormalisation scale）仅显示温和敏感性，且当增加活跃味夸克数（N_f）时系统性地降低了束缚程度。

Conclusion: 尽管物理顶夸克在强子化前通过弱相互作用衰变，但研究结果表明在Poincaré协变的非微扰框架内，量子色动力学（QCD）在极端重夸克极限下能够产生紧密关联的伪标量和矢量顶偶素系统。

Abstract: We study the pseudoscalar ($J^{PC}=0^{-+}$) and vector ($1^{--}$) top--antitop (toponium) systems within the rainbow--ladder truncation of the Dyson--Schwinger and Bethe--Salpeter equations, employing the Qin--Chang effective interaction. After validating the framework in the charmonium and bottomonium sectors, we extend it consistently to the top sector, incorporating renormalisation-group running of the current quark mass and a careful treatment of the number of active flavours. We compute masses and leptonic decay constants for $N_f=5$ and $6$, then analyse their dependence on the renormalisation scale in the range $μ=400-800\,\text{GeV}$. The resulting toponium masses lie near $344-346\,\text{GeV}$ with hyperfine splittings below $0.14-0.17\,\text{GeV}$, while the decay constants are large, $6-7\,\text{GeV}$, and exhibit the expected heavy-quark scaling behaviour. We find only mild sensitivity to the renormalisation point and a systematic reduction of binding when increasing $N_f$. Although the physical top quark decays weakly before hadronisation, our results demonstrate that, within a Poincaré-covariant nonperturbative framework, quantum chromodynamics (QCD) generates tightly correlated pseudoscalar and vector toponium systems in that extreme heavy-quark limit.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用色偶极子S矩阵形式（color dipole S-matrix formalism），基于不同QCD动力学假设构建多种未积分胶子分布（unintegrated gluon distribution）模型。方法包括估计b→D⁰跃迁贡献，并考虑重夸克碎裂处理对预测的影响。

Abstract: The inclusive photoproduction of heavy mesons in ultraperipheral $pPb$ and $PbPb$ collisions at the LHC energies is investigated considering the color dipole $S$-matrix formalism and assuming distinct models for the unintegrated gluon distribution, based on different assumptions for the description of the QCD dynamics. In particular, predictions for the $B^0$-meson photoproduction are presented here for the first time. The study of the $D^0$-meson photoproduction is revisited by estimating the impact of the treatment of the heavy charm fragmentation on the predictions and extended for $pPb$ collisions. Moreover, the contribution associated with the $b \rightarrow D^0$ transition is estimated. Our results indicate that a future experimental analysis of the heavy meson photoproduction will provide important constrains on the description of the hadronic structure at high energies.

### [50] [Multi-Component Dark Matter as a Solution to the Galactic Center GeV Excess](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17095)
*Farinaldo S. Queiroz,Clarissa Siqueira,Carlos E. Yaguna*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 该研究通过系统分析多组分暗物质模型，发现银河系中心过剩辐射（GCE）数据在统计上更支持包含两个不同粒子物种（N=2）的暗物质框架，其中每个组分通过单一末态湮灭，且具有轻重质量层级结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 银河系中心过剩辐射（Galactic Center Excess, GCE）是暗物质湮灭的有力证据，但其能谱形态难以用单一粒子物种的传统范式解释。这促使研究者探索多组分暗物质模型以更好地拟合观测数据。

Method: 研究系统性地调查了多组分暗物质模型，考虑了两个（N=2）和三个（N=3）不同粒子物种，并分析了排他性和混合湮灭通道。采用赤池信息准则（Akaike Information Criterion, AIC）来严格惩罚模型复杂度，以进行统计比较。

Result: 研究发现GCE数据在统计上更支持N=2情景，其中每个暗物质组分通过单一末态湮灭。优选解呈现轻重质量层级结构，且原本单独无法解释过剩的末态（如$t\bar{t}$、$ZZ$和$hh$）在多组分框架下因形态拟合改善而"复活"。这些情景可能缓解与现有约束的张力，在不确定性范围内达到兼容性。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明GCE可能是多样化暗物质区的首个证据，支持多尺度解决方案而非最小弱相互作用大质量粒子（WIMP）范式。这为理解暗物质性质提供了新的理论框架方向。

Abstract: The Galactic Center Excess (GCE) is a compelling signature of dark matter annihilation, but its spectral morphology is difficult to reconcile with the traditional paradigm of a single particle species. In this work, we perform a systematic investigation of multi-component dark matter sectors, exploring scenarios with two ($N=2$) and three ($N=3$) distinct particle species while considering both exclusive and mixed annihilation channels. Using the Akaike Information Criterion (AIC) to rigorously penalize model complexity, we find that the GCE data statistically favors an $N=2$ scenario where each dark matter component annihilates exclusively into a single final state. Our results reveal that the preferred solutions naturally follow a light-plus-heavy mass hierarchy, and that specific final states such as $t\bar{t}$, $ZZ$, and $hh$, which are individually unable to explain the excess are effectively ``resurrected'' by the improved morphological fit provided by the multi-component framework. Furthermore, we show that these scenarios may mitigate the tension with current constraints, reaching compatibility within existing uncertainties. Our results suggest that the GCE may be the first evidence of a diverse dark sector, favoring a multi-scale solution over the minimal WIMP paradigm.

### [51] [Embedding light dark matter and small neutrino mass in the flipped standard model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17994)
*D. T. Huong,Phung Van Dong,A. E. Carcamo Hernandez*
