<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用翻转标准模型框架，添加$U(1)_N$规范群，暗电荷定义为$D=T_3+N$。中微子质量通过暗场介导的辐射逆跷跷板机制（radiative inverse seesaw mechanism）生成，暗物质候选者为keV尺度的轻费米子。

Result: 发现$U(1)_N$对称性破缺产生的剩余$Z_2$宇称（residual $Z_2$ parity）既稳定了暗物质候选者，又防止其与中微子混合。keV暗物质在早期宇宙可通过$U(1)_N$门户相互作用热产生，但需通过长寿命粒子衰变的晚期熵产生来调节丰度。

Conclusion: 所考虑的参量空间能同时容纳宇宙暴胀和keV暗物质的观测数据。该模型为统一解释中微子质量生成、暗物质候选及宇宙学观测提供了自洽的理论框架。

Abstract: We revisit the flipped standard model where a $U(1)_N$ gauge group is added, determining a dark charge through the weak isospin such as $D=T_3+N$, analogous to the electric charge and hypercharge relation. We find %discover that neutrino masses are appropriately generated by a radiative inverse seesaw mechanism mediated by dark fields. Dark matter candidate is a naturally light fermion with the mass radiatively induced at the keV scale. The residual $Z_2$ parity arising from $U(1)_N$ symmetry breaking both stabilizes the dark matter candidate and prevents its potential mixing with neutrinos. Such residual $Z_2$ parity also guarantees the radiative nature of the inverse seesaw mechanism responsible for light active neutrino mass generation. It is noted that the keV dark matter may be thermally produced in the early Universe as decoupled but being still relativistic and typically overpopulated due to $U(1)_N$ portal interactions. To achieve the correct abundance, the excessive thermal production is counterbalanced by sufficient late-time entropy generation from the decay of long-lived particles. The parameter space under consideration can simultaneously accommodate the observational data from cosmic inflation and keV dark matter.

### [52] [Universal scaling of transport coefficients near the liquid-gas critical point](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17874)
*Johannes V. Roth,Yunxin Ye,Sören Schlichting,Lorenz von Smekal*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究液-气临界点附近输运系数的普适标度行为，特别是热扩散率和剪切粘度的动力学特性，这对于理解临界现象中的非平衡动力学过程具有重要意义。

Method: 采用新颖的实时泛函重整化群（functional renormalization group, FRG）方法，该方法属于非微扰框架，能够处理临界点附近的强关联效应，并与微扰单圈近似的Kawasaki近似进行对比。

Result: 实时FRG计算得到了输运系数（热扩散率和剪切粘度）随温度、外磁场和波数的普适依赖关系，发现其标度函数对趋近临界点的热力学路径依赖较弱，与Kawasaki近似形成对比，且热扩散率的普适波数和温度依赖与临界流体实验数据相符。

Conclusion: 实时FRG方法为研究临界动力学提供了有效的非微扰工具，能够获得更准确的普适标度函数，揭示了输运系数在临界点附近的行为特征，并与实验观测一致。

Abstract: We employ a novel real-time formulation of the functional renormalization group (FRG) to compute universal scaling functions of the thermal diffusivity and the shear viscosity in the vicinity of the liquid-gas critical point, i.e., for the dynamic universality class of Model H from the Halperin-Hohenberg classification. We map out the universal dependence of the transport coefficients on temperature, external magnetic field, and wavenumber, and provide a detailed comparison with the Kawasaki approximation, which is here obtained from a perturbative one-loop approximation to our real-time FRG flow. In contrast to the Kawasaki approximation, the non-perturbative scaling functions from the full real-time FRG flow show a mild dependence on the thermodynamic path towards the critical point. We further compare our FRG results for the universal wavenumber and temperature dependence of the thermal diffusivity with experimental data from critical fluids.

### [53] [On deforming and breaking integrability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17018)
*Ysla F. Adans,Marius de Leeuw,Tristan McLoughlin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究可积模型（integrable models）的最近邻变形（nearest-neighbour deformations），识别出四种变形类型，并在XXZ自旋链（XXZ spin chain）中分析各类变形的能级统计（level statistics）和混沌（chaos）出现特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究可积模型的变形行为，旨在理解不同类型的变形如何影响系统的可积性（integrability）和混沌特性，特别是区分单纯破坏或保持可积性的变形与更微妙的中间情况。

Method: 通过变形参数展开（expanding in the deformation parameter），识别四种变形类型，并在XXZ自旋链中具体分析各类变形；使用能级统计方法（level statistics）数值研究混沌出现方式。

Result: 发现四种变形类型：单纯破坏或保持可积性的变形；需考虑所有阶变形参数才可积的变形（如全息模型中的长程变形）；以及微扰可积（perturbatively integrable）但无法扩展为完全可积模型的变形。数值证据表明各类模型中混沌出现方式不同，微扰可积模型的混沌出现强度呈现介于强弱可积性破坏模型之间的体积标度（volume-scaling）。

Conclusion: 可积模型的变形存在多种类型，包括微妙的中间情况；不同类型的变形导致混沌出现方式存在差异，微扰可积模型表现出独特的体积标度行为，这深化了对可积性破坏机制的理解。

Abstract: In this paper we study nearest-neighbour deformations of integrable models. After expanding in the deformation parameter, we identify four possible types of deformations. First there are deformations that simply break or preserve integrability. Then we find two different subtle cases. The first case is where the deformation is only integrable if all orders of the deformation parameter are taken into account. An example of these are the long-range deformations that appear in holographic models. The second case is when the deformation is perturbatively integrable to some order in the deformation parameter but can not be extended to an integrable model. In this paper we work this out for the XXZ spin chain and discuss the level statistics of each of these cases. We find numerical evidence that the onset of chaos occurs differently in each of these models. For the perturbatively integrable models, we find that the deformation strength at which chaos appears demonstrates a volume-scaling intermediate between strong and weak integrability breaking models.

</details>


### [54] [Resetting in a viscoelastic bath: the bath remembers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17027)
*Ion Santra,Debankur Das*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 研究粘弹性环境中探针粒子的随机重置（stochastic resetting）问题，其中仅探针被重置而介质保留其历史动力学记忆。分析了重置时间尺度与粘弹性弛豫时间尺度之间的竞争，发现非平衡稳态分布与马尔可夫布朗运动的重置结果存在本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究粘弹性环境中随机重置的独特效应，其中仅探针粒子被重置而介质保留记忆。探索重置时间尺度与粘弹性弛豫时间尺度之间的竞争如何影响非平衡稳态的性质。

Method: 采用具有有限相关时间的最小模型进行分析。对于瞬时重置（instantaneous resets），通过解析方法推导极限稳态分布并精确计算时间依赖的主导非零矩。同时研究通过恒定速度返回协议（constant-velocity return protocols）的非瞬时重置。

Result: 发现强记忆效应导致具有非指数尾部的稳态位置分布。与过阻尼布朗运动不同，在粘弹性介质中稳态涨落依赖于重置速度。这种协议依赖性源于环境的有限记忆，突显了环境相关性在重置诱导稳态中的作用。

Conclusion: 粘弹性环境中的随机重置产生与马尔可夫布朗运动重置本质不同的非平衡稳态。环境记忆效应导致稳态分布具有非指数尾部，且稳态涨落对重置协议具有依赖性，表明环境相关性在重置诱导稳态中起关键作用。

Abstract: We study stochastic resetting of a probe particle in a viscoelastic environment where only the probe is reset while the medium retains memory of its past dynamics. Using a minimal model with finite correlation time, we analyze the competition between the resetting timescale and the viscoelastic relaxation timescale. This interplay leads to nonequilibrium steady states that differ qualitatively from those of Markovian Brownian motion with resetting. In particular, strong memory effects produce stationary position distributions with non-exponential tails. For instantaneous resets, we derive the limiting steady-state distributions analytically and compute exactly the time dependent leading non-vanishing moments. We also investigate non-instantaneous resetting via constant-velocity return protocols. In contrast to overdamped Brownian motion, where steady-state fluctuations are independent of the return dynamics, we find that in a viscoelastic medium the fluctuations depend on the reset velocity. This protocol dependence arises from the finite memory of the environment and highlights the role of environmental correlations in resetting-induced steady states.

*Tomaž Prosen*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用矩阵乘积态（matrix-product ansatz）方法，在足够强的边界相互作用条件下显式构造出准局域于边界附近的守恒算符，并分析边界关联函数的衰减特性。

Result: 发现准局域边界模式导致边界关联函数不衰减，对应非零的边界Drude权重。边界模式的关联长度在边界相互作用的有限临界值处发散，表明亚临界相互作用下边界动力学向遍历性转变。

For sufficiently strong boundary interaction we explicitly construct a conserved operator quasi-localized near the boundary using a matrix-product ansatz. This quasi-local edge mode leads to non-decaying boundary correlation functions, corresponding to a nonzero boundary Drude weight. The correlation length of the edge mode diverges at a finite critical value of the boundary interaction, signaling a transition to ergodic boundary dynamics for subcritical interactions.

### [56] [Rejection-free Glauber Monte Carlo for the 2D Random Field Ising Model via Hierarchical Probabilistic Counters](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17032)
*Luca Cattaneo,Federico Ettori,Giovanni Cerri,Paolo Biscari,Ezio Puppin*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种用于二维随机场伊辛模型（RFIM）的高效蒙特卡洛算法，该算法结合了Bortz-Kalos-Lebowitz（BKL）算法的事件驱动、无拒绝特性与Glauber跃迁概率，通过引入分层概率计数器实现O(log N)的自旋选择操作。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统Metropolis算法在低温和低无序（low-disorder）区域存在临界慢化（critical slowing down）问题，而BKL方法无法正确处理随机场（Random Field）存在下的伊辛系统动力学模拟。

Method: 该方法将BKL算法的事件驱动、无拒绝特性与Glauber跃迁概率相结合，引入分层概率计数器（hierarchical probabilistic counters）实现O(log N)复杂度的自旋选择，从而高效采样系统动力学。

Abstract: We present an efficient Monte Carlo algorithm for the simulation of the two-dimensional Random Field Ising Model (RFIM). The method combines the event-driven, rejection-free character of the Bortz Kalos-Lebowitz (BKL) algorithm with Glauber transition probabilities, introducing hierarchical probabilistic counters to perform spin selection in O(log N) operations. This enables efficient sampling of the system's dynamics, especially in the low-temperature and low-disorder regime, where traditional Metropolis updates suffer from critical slowing down. Furthermore, this approach allows a proper dynamical simulation of the Ising system's behavior even in the presence of a Random Field (RF), unlike the BKL method. RFIM simulations with Gaussian field distributions reproduce the expected reduction of the pseudo-critical temperature with increasing disorder. Benchmarking shows speedups exceeding two orders of magnitude compared to the Metropolis algorithm in the low-temperature regime. The proposed method provides an efficient and dynamically faithful tool for studying both equilibrium and non-equilibrium phenomena in disordered spin systems.

By obtaining an exact solution for the renormalization group flows, we investigate the phase structure in the one-pair sector, which includes localized, fractal, and delocalized phases. We show that the quantum number Q, arising from the Bethe ansatz equations, counts the number of cycles and parametrizes the towers of states. Using the action of the renormalization group on the eigenstates, we demonstrate that Q serves as an order parameter, providing a new mechanism for the formation of the fractal phase in the deterministic systems and an example of the interplay between fractality and cyclic RG.

Abstract: This study investigates how visibility graphs constructed from Monte Carlo Markov Chain time series of spin models capture the critical behavior of the system. More precisely, we show that this approach identifies continuous phase transitions as well as important nuances, such as crossover effects occurring in the transition from a critical line to a first-order line through a tricritical point, as observed, for example, in the Blume--Emery--Griffiths model or, in a simpler setting, in the Blume--Capel model. By applying Kirchhoff's theorem, we show that the number of spanning trees of the resulting graphs serves as a sensitive indicator of these phase transitions. Furthermore, a qualitative analysis of the adjacency matrices based on random matrix theory provides additional evidence for these phenomena. The methodology developed here can potentially be extended to the analysis of criticality in empirical time series from complex systems, such as climate, financial, and epidemiological data, where the Hamiltonian governing the dynamics is not necessarily known.

*Amijit Bhattacharjee,Himanshu Bora,Prabwal Phukon*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 在一维Blume-Capel模型中，基于Tsallis非广延统计框架研究热力学几何，发现Tsallis参数q系统地改变赝临界行为和关联结构。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 使用转移矩阵方法，在参数空间(β, J)上构建基于Tsallis熵的热力学度量（作为其负Hessian矩阵），以晶体场各向异性D为控制参数，并计算相关的标量曲率R(T)作为关联度量。

Result: 虽然一维系统中没有真正的相变，但R(T)表现出有限的峰值，标志着赝临界交叉。分析D<J和D>J两种状态，发现偏离Boltzmann-Gibbs极限(q=1)会系统地改变曲率分布：q>1时峰值移动且关联在交叉后持续存在，q<1时峰值减弱或抑制。

Conclusion: Tsallis参数q从几何上重塑了熵表面，为自旋-1系统中的非广延效应提供了清晰的信息几何解释。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamic geometry of the one-dimensional Blume--Capel model within the Tsallis nonextensive framework to understand how generalized statistics modify correlation structure and pseudo-critical behaviour. Using the transfer matrix method, we construct the Tsallis entropy based thermodynamic metric as its negative Hessian on the parameter space $(β, J)$, with the crystal-field anisotropy $D$ as a control parameter, and compute the associated scalar curvature $R(T)$ as a measure of correlations. Although no true phase transition occurs in one dimension, $R(T)$ exhibits finite peaks signaling pseudo-critical crossovers. We analyze both $D < J$ and $D > J$ regimes and show that deviations from the Boltzmann--Gibbs limit ($q=1$) systematically deform the curvature profile: for $q>1$ the peak shifts and correlations persist beyond the crossover, whereas for $q<1$ the peak is weakened or suppressed. Our results demonstrate that the Tsallis parameter $q$ geometrically reshapes the entropy surface, providing a clear information-geometric interpretation of nonextensive effects in spin-1 systems.

### [60] [Study of Meta-Fibonacci Integer Sequences by Continuous Self-Referential Functional Equations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17509)
*Klaus Pinn*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出并研究了使用连续函数方程（continuous functional equations）分析元斐波那契整数序列（meta-Fibonacci integer sequences）的方法，重点考察了Conway序列、作者提出的D序列和Hofstadter的Q序列，通过去趋势化形式建立了连续函数模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索使用连续函数方程分析元斐波那契整数序列的方法。这类序列具有复杂的递归结构，传统离散分析方法难以揭示其全局行为特征，需要建立连续模型来更好地理解其数学本质。

Method: 方法包括：1）将三个元斐波那契序列转换为去趋势化形式（detrended forms）$(a,d,q)(n)=2\,(A,D,Q)(n)-n$；2）对$a(n)$和$d(n)$建立高度对称的函数方程并求解精确连续解；3）对Hofstadter序列开发连续函数模型，并采用随机矩阵方法（random matrix approach）生成和研究分形解。

Result: 研究结果显示：对于$a(n)$和$d(n)$，高度对称的函数方程存在精确连续解，能够很好地模拟序列的全局行为（骨干结构）。对于Q序列，连续函数模型成功再现了两个显著特性：生成长度的反常标度（anomalous scaling）以$\sim (2-η)^k$形式标度，以及振幅增长以$2^{αk}$形式标度的反常增长模式。

Conclusion: 结论表明连续函数方程为研究元斐波那契序列提供了有效的分析框架。该方法不仅能够精确描述某些序列的全局行为，还能通过随机矩阵方法研究分形解，成功再现了Hofstadter序列的复杂标度特性，为理解这类递归序列的数学结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: I propose and investigate the use of continuous functional equations for the study of meta-Fibonacci integer sequences. This exploratory study includes three sequences with quite different behavior: Conway's famous sequence $A(n)= A(A(n-1))+A(n-A(n-1))$, the sequence $D(n)= D(D(n-1))+D(n-1-D(n-2))$ introduced by the present author more than 25 years ago, and Hofstadter's well-known $Q(n)= Q(n-Q(n-1))+Q(n-Q(n-2))$. The sequences are studied in their equivalent detrended forms $(a,d,q)(n)=2\,(A,D,Q)(n)-n$. For $a(n)$ and $d(n)$, a highly symmetric functional equation admits exact continuous solutions that nicely model the global behavior (backbone) of the sequences. For the Hofstadter sequence, a continuous functional model is developed that leads to a random matrix approach for the generation and study of fractal solutions. Two remarkable properties of the Q-sequence are reproduced by the model: the anomalous scaling of the generation length, which scales $\sim (2-η)^k$, and the anomalous amplitude growth that scales like $2^{αk}$.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 作者引入了一种唯象理论（phenomenological theory），用于预测接近边际稳定性时涨落的反常标度。通过两种不同的简化模型（simplified models）进行扩展数值模拟（extended numerical simulations）来验证理论预测。

Result: 理论预测了反常标度行为，并确定了反常涨落存在的临界窗口（critical window）。该临界窗口以$N^{-1/5}$的缓慢速率收缩，在边际稳定性周围覆盖了广泛区域。数值模拟结果证实了理论预测。

Conclusion: 该唯象理论成功预测了长程相互作用无碰撞系统中有限尺寸涨落在接近边际稳定性时的反常标度行为，明确了反常涨落与高斯涨落之间的临界窗口，并通过数值模拟验证了理论的有效性。

Abstract: Finite size fluctuations are a crucial ingredient in kinetic theory of long-range interacting collisionless systems. In this Letter, we introduce a phenomenological theory which predicts an anomalous scaling close to marginal stability for these fluctuations. It also pinpoints the critical window inside which the fluctuations are anomalous, and outside which they are Gaussian. Shrinking very slowly as $N^{-1/5}$, this critical window encompasses a wide region around marginal stability. We confirm our predictions through extended numerical simulations on two different simplified models.

### [62] [Two stroke Pumping Technique for Many-Body Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17873)
*Serge Galam*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于两冲程泵浦技术（two stroke pumping technique, TSP），该技术结合了Bethe簇设置、Metropolis更新和社会物理学中的Galam多数模型（Galam Majority Model），构建了一个通用的分析框架。

Result: 在Ising模型中，TSP在维度d=2,3,4下得到的临界温度T_c值均比精确估计值高出+0.03，在d=1时准确得到T_c=0；同时分析表明在T=0时实现完全对称破缺实际上是不可能的，结果与数值发现吻合良好。

Conclusion: TSP框架具有计算高效、透明的特点，所需计算资源显著少于蒙特卡洛采样，且具有通用性，可扩展到广泛的离散自旋模型，是研究多体相互作用系统中合作行为的中间但可扩展的工具。

Abstract: I introduce a new analytical framework for estimating critical temperatures in interacting many-body systems, focusing on the Ising model. Combining the Bethe cluster setting, the Metropolis update, and the Galam Majority Model developed in sociophysics, I build a two stroke pumping technique (TSP). Applied to the Ising model in dimensions d=2, 3, 4, TSP yields values of T_c which are all at an excess of +0.03 from exact estimates. At d=1 the exact value T_c=0 is obtained. In addition, TSP indicates analytically the practical impossibility to reach full symmetry breaking at T=0. The results are thus found in good agreement with numerical findings while requiring significantly fewer computational resources than Monte Carlo sampling. Calculations are computationally efficient and transparent. The framework is general and can be extended to a broad class of discrete spin models. This positions TSP as an intermediate yet scalable tool for studying cooperative behavior in many body interacting systems.

### [63] [A dynamic mechanism for prevalence of triangles in competitive networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17584)
*M. N. Mooij,M. Baudena,A. S. von der Heydt,L. Miele,I. Kryven*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该研究提出三角形（triangles）在现实网络中的普遍存在可能源于Lotka-Volterra竞争系统中维持物种共存的动态稳定性要求，而非传统的三元闭合或几何连接机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实网络中三角形普遍存在，但稀疏图的标准零模型中却很少见。现有解释通常依赖显式的三元闭合机制或基于几何的连接规则，本研究旨在探索三角形出现的替代性解释。

Method: 通过分析所有可能的相互作用图，证明当耦合强度低于图最大度的倒数时，共存得以保证；同时证明共存可维持至临界耦合强度为1。在保持度序列固定的情况下，算法优化网络结构，并分析真实草地植物网络。

Result: 支持更强相互作用强度的网络在多个网络模型中始终表现出更高的聚类系数（clustering coefficients）。在真实草地植物网络中，观测到的聚类和稳定性均高于具有相同度序列的配置模型预期值。

Conclusion: 三角形及一般聚类可能作为稳定竞争的结构特征而出现，这为现实网络中三角形的普遍存在提供了基于动态稳定性要求的新解释。

Abstract: Triangles are abundant in real-world networks but rare in standard null models for sparse graphs. Existing explanations typically rely on explicit triadic closure mechanisms or geometry-based connection rules. We propose an alternative hypothesis: the frequent appearance of triangles may arise naturally from the requirement of dynamic stability that maintains coexistence of species in Lotka-Volterra systems with competitive interactions. To evaluate this idea, we show that, across all possible interaction graphs, coexistence is guaranteed whenever the coupling strength is below the reciprocal of the graph's maximum degree. We also show that coexistence can persist up to a critical coupling strength of 1, which leaves a large gap that is unexplained by the graph degrees alone. These lower and upper bounds are achieved for star and complete graphs respectively. To investigate what structural properties of the interaction graph control the critical coupling within the gap, we optimise networks algorithmically while keeping the degree sequence fixed. We find that networks supporting stronger interaction strengths consistently exhibit higher clustering coefficients in several network models. Moreover, in real-world grassland plant networks, we observe higher clustering and stronger stability than those expected from a configuration model with the same degree sequence. Our result suggests that triangles, and clustering in general, may emerge as a structural signature of stabilising competition.

### [64] [On the Astrophysical Origin of Binary Black Hole Subpopulations: A Tale of Three Channels?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17987)
*Anarya Ray,Shirsha Mukherjee,Michael Zevin,Vicky Kalogera*

Main category: astro-ph.HE

TL;DR: 该研究通过参数化混合模型分析LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA引力波数据，发现双黑洞（BBH）探测样本包含三个不同的天体物理亚群，分别对应不同的形成通道，并约束了各通道的相对比例及其宇宙学演化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA合作组积累的引力波目录中，越来越多的证据表明双黑洞（BBH）存在多个亚群。然而，对这些复杂基础群体的天体物理解释受到双星演化、核心坍缩和宿主环境处理中理论不确定性的限制。

Method: 本研究采用参数化混合模型（parametrized mixture models）分析双黑洞探测样本，识别不同的天体物理亚群及其特征，而不对双黑洞参数分布中的质量转变进行显式建模。

Result: 研究发现双黑洞质量谱中的10M⊙峰值和35M⊙特征对应着不同的质量比、自旋对齐、自旋进动和红移演化特性。推断的分布自然呈现出先前报道的质量转变现象，结果与孤立双星演化、球状星团中的动力学形成以及高代双黑洞合并的相对丰度一致。

Conclusion: 研究约束了三种形成通道的相对基础比例分别为79.0^{+11.5}_{-10.9}%、14.5^{+11.6}_{-8.0}%和2.5^{+5.5}_{-1.8}%，并发现这些相对比例以超过1σ置信度随宇宙时间演化。该解释基于相对稳健的理论预测，预期未来将获得更明确的结论。

Abstract: There is increasing evidence for multiple binary black hole~(BBH) subpopulations in the cumulative gravitational wave catalog by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA Collaboration. The astrophysical interpretation of this complex underlying population is subject to theoretical uncertainties in treatments of binary stellar evolution, core collapse, and host environments. In this \textit{Letter}, using parametrized mixture models, we show that the BBH detection sample comprises three astrophysical subpopulations that are likely dominated by specific formation channels. In particular, we show that the $10M_{\odot}$ peak and the $35M_{\odot}$ feature in the BBH mass spectrum correspond to distinct mass-ratio, spin alignment, spin precession, and redshift evolution properties. We show that mass-based transitions reported in the distribution of BBH parameters naturally emerge from our inferred distributions without explicit modeling. Our results are consistent with the current observed population arising from specific relative abundances of isolated binary evolution, dynamical formation in globular clusters, and higher-generation BBH mergers. Under this interpretation, we constrain the relative underlying fraction of these channels to be $79.0^{+11.5}_{-10.9}\%$, $14.5^{+11.6}_{-8.0}\%$, and, $2.5^{+5.5}_{-1.8}\%$, respectively, and find these relative fractions to be evolving over cosmic time with more than $1σ$ confidence. Our interpretation relies on simple theoretical predictions that are mostly robust against uncertainties in BBH formation, with more definite conclusions expected in the near future.

</details>

### [65] [Momentum-gapped quasiparticles in disordered metals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17002)
*Miguel-Ángel Sánchez-Martínez,Blaise Goutéraux,Louk Rademaker,Felix Flicker*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文发现了一种新型量子集体模式，其色散关系在低动量下具有纯虚能量，对应于有限寿命的动量弛豫模式，首次在相关量子物质中直接观测到这种第三类色散行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自然界存在线性色散的无质量粒子和具有有限质量隙的二次色散有质量粒子，两者在凝聚态物理中都有对应物。然而，假设的第三类粒子——超光速快子（tachyon）在低动量下能量未定义，类似地，流体力学中长期假设的集体模式在低动量下具有纯虚能量，这种第三类可能性从未在量子系统中被直接观测到。

Method: 通过仔细比较流体力学与金属微观模型，建立了这种先前未见色散出现在相关量子物质中的条件。作为动量弛豫模式的具体例子，考虑了在Sr$_2$RuO$_4$中最近发现的声学等离子体激元（称为Pines' demon）。

Result: 研究发现，当电子流体因杂质导致的平移对称性显式破缺而经历动量弛豫时，这种第三类色散出现在相关量子物质中。观测到的中性模式色散与随机相位近似（random phase approximation）预测的无质量线性行为显著不同，实际上对应于动量带隙准粒子（momentum-gapped quasiparticle）。

Conclusion: 该工作首次在量子系统中直接观测到具有纯虚能量的第三类色散关系，揭示了动量弛豫模式在相关量子物质中的存在，为理解集体激发行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: Nature contains massless particles with linear dispersions, and massive particles whose energies depend quadratically on their momenta with finite mass gaps. Both have equivalents in condensed matter physics in the form of collective modes and quasiparticles, measurable excitations with well-defined energy-momentum relations. A hypothesised third particle type - the super-luminal tachyon - would have an undefined energy at low momentum. A similar collective mode - long hypothesised within the hydrodynamic theory of matter - would have a purely imaginary energy at low momentum, corresponding to a finite lifetime. This third possibility has never been directly observed in a quantum system. Through a careful comparison of hydrodynamics with microscopic models of metals, we establish that this previously unseen third dispersion occurs in correlated quantum matter whenever the electronic fluid undergoes momentum relaxation due to explicit breaking of translation by impurities. As a specific example of these momentum-relaxed modes we consider the recent discovery of an acoustic plasmon - dubbed Pines' demon - in Sr$_2$RuO$_4$. The observed dispersion of this neutral mode differed significantly from the massless linear behaviour predicted by the random phase approximation. We demonstrate that the observed dispersion corresponds, in fact, to a momentum-gapped quasiparticle.

</details>


### [66] [Luttinger's Theorem Violation and Green's Function Topological Invariants in a Fractional Chern Insulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17006)
*Anton A. Markov,Andrey M. Nikishin,Nigel R. Cooper,Nathan Goldman,Lucila Peralta Gavensky*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过精确对角化方法，在分数陈绝缘体（fractional Chern insulator）相中计算单粒子格林函数，揭示了Luttinger定理的违反现象，并阐明了格林函数拓扑不变量与多体陈数（many-body Chern number）之间的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在强关联拓扑相（如分数陈绝缘体）中，分数化准粒子缺乏与电子的绝热连接，这引发了格林函数拓扑不变量如何在此类相中表现的问题。Luttinger定理的违反现象在强关联拓扑相中尤为引人注目。

Method: 采用费米子Harper-Hofstadter-Hubbard模型的精确对角化（exact diagonalization）方法，在分数陈绝缘体相深处计算体单粒子格林函数（bulk single-particle Green's functions），并直接评估Luttinger计数、其可能的修正（Luttinger积分）以及Ishikawa-Matsuyama不变量$N_3[\mathrm{G}]$。

Result: 研究明确展示了Luttinger定理的违反，并证明多体陈数的分数性质编码在Luttinger积分的Středa响应中，而整数不变量$N_3[\mathrm{G}]$则源于Luttinger计数的Středa响应。在忽略Bloch带混合的情况下，$N_3[\mathrm{G}]$完全由Luttinger计数与占据Bloch带的陈数决定。

Conclusion: 研究提出了从局域态密度测量中提取所有基于格林函数的拓扑不变量的实验方案，该方案在分数量子霍尔系统中具有实验可行性。这为在强关联拓扑相中表征格林函数拓扑不变量提供了理论框架和实验途径。

Abstract: Luttinger's theorem constrains the particle density of interacting fermions through global properties of the single-particle Green's function, and its violation signals a breakdown of the identification between the quantized Hall response and the Green-function-based Ishikawa-Matsuyama invariant. This phenomenon becomes especially compelling in strongly correlated topological phases, such as fractional Chern insulators, where fractionalized quasiparticles lack an adiabatic connection to electrons, raising the question of how Green's-function-based topological invariants manifest in such phases. Using exact diagonalization of the fermionic Harper-Hofstadter-Hubbard model, we compute bulk single-particle Green's functions deep inside a fractional Chern insulating phase and directly evaluate the Luttinger count, its possible correction (the Luttinger integral), and the Ishikawa-Matsuyama invariant $N_3[\mathrm{G}]$. We demonstrate a clear violation of Luttinger's theorem and show that the fractional nature of the many-body Chern number is encoded in the Středa response of the Luttinger integral, while the integer invariant $N_3[\mathrm{G}]$ arises from the Středa response of the Luttinger count. We also analytically prove that $N_3[\mathrm{G}]$ is fully determined by the Luttinger count together with the Chern number of the occupied Bloch band, upon neglecting Bloch-band mixing. Finally, we propose an experimental protocol to extract all Green-function-based topological invariants from local density-of-states measurements, experimentally accessible in fractional quantum Hall systems.

</details>


### [67] [Field-direction sensitivity of Kondo hybridization in UTe$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17037)
*Thomas Halloran,Gicela Saucedo Salas,Sylvia K. Lewin,J. A. Rodriguez-Rivera,Colin L. Sarkis,Jakob Lass,Daniel G. Mazzone,Marc Janoschek,Nicholas P. Butch*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过中子散射实验发现，自旋三重态超导体UTe₂在沿晶体a轴施加磁场时，其低能磁响应表现出与Kondo杂化相关的特征性变化，特别是在μ₀H=7 T附近出现显著转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索自旋三重态超导体（spin-triplet superconductor）UTe₂中低能磁响应对外加磁场的敏感性，特别是沿晶体a轴方向磁场对重f电子与裸导带之间杂化（hybridization）的影响。

Method: 采用中子散射（neutron scattering）实验方法，测量UTe₂在沿晶体a轴磁场（最高达μ₀H=13 T）作用下的非弹性中子谱权重（inelastic neutron spectral weight）变化，并分析其能量转移特征。

Result: 实验发现最大非弹性中子谱权重随磁场增加向更高能量转移，且在μ₀H=7 T附近dℏω_peak/dH出现显著增加。这一行为与电阻率中观察到的Kondo杂化（Kondo hybridization）特征平行。

Conclusion: 测量结果表明，沿晶体a轴方向约μ₀H=7 T的磁场诱导了重f电子（heavy f-electrons）与裸导带（bare conduction band）之间杂化状态的变化，揭示了磁场对UTe₂中电子关联效应的调控作用。

Abstract: Neutron scattering experiments on the spin-triplet superconductor UTe$_2$ have established that the dominant low-energy magnetic response is along Brillouin zone boundaries, resembling the magnetic susceptibility of narrow-gap interband excitations. We report a study of the sensitivity of these excitations to magnetic field along the crystallographic $\hat{a}$-axis. Up to fields of $μ_0 H$=13 T, the maximal inelastic neutron spectral weight increases in energy transfer, with a pronounced increase in $d\hbarω_{peak}/dH$ near $μ_0 H$=7 T. This behavior parallels the field and temperature dependent features of the electrical resistivity that are associated with Kondo hybridization. Our measurements suggest that $\hat{a}$-axis fields near $μ_0 H$=7~T induce a change in the hybridization between heavy $f$-electrons and the bare conduction band.

</details>


### [68] [Generalized symmetry-protected topological phases in mixed states from gauging dualities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17282)
*Linhao Li,Zhen Bi,Weiguang Cao*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过建立具有广义对称性的混合态相与具有普通群对称性的混合态相之间的规范对应关系，将非可逆和偶极平均对称保护拓扑相的分类问题转化为具有对偶对称性的对称破缺相和平均对称保护拓扑相的熟悉分类问题。

Result: 在(1+1)维中分类和构造了具有非可逆和偶极对称性的平均对称保护拓扑相子类，包括那些对混合态本质的相，并通过弦序参数和受保护的边缘模式对其进行了表征。

Conclusion: 该工作通过规范对应关系连接了广义对称性与混合态拓扑相的研究方向，为理解非可逆和偶极对称性在混合态中的影响提供了系统框架，并将复杂分类问题转化为已知的对称破缺和平均对称保护拓扑相分类问题。

Abstract: Decoherence in realistic quantum platforms motivates a mixed-state notion of topological phases of matter, including average symmetry-protected topological (ASPT) phases. Alongside this progress, generalized symmetries--notably noninvertible and dipole symmetries--have become powerful organizing principles for exotic quantum phases, yet their implications for mixed states remain less explored. In this work, we bridge these directions through a gauging correspondence between mixed-state phases with generalized symmetries and mixed-state phases with ordinary group symmetries, recasting the classification of noninvertible and dipole ASPT phases into familiar classifications of symmetry breaking and ASPT phases with dual symmetries. Using this approach, we classify and construct a subclass of ASPT phases with non-invertible and dipole symmetries in $(1+1)d$, including phases that are intrinsic to mixed states, and characterize them via string order parameters and protected edge modes.

### [69] [Exactly Solvable Disorder-free Quantum Breakdown Model: Spectrum, Thermodynamics, and Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17379)
*Kinya Guan,Hosho Katsura*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文引入并研究了一种具有全对全相互作用的无序量子击穿模型，该模型哈密顿量可分解为零动量模占据数与仅含配对项的二次哈密顿量的乘积，使其精确可解并产生大量零能态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在建立一个精确可解的理论框架，用于在无序、空间结构和环境耦合缺失的情况下，以可控方式分析量子系统的谱性质和实时动力学行为。

Method: 通过引入具有全对全相互作用的无序量子击穿模型，其哈密顿量具有因子化结构：可分解为零动量模占据数与仅含配对项的二次哈密顿量的乘积，这一特殊结构使模型精确可解。

Result: 模型产生大量零能态，因子化结构显著影响谱形状因子和实时动力学；计算两点函数和失序时间关联函数（OTOCs）时，在OTOCs中发现了独特的早期增长机制。

Conclusion: 该模型提供了一个精确可解的理论框架，使得在无序、空间结构和环境耦合缺失的情况下，能够以可控方式分析量子系统的谱性质和实时动力学行为。

Abstract: We introduce and study a disorder-free version of the quantum breakdown model with all-to-all interactions. The Hamiltonian factorizes into the product of the zero-momentum-mode occupation number and a quadratic Hamiltonian including only pairing terms. This structure makes the model exactly solvable and produces a large set of zero-energy states. We analyze its spectral, thermodynamic, and dynamical properties. In particular, we show how the factorized structure shapes the spectral form factor and the real-time dynamics. We also compute two-point functions and out-of-time-ordered correlators (OTOCs), and find a distinct early-time growth regime in the OTOCs. These results provide a solvable setting in which spectral properties and real-time dynamics can be analyzed in a controlled way in the absence of disorder, spatial structure, and environmental coupling.

### [70] [Emergent superconformal symmetry in the phase diagram of a 1D $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ lattice gauge theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17807)
*Bachana Beradze,Mikheil Tsitsishvili,Sergej Moroz*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维$\mathbb{Z}_{2}$晶格规范理论（lattice gauge theory）的相图和临界性质，该理论描述正交金属（orthogonal metal），其中无自旋费米子（spinless fermions）和伊辛自旋（Ising spins）与去禁闭$\mathbb{Z}_{2}$规范场（gauge field）最小耦合。通过精确映射和场论分析，揭示了超共形对称性（superconformal symmetry）的涌现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索规范-物质系统中涌现的超共形临界性（emergent superconformal criticalities）。该工作旨在建立规范-物质系统中超共形临界性的最小晶格实现，并为量子模拟器（quantum simulators）中的探索提供途径。

Method: 在费米子半填充（half-filling）条件下，推导出精确的规范不变表述，将模型映射到解耦的XXZ和横场伊辛链（transverse-field Ising chains）。该映射实现了受控的低能场论描述，基于微扰的Luttinger液体（Luttinger liquid）和伊辛共形场论（Ising conformal field theories）。结合解析论证和数值模拟（numerical simulations）来确定完整相图。

Result: 确定了完整的相图，识别了各种临界和多临界区域（critical and multi-critical regimes）。在费米子和玻色子速度重合的特定多临界线（multi-critical line）上，发现了涌现超共形对称性（emergent superconformal symmetry）的有力证据。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了规范-物质系统中涌现超共形临界性的最小晶格实现，并为量子模拟器中的探索提供了可行路径。该工作为理解规范-物质耦合系统中的新型临界现象提供了理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate the phase diagram and critical properties of a one-dimensional $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ lattice gauge theory describing an orthogonal metal, where spinless fermions and Ising spins are minimally coupled to a deconfined $\mathbb{Z}_{2}$ gauge field. Working at half-filling of fermions, we derive an exact gauge-invariant formulation that maps the model onto decoupled XXZ and transverse-field Ising chains. This mapping enables a controlled low-energy field-theory description in terms of a perturbed Luttinger liquid and Ising conformal field theories. Combining analytical arguments with numerical simulations, we determine the full phase diagram and identify various critical and multi-critical regimes. Along a specific multi-critical line, where the fermionic and bosonic velocities coincide, we find strong evidence for an emergent superconformal symmetry. Our results establish a minimal lattice realization of emergent superconformal criticalities in a gauge-matter system and provide a route toward its exploration in quantum simulators.

Method: 研究采用电子自旋共振（electron spin resonance, ESR）光谱技术，探索了在反铁磁有序温度（TN ≈ 30 K）以下磁振子激发谱的磁场（H）依赖性，以及在TN以上的相关自旋动力学行为。

Result: ESR揭示了显著的铁磁（ferromagnetic, FM）自旋关联，这些关联在远高于TN的温度下持续存在，表明CuCrP₂S₆的自旋动力学具有本质的二维特征。在T < TN时，材料在零磁场下表现出两个非简并（即能量不同）的反铁磁磁振子模式，这些模式可随磁场增加而调谐为铁磁型集体自旋激发。

Conclusion: 这些显著特性有利于在CuCrP₂S₆中诱导和控制单向自旋电流（unidirectional spin current），表明该材料可作为磁电子学的新型功能材料。

Abstract: The use of antiferromagnets in magnetoelectronic devices as counterparts of ferromagnets is a new, rapidly developing trend in spintronics that leverages antiferromagnetic (AFM) magnons for transmitting of spin currents. Van der Waals (vdW) antiferromagnets are particularly attractive in this respect as they possess tunable magnetic properties and can be easily integrated into spintronic devices. In this work we use electron spin resonance (ESR) spectroscopy to assess the potential of the vdW AFM compound CuCrP$_{2}$S$_{6}$ for magnonic applications by exploring the magnetic field ($H$) dependence of the spectrum of magnon excitations below its AFM ordering temperature $T_{\rm N} \approx 30$ K and the correlated spin dynamics above $T_{\rm N}$. ESR reveals prominent ferromagnetic (FM) spin correlations that persist far above $T_{\rm N}$ suggesting an intrinsically two-dimensional character of the spin dynamics in CuCrP$_{2}$S$_{6}$. Most interestingly, at $T < T_{\rm N}$, CuCrP$_{2}$S$_{6}$ features two non-degenerate, i.e., distinct in energy AFM magnon modes at $H = 0$ which can be tuned to the FM type of collective spin excitations with increasing $H$. These remarkable properties are favorable for the induction and control of unidirectional spin current in CuCrP$_{2}$S$_{6}$ and suggest it as a new functional material for magnetoelectronics.

### [72] [Novel Magnetoacoustic Resonance Technique for Exploring Hidden Quadrupoles in a Crystal Field Quartet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17359)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出了一种新型磁声共振技术，结合声学诱导的应变场与线性偏振高频微波场来探测四重态中的四极矩。利用Floquet理论（Floquet theory）公式化了同时单声子-单光子吸收跃迁过程，并通过改变体声波传播方向来研究跃迁概率的变化。

Abstract: Crystal field quartets with quadrupole degrees of freedom play a crucial role in hidden ordering systems, as exemplified by CeB$_6$. We present a novel magnetoacoustic resonance technique that combines acoustically induced strain fields with a linearly polarized high-frequency microwave field to probe quadrupoles inherent in the quartet hidden behind magnetic properties. This method offers the advantage of enabling quantum quadrupole resonance transitions for large excitation energy gaps within quartet sublevels under a strong magnetic field, which cannot be achieved by acoustic experiments alone. Formulating a simultaneous single-phonon-single-photon absorption transition process using Floquet theory, we demonstrate how the transition probabilities are affected by changing the propagation direction of a bulk acoustic wave. The key result is that distinct maxima in transition probabilities, attributed to specific propagation directions, indicate a characteristic of quadrupole physics and exhibit an abrupt change owing to an induced ordered moment. This photon-assisted magnetoacoustic resonance technique will promote a broader range of applications of acoustic experiments for the study of quadrupole physics.

### [73] [Field-induced quasi-bound state within the two-magnon continuum of a square-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17635)

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过高分辨率非弹性中子散射（high-resolution inelastic neutron scattering）和矩阵乘积态（MPS）计算，在二维S=1/2正方晶格海森堡反铁磁体（square-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet）中发现了一种位于双磁振子连续谱（two-magnon continuum）内的尖锐、色散的"拉莫尔阴影模式（Larmor-shadow mode）"，这是无隙二维反铁磁体中首次观测到的尖锐准束缚态（quasi-bound state）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究二维量子磁体（quantum magnets）中的强量子相互作用效应，特别是在磁场诱导下的自旋动力学。使用金属有机框架材料CuF$_2$(D$_2$O)$_2$(pyz)作为S=1/2正方晶格海森堡反铁磁体模型系统，探索超越三分之一饱和场的场依赖自旋动力学。

Method: 采用高分辨率非弹性中子散射技术测量磁场依赖的自旋动力学谱。通过圆柱矩阵乘积态（cylinder matrix-product-state, MPS）计算定量重现场诱导谱，并应用谱一致的1/S自旋波理论（spin-wave theory）分析模式性质。

Result: 发现了一个异常尖锐、色散的"阴影模式（shadow mode）"，该模式位于双磁振子连续谱内，以拉莫尔能量（Larmor energy）为偏移量跟随横向单磁振子支的色散。该"拉莫尔阴影模式"被确认为复合双磁振子共振（composite two-magnon resonance），其小本征线宽表明吸引性磁振子-磁振子相互作用（attractive magnon-magnon interactions）的非微扰效应。零场下的(π,0)异常（zero-field (π,0) anomaly）随磁场增加而消失。

Conclusion: 研究首次在无隙二维反铁磁体中观测到嵌入连续谱的尖锐准束缚态。拉莫尔阴影模式源于波矢Q处的色散磁振子与Γ点均匀拉莫尔进动的耦合，其尖锐特征揭示了吸引性磁振子相互作用的非微扰本质。磁场增强使谱权重集中于单磁振子和拉莫尔阴影模式，改变了量子涨落现象。

Abstract: Quantum magnets in two dimensions display strong quantum interaction effects even when magnetically ordered. Using the metal-organic framework material CuF$_2$(D$_2$O)$_2$(pyz), we investigate the field-dependent spin dynamics of the $S = 1/2$ square-lattice Heisenberg antiferromagnet by high-resolution inelastic neutron scattering to applied fields beyond one third of saturation. We discover an anomalously sharp, dispersive ``shadow mode'' residing within the two-magnon continuum, which shadows the dispersion of the transverse one-magnon branches across the Brillouin zone at an offset equal to the Larmor energy. We perform cylinder matrix-product-state (MPS) calculations that reproduce the field-induced spectrum quantitatively and apply a spectrally consistent $1/S$ spin-wave theory to deduce that the ``Larmor-shadow mode'' is a composite two-magnon resonance: a dispersing magnon at wavevector ${\bf Q}$ couples to the uniform Larmor precession at $Γ$, its small intrinsic linewidth indicating a non-perturbative effect of attractive magnon-magnon interactions. Another quantum-fluctuation phenomenon, the zero-field $(π,0)$ anomaly, is lost at increasing fields, which tighten the spectral weight into the one-magnon and Larmor-shadow modes. To our knowledge, these results constitute the first observation of a sharp quasi-bound state embedded in the continuum of a gapless two-dimensional antiferromagnet.

### [74] [Hamiltonian Monte Carlo enhanced by Exact Diagonalization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17788)
*Finn L. Temmen,Martina Gisti,David J. Luitz,Thomas Luu,Johann Ostmeyer*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种结合精确对角化（ED）和哈密顿蒙特卡洛（HMC）的混合算法H²MC，用于模拟二维耦合量子线阵列（相互作用费米子哈伯德链），以克服两种方法各自的计算限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 强关联费米子系统在凝聚态物理中具有重要意义，但现有数值方法存在根本性限制：精确对角化（ED）受限于系统尺寸的指数级扩展，而蒙特卡洛方法则面临符号问题（sign problem）和长自相关时间（autocorrelation times）的困扰。

Method: 提出了一种混合算法H²MC，结合了精确对角化（ED）和哈密顿蒙特卡洛（HMC）方法，用于模拟二维耦合量子线阵列（2D arrays of coupled quantum wires），这些阵列被建模为相互作用的费米子哈伯德链（interacting fermionic Hubbard chains）。

Result: H²MC在多个关键模拟方面优于单独使用任一种方法：与纯ED相比，H²MC具有更有利的计算扩展性，能够模拟更大的二维阵列；与纯HMC相比，H²MC显著缓解了符号问题并减少了自相关时间，无论使用实辅助场（real auxiliary fields）还是虚辅助场（imaginary auxiliary fields）。

Conclusion: 该形式化方法展示了如何利用看似不同方法的互补优势，在扩展参数空间（extended parameter space）中实现可行的模拟，为解决计算物理中的核心挑战提供了新途径。

Abstract: Strongly correlated fermionic systems are of great interest in condensed matter physics and numerical methods are indispensable tools for their study. However, existing approaches such as exact diagonalization (ED) and stochastic quantum Monte Carlo methods each suffer from fundamental limitations: ED is hindered by exponential scaling in system size, while Monte Carlo methods are plagued by sign problems and long autocorrelation times. These limitations restrict the accessible parameter space and developing algorithms that efficiently alleviate them remains a central challenge in computational physics. In this work, we propose a hybrid algorithm that combines ED and Hamiltonian Monte Carlo (HMC) to simulate 2D arrays of coupled quantum wires, modeled as interacting fermionic Hubbard chains. We demonstrate how our hybrid implementation of HMC, which we dub H$^2$MC, outperforms either method alone across several key simulation facets. When compared to pure ED, H$^2$MC has a much more favorable computational scaling, which allows us to push simulations to much larger 2D arrays. H$^2$MC also greatly alleviates the sign problem and reduces autocorrelation times when compared to pure HMC formulations utilizing either real or imaginary auxiliary fields. Our formalism demonstrates how complementary strengths of seemingly disparate methods can be leveraged to enable feasible simulations in an extended parameter space.

### [75] [Site-selective renormalization and competing magnetic instabilities in paramagnet Y$_{3}$Cu$_{2}$Sb$_{3}$O$_{14}$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17796)
*Yanpeng Zhou,Gang Li*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过理论计算揭示了Y₃Cu₂Sb₃O₁₄中两个不等价Cu位点具有相反的晶体场劈裂，导致选择性轨道重整化，并结合几何阻挫和竞争磁不稳定性，使其成为有前景的量子自旋液体候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用综合理论研究方法：分析晶体结构中两个不等价Cu位点（八面体CuO₆和轴向压缩CuO₈）的晶体场劈裂；运用动力学平均场理论（dynamical mean-field theory, DMFT）计算轨道选择性重整化；通过FLEX计算研究磁不稳定性竞争。

Result: 发现Cu-2位点未配对空穴位于d_{z^2}轨道，而Cu-1保持传统d_{x^2-y^2}/d_{xy}特性，形成窄带结构。DMFT显示Cu-1经历莫特转变（Mott transition）而Cu-2保持金属性。FLEX计算表明多个磁不稳定性以近乎相等的强度竞争，自旋磁化率无主导峰，与实验中无长程磁有序一致。

Conclusion: Y₃Cu₂Sb₃O₁₄中不同的晶体场环境、强关联效应和竞争交换相互作用共同作用，稳定了奇异的量子基态，使其成为有前景的量子自旋液体候选材料。这种独特组合源于三角晶格上的几何阻挫和局部环境差异。

Abstract: Quantum spin liquids (QSLs) are exotic phases of matter characterized by long-range entanglement and the absence of magnetic order even at zero temperature. Here, we present a comprehensive theoretical study of the frustrated magnet Y$_{3}$Cu$_{2}$Sb$_{3}$O$_{14}$ to elucidate its electronic and magnetic properties. We uncover two inequivalent Cu sites with fundamentally distinct oxygen coordination, i.e. octahedral CuO$_6$ and axially compressed CuO$_8$, that give rise to completely opposite crystal-field splittings. This inversion places the unpaired hole in the $d_{z^2}$ orbital at the Cu-2 site, while Cu-1 maintains conventional $d_{x^2-y^2}/d_{xy}$ character, producing narrow bands at commensurate filling. Dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) calculation reveals a selective band-renormalization of orbitals from the two Cu ions with Cu-1 undergoing a Mott transition while Cu-2 remaining metallic under electronic correlations. Crucially, FLEX calculations demonstrate that multiple magnetic instabilities compete with nearly equal strength: the spin susceptibility lacks dominant peaks, and the leading eigenvalues approach unity simultaneously across all wavevectors with increasing interaction. This competitive interplay, originating from the distinct local environments and geometric frustration on the triangular lattice, agrees well with the absence of long-range magnetic order in experiment. Our results suggest Y$_{3}$Cu$_{2}$Sb$_{3}$O$_{14}$ as a promising QSL candidate where the unique combination of disparate crystal-field environments, strong correlations, and competing exchange interactions conspire to stabilize an exotic quantum ground state.

Abstract: This thesis investigates the magnetic, spectral, and transport properties of strongly correlated electronic systems, with a primary focus on the Hubbard model and its extensions relevant for real materials. Within the dynamical mean-field theory (DMFT) framework, different regimes of interaction strength, temperature, doping, and magnetic field are explored, highlighting the central role of local electronic correlations in shaping spectral reconstruction and nontrivial transport responses.

A minimal, purely correlation-driven mechanism for generating spin-polarized charge transport in structurally conventional collinear antiferromagnets is identified, controlled by the simultaneous breaking of particle--hole symmetry and antiferromagnetic sublattice equivalence.
  Finally, these concepts are applied to correlated materials with strong spin--orbit coupling, such as Sr$_2$IrO$_4$ and Sr$_3$Ir$_2$O$_7$, and to nanoparticle solids dominated by Coulomb blockade and disorder. ### [77] [Toward bootstrapping tensor-network contractions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17856)
*Seishiro Ono,Yanbai Zhang,Hoi Chun Po*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于数值自举（numerical bootstrap）的张量网络收缩框架，将张量网络收缩问题转化为凸优化问题，为物理可观测量期望值提供经过认证的上下界。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有张量网络收缩方法通常依赖近似方案，且无法提供经过认证的误差范围。在多维张量网络收缩中，这一问题尤为突出，而准确收缩对于量子多体物理等领域至关重要。

Method: 引入数值自举框架，将张量网络收缩问题转化为凸优化问题。对于平移不变矩阵乘积态（translationally invariant matrix product states），在正则形式（canonical form）假设下，采用二阶锥松弛（second-order-cone relaxation）构建约束；当放宽正则形式要求时，采用更一般的半定规划（semidefinite-programming）方法。

Result: 在正则形式假设下，二阶锥松弛能够为收缩结果提供紧致的上下界。当放宽正则形式要求时，半定规划方法虽然计算成本更高（但仍为多项式复杂度），同样能产生类似的紧致边界。

Conclusion: 数值自举方法为张量网络的严格收缩提供了一条可行的前进路径，能够为物理可观测量期望值提供经过认证的误差范围，这对于量子多体物理等领域的精确计算具有重要意义。

Abstract: Accurate contraction of tensor networks beyond one dimension is essential in various fields including quantum many-body physics. Existing approaches typically rely on approximate contraction schemes and do not provide certified error bars. We introduce a numerical bootstrap framework which casts the problem of tensor-network contractions into a convex optimization problem, thereby yielding certified lower and upper bounds on expectation values of physical observables. As a proof-of-principle, we construct such constraints explicitly for translationally invariant matrix product states and demonstrate that, assuming a canonical form, second-order-cone relaxation can provide tight bounds on the contraction result. We further demonstrate that when the requirement on canonical form is lifted, a more general semidefinite-programming approach could yield similar tight bounds at higher but still polynomial computational cost. Our work suggests numerical bootstrap could be a possible way forward for the rigorous contractions of tensor networks.

</details>


### [78] [Non-Fermi-liquid behaviour of electrons coupled to gauge phonons](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17937)
*Rutvij Gholap,Alexey Ermakov,Alexander Kazantsev,Mohammad Saeed Bahramy,Marco Polini,Alessandro Principi*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究提出过阻尼规范声子（overdamped gauge phonons）是狄拉克材料中非费米液体行为的新微观机制，无需量子临界点即可实现横向规范场机制的晶格类比，为扭曲双层石墨烯等系统中的反常金属行为提供了新解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探索狄拉克材料中非费米液体行为的新微观机制，特别是寻找不依赖于量子临界点的替代途径。传统机制通常需要接近量子临界点，而该工作试图通过晶格振动（声子）与电子电流的耦合来提供新的解释框架。

Method: 通过计算电子自能（electronic self-energy），采用经电子-声子相互作用修饰的声子传播子（phonon propagator）。分析低能行为由轨道磁化率（orbital susceptibility）χ和无量纲阻尼参数α控制，特别关注过阻尼区域（α >> 1）的物理特性。

Result: 在过阻尼区域，准粒子（quasiparticles）表现出强烈的非费米液体行为偏离。当χ > 0时，费米液体行为仅存在于参数上狭窄的红外窗口，随后过渡到非费米液体标度行为；当χ < 0时，最低能标下费米液体区域被边际费米液体（marginal-Fermi-liquid）行为取代，随后也过渡到非费米液体标度。

Conclusion: 应变诱导的规范声子（strain-induced gauge phonons）是扭曲双层石墨烯等系统中反常金属行为的有前景来源，为理解非费米液体物理提供了不依赖于量子临界点的新微观机制。

Abstract: We identify overdamped gauge phonons as a new microscopic route to non-Fermi-liquid behaviour in Dirac materials. These phonons couple to electronic currents rather than densities, thereby realising a lattice analogue of transverse gauge-field mechanisms without requiring proximity to a quantum critical point. By computing the electronic self-energy with a phonon propagator dressed by electron-phonon interactions, we show that the low-energy behaviour is controlled by the orbital susceptibility chi and a dimensionless damping parameter alpha. In the overdamped regime, alpha >> 1, quasiparticles display strong deviations from Fermi-liquid theory. For chi > 0, Fermi-liquid behaviour persists only in a parametrically narrow infrared window before crossing over to non-Fermi-liquid scaling. For chi < 0, the Fermi-liquid regime is replaced by marginal-Fermi-liquid behaviour at the lowest energies, followed by a crossover to non-Fermi-liquid scaling. These results establish strain- induced gauge phonons as a promising source of anomalous metallic behaviour in systems such as twisted bilayer graphene.

Here, we present an inverse method for reconstructing the abelian Berry curvature of a single band using angle-resolved measurements of the transverse conductance. ### [81] [Characterization of Deconvolution-Based PMT Waveform Reconstruction Under Large Charge Dynamic Range and Varying Scintillation Time Profiles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17556)
*Xingyi Lin,Jinghuan Xu,Yongbo Huang,Jingzhe Tang,Tianying Xiao,Yingke Li*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本研究探讨了基于解卷积（deconvolution）技术的算法在光电倍增管（PMT）波形重建中的可靠性，特别是在处理大电荷动态范围（0-200光电子）、不同闪烁时间轮廓以及μ子诱发大信号时的性能表现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 光电倍增管（PMT）作为中微子和暗物质探测中的光子传感器，其波形中提取的精确电荷和时间信息对事件重建至关重要。需要验证解卷积算法在处理复杂信号条件下的可靠性。

Method: 采用基于解卷积（deconvolution）技术的算法进行PMT波形重建，并利用蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟数据评估算法性能。研究重点考察算法在大电荷动态范围（0-200光电子）、不同闪烁时间轮廓（scintillation time profiles）以及μ子诱发大信号条件下的表现。

Result: 蒙特卡洛数据证实解卷积算法表现出相对稳定的重建性能：在各种欠冲（undershoots）和闪烁时间轮廓配置下，电荷重建的残余非线性（residual non-linearity）在0-200光电子范围内控制在约1%；算法能够有效处理μ子诱发的大信号。

Conclusion: 解卷积算法在复杂信号条件下具有可靠的PMT波形重建能力，电荷重建精度高且能处理大动态范围信号，适用于中微子和暗物质探测实验的数据处理需求。

Abstract: Photomultiplier tubes (PMTs) are widely used as photon sensors for neutrino and dark matter detection. Accurate charge and time information extracted from PMT waveforms is crucial for event reconstruction. An algorithm based on deconvolution technology was proposed and applied to the reconstruction of PMT waveforms. This study further investigated the reliability of the deconvolution algorithm when handling a large charge dynamic range (0-200 photoelectrons), varying scintillation time profiles, and muon-induced large signals. Monte Carlo data confirmed that the deconvolution algorithm exhibits relatively stable reconstruction performance: the residual non-linearity of charge reconstruction is controlled to approximately 1\% over the range of 0 to 200 photoelectrons for various configurations of undershoots and scintillation time profiles, and the algorithm is capable of handling muon-induced large signals.

</details>

### [82] [The cosmic shallows I: interaction of CMB photons in extended galaxy halos](https://arxiv.org/abs/2206.14217)
*Heliana E. Luparello,Ezequiel F. Boero,Marcelo Lares,Ariel G. Sánchez,Diego García Lambas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究通过交叉相关分析发现，邻近星系周围存在与宇宙微波背景辐射相关的显著前景信号，表现为温度径向分布的系统性降低，延伸至数个星系半径范围。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索宇宙微波背景辐射（cosmic microwave background, CMB）中与延伸星系晕相关的前景信号，这对于精确宇宙学研究至关重要，因为这些前景可能影响CMB数据的解释。

Method: 采用普朗克（Planck）和威尔金森微波各向异性探测器（WMAP）地图与2MRS星系目录的交叉相关分析，研究红移速度cz≤4500 km/s范围内邻近星系的平均温度径向分布。

Result: 研究发现邻近星系周围存在统计显著的约15μK系统性温度降低，延伸至数个星系半径；该效应在数十倍星系尺度内强烈依赖于星系形态类型，而在更大尺度上几乎与形态无关；更延伸的星系效应更强，且星系团簇对结果有重要影响。

Conclusion: 这些发现表明CMB地图中存在统计相关的前景信号，需要在详细宇宙学研究中予以考虑；同时，这些信号可用于探索明亮晚型星系周围的星系际介质，并支持多样化的天体物理分析。

Abstract: We report and analyse the presence of foregrounds in the cosmic microwave background (CMB) radiation associated to extended galactic halos. Using the cross correlation of Planck and WMAP maps and the 2MRS galaxy catalogue, we find that the mean temperature radial profiles around nearby galaxies at $cz\le 4500~\rm{km~s^{-1}}$ show a statistically significant systematic decrease of $\sim 15~μ\rm{K}$ extending up to several galaxy radii. This effect strongly depends on the galaxy morphological type at scales within several tens of times the galaxy size, becoming nearly independent of galaxy morphology at larger scales. The effect is significantly stronger for the more extended galaxies, with galaxy clustering having a large impact on the results. Our findings indicate the presence of statistically relevant foregrounds in the CMB maps that should be considered in detailed cosmological studies. Besides, we argue that these can be used to explore the intergalactic medium surrounding bright late-type galaxies and allow for diverse astrophysical analyses.

</details>


### [83] [A possible common explanation for several cosmic microwave background (CMB) anomalies: A strong impact of nearby galaxies on observed large-scale CMB fluctuations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2305.00268)
*Frode K. Hansen,Ezequiel F. Boero,Heliana E. Luparello,Diego Garcia Lambas*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: Luparello等人（2023）发现了一种新的宇宙微波背景（CMB）前景成分，表现为邻近大螺旋星系周围CMB温度的系统性降低。该前景成分与CMB异常现象存在显著相关性，可能影响宇宙学参数测量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在探究新发现的CMB前景成分对CMB涨落图的影响，特别是解释所谓的CMB异常现象（CMB anomalies）。这些异常包括大尺度模式（如四极矩、八极矩）的异常特征以及著名的CMB冷点（CMB cold spot）。

Method: 基于观测到的星系周围温度降低现象，研究者提出了一个通用的径向温度剖面（radial temperature profile）。将该剖面分配给红移范围$z=[0.004,0.02]$内的邻近星系，构建了一个前景图模型（foreground map model）。通过1000个模拟图的统计分析，评估该模型与Planck CMB图的相关性。

Result: 基于邻近星系构建的温度模型图与Planck CMB图显示出显著相似性。在1000个模拟图中，没有一个在大小角尺度上显示出如此强的相关性。四极矩（quadrupole）、八极矩（octopole）以及$\ell=4$和$\ell=5$模式与前景图高度相关。前景图中一个最显著的温度降低区与CMB冷点位置重合。

Conclusion: CMB的最大尺度特征以及由此推导的宇宙学参数，在对此前景成分进行适当校正后可能发生重要变化。然而，只有在提出并测试合适的物理机制后，才能获得可靠的校正CMB图。

Abstract: In Luparello et al. 2023, a new and hitherto unknown CMB foreground was detected. A systematic decrease in Cosmic Microwave Background (CMB) temperatures around nearby large spiral galaxies points to an unknown interaction with CMB photons in a sphere up to several projected Mpc around these galaxies. We investigate to which extent this foreground may impact the CMB fluctuations map and create the so-called CMB anomalies. Using the observed temperature decrements around the galaxies, and making some general assumptions about the unknown interaction, we propose a common radial temperature profile. By assigning this profile to nearby galaxies in the redshift range $z=[0.004,0.02]$ we create a foreground map model. We find a remarkable resemblance between this temperature model map based on nearby galaxies and the Planck CMB map. Out of 1000 simulated maps, none of them show such a strong correlation with the foreground map over both large and small angular scales. In particular, the quadrupole, octopole, as well as $\ell=4$ and $\ell=5$ modes correlate with the foreground map to high significance. Furthermore, one of the most prominent temperature decrements in the foreground map coincides with the position of the CMB cold spot. The largest scales of the CMB and thereby the cosmological parameters, may have important changes after proper corrections of this foreground component. However, a reliable corrected CMB map can only be derived when suitable physical mechanisms are proposed and tested.

</details>


### [84] [The CMB Cold Spot as predicted by foregrounds around nearby galaxies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2310.13755)
*Diego Garcia Lambas,Frode K. Hansen,Facundo Toscano,Heliana E. Luparello,Ezequiel F. Boero*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了宇宙微波背景（CMB）中非高斯冷点（Cold Spot）的温度下降是否可由附近星系的前景效应解释。通过分析波江座超星系团等星系数据，发现该区域星系周围的温度下降显著强于天空其他部分，表明局部河外前景可能解释观测到的温度下降。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宇宙微波背景（CMB）中的非高斯冷点（Cold Spot, CS）及其周围热环是CMB最显著的特征之一。先前研究推测新物理或高红移宇宙空洞引起的ISW效应（integrated Sachs-Wolfe effect）可解释该现象，本文旨在探究附近星系系统性的CMB温度下降是否可能产生如此强烈的温度凹陷。

Method: 使用Planck SMICA地图和星系目录2MRS、6dF、HIPASS作为前景示踪物。应用平均温度剖面（mean temperature profiles）来建模冷点区域星系引起的温度下降，并分析波江座超星系团（Eridanus supergroup）及其邻近星系群的性质。

Result: 即使校正了冷点区域的平均低温，星系周围的温度下降仍显著强于天空其他部分的平均下降。研究发现冷点区域与最缺乏中性氢（HI deficient）星系的区域之一重合，且晚期型星系（late-type）过度丰富的大型星系群复合体产生了特别强的温度下降，其形状与CMB冷点高度重叠。

Conclusion: 冷点区域存在唯一的附近螺旋星系丰富星系群复合体，且建模成功，这为存在局部河外前景（local extragalactic foreground）提供了有力证据，该前景可解释观测到的温度下降，从而缓解与CMB预期高斯场（Gaussian field）的张力。

Abstract: The non-Gaussian Cold Spot (CS) surrounded by its hot ring is one of the most striking features of the CMB. It has been speculated that either new physics or ISW effect induced by the presence of a cosmic void at high redshift can account for the observations. Here we investigate if the systematic decrease in CMB temperature in the neighbourhood of nearby galaxies may create such a strong temperature depression. In particular, we note that the Eridanus supergroup and its neighbouring groups, is in the CS area. Our goal is to analyse observational galaxy data to characterise the neighbourhood of the CS, explore the properties of these galaxies and thereby make a prediction of the CMB temperature decrement in this region. We use the Planck SMICA maps and the galaxy catalogues 2MRS, 6dF and HIPASS as foreground tracers. We apply mean temperature profiles to model the temperature decrement from the galaxies in the CS area. Even after correcting for the mean low temperature of the CS region, we find that the temperature decrement around galaxies is significantly stronger than the mean decrement in other parts of the sky. We discuss whether this could be attributed to the fact that the CS area coincides with one of the regions populated by the most HI deficient galaxies. Modelling the foreground temperature profile, we find a particularly strong temperature decrement due to the presence of the late-type overabundant largest group complex in the nearby universe. A CS shape, which to a large degree overlaps with the CMB CS, is observed. We conclude that the coincidence of the only nearby spiral rich group complex located in the CS region, and the success of the modelling performed, adds strong evidence to the existence of a local extragalactic foreground which could account for the observed temperature depression, alleviating the tension with an otherwise Gaussian field expected in the CMB.

</details>


### [85] [What Shape is the Inflationary Bispectrum?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17004)
*Oliver H. E. Philcox*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究提出了一种直接从观测数据重建原初曲率扰动三阶关联函数形状函数S(x,y)的新方法，避免了传统上为每种形状构建专门估计器的计算负担。该方法应用于普朗克卫星的温度和偏振数据，实现了高分辨率形状测量，并用于探索大质量粒子交换等暴胀模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 暴胀期间的非线性相互作用会在原初曲率分布中产生非高斯性。许多理论具有标度不变性，导致三阶关联函数仅依赖于无量纲形状函数S(x,y)。传统方法需要为每种形状构建专门的估计器，并在宇宙微波背景数据集上应用，计算成本高昂。

Method: 研究采用不同方法，直接从观测数据重建S(x,y)，使用在原始空间中高效的对数分箱估计器（受模态程序启发）。该方法应用于普朗克卫星的温度和偏振图，获得覆盖完整(x,y)平面的高分辨率形状测量，包括挤压极限。

Result: 该方法接近最优，具有高度可解释性，对（最优分析的）标准模板的信息保留率约为10%。研究发现普朗克对约6个e折的非高斯演化敏感，峰值灵敏度在0.1h Mpc⁻¹附近。在形状空间中，数据和理论的比较可在毫秒级完成。

Conclusion: 该方法可用于探索广泛的标度不变模型，计算时间比直接估计器少几个数量级，为暴胀范式提供了新的探索方式。作为示例，研究使用精确自举方法计算了超过20,000个理论模板，对自旋二的分析显示最大显著性为2.6σ。

Abstract: Non-linear interactions during inflation generate non-Gaussianities in the distribution of primordial curvature. In many theories, the physics is scale-invariant, such that the induced three-point function depends solely on a dimensionless shape function $S(x,y)\sim k^6B_ζ(kx,ky,k)$. To confront such models with observations, one typically builds specialized estimators for each shape, then applies them to cosmic microwave background datasets at significant computational expense. In this Letter, we take a different approach, directly reconstructing $S(x,y)$ from observations using an efficient logarithmically-binned estimator in primordial-space (motivated by the modal program). Applying this to temperature and polarization maps from Planck, we obtain high-resolution shape measurements across the full $(x,y)$-plane, including squeezed limits. Our approach is close-to-optimal, highly interpretable, and preserves the information content on (optimally-analyzed) standard templates within $\approx 10\%$; moreover, we can use it to assess the scale-dependence of our constraints, finding that Planck is sensitive to $\approx 6$ $e$-folds of non-Gaussian evolution with a peak sensitivity around $0.1h\,\mathrm{Mpc}^{-1}$. Since we work directly in shape-space, data and theory can be compared in milliseconds. As an example, we perform a search for massive particle exchange using a suite of over $20\,000$ theoretical templates computed with exact bootstrap methods (for the first time) across a wide range of masses, spins, and sound-speeds; the spin-two analysis yields a maximum significance of $2.6σ$. Our approach can be used to probe a wide range of scale-invariant models in orders-of-magnitude less time than with direct estimators, allowing the inflationary paradigm to be explored in new ways.

</details>


### [86] [Natura Non Facit Saltum: An Analytical Model of Smooth Slow-Roll to Ultra-Slow-Roll Transition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17465)
*Diego Cruces,Minxi He,Shi Pi,Jianing Wang,Masahide Yamaguchi,Yuhang Zhu*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种实现慢滚（slow-roll）到超慢滚（ultra-slow-roll）平滑过渡的单场暴胀模型，通过修改Mukhanov-Sasaki方程的有效质量项获得完全解析解，并与尖锐过渡模型进行对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型在实现慢滚到超慢滚过渡时通常伴随第二个慢滚参数的急剧变化，本文旨在构建一个保持该参数平滑变化的模型，以更自然地描述暴胀过程。

Method: 通过最小化修改，在Mukhanov-Sasaki方程的有效质量项中引入简单的时间依赖性，从而构建单场暴胀模型，实现了背景演化和曲率扰动的完全解析求解。

Result: 获得了背景演化和曲率扰动的完全解析解，使得曲率功率谱的参数依赖性易于追踪；据作者所知，这是首个描述此类平滑过渡的解析模型，并与相应的尖锐过渡模型特征进行了对比。

Conclusion: 该模型成功实现了慢滚到超慢滚的平滑过渡，同时保持第二个慢滚参数在整个过程中平滑变化，为研究暴胀动力学提供了新的解析工具。

Abstract: In this letter, we propose a single-field inflation model that realizes a slow-roll-to-ultra-slow-roll transition while keeping the second slow-roll parameter smoothly varying throughout. The model is built through a minimal modification by introducing a simple time dependence in the effective mass term of the Mukhanov-Sasaki equation. We obtain fully analytical solutions for both the background evolution and the curvature perturbations, which makes the parameter dependence of the curvature power spectrum easy to track. To the best of our knowledge, this is the first analytical model that describes a smooth transition of this kind. We also compare its signatures with those of the corresponding sharp-transition counterpart.

### [87] [Tightening Cosmological Constraints Within and Beyond $Λ$CDM Using Gamma-Ray Bursts Calibrated with Type Ia Supernovae](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17500)
*Wei Hong,Luca Izzo,Massimo Della Valle,Orlando Luongo,Marco Muccino,Tong-Jie Zhang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种模型无关的方法，通过结合Pantheon+超新星数据、人工神经网络距离重建和两种伽马暴相关性（Amati和Combo），构建从低红移到高红移的距离阶梯，以约束ΛCDM和w0waCDM宇宙学参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 伽马暴（GRBs）能够探测到比Ia型超新星（SNe Ia）更高的红移，可将距离测量延伸至早期宇宙，但其作为距离指示器的应用受到经验光度关系校准中循环性问题的限制。

Method: 使用ReFANN从Pantheon+数据集重建光度距离dL(z)和距离模数μ(z)，通过近似贝叶斯计算拒绝法和风险函数优化超参数。这种模型无关的重建使用来自Fermi GBM和Swift-XRT的低红移（z<1）GRB样本来校准Amati和Combo关系，然后为z≥1的GRB提供距离估计，最后通过联合贝叶斯分析同时约束宇宙学和GRB相关参数。

Result: 从两种独立的GRB相关性获得了一致的宇宙学约束，哈勃常数H0与SNe Ia值一致（尽管可能受Pantheon+数据集影响），高红移GRB倾向于比Pantheon+更高的物质密度Ωm，并暗示可能的暗能量演化。

Conclusion: 本文提出了一个缓解GRB宇宙学循环性问题的框架，将距离阶梯扩展到z∼9，确立了GRB作为高红移探测工具的地位。

Abstract: Context. Gamma-ray bursts (GRBs) reach redshifts beyond Type Ia supernovae (SNe Ia) and can extend distance measurements into the early Universe, but their use as distance indicators is limited by the circularity problem in calibrating empirical luminosity relations. Aims. We present a model-independent methodology to overcome this circularity by combining Pantheon$+$ SNe Ia, a distance reconstruction based on artificial neural networks (ANNs), and two GRB correlations (Amati and Combo) into a distance ladder from low to high redshift, with the goal of constraining cosmological parameters in $Λ\mathrm{CDM}$ and $w_0 w_a \mathrm{CDM}$. Methods. We use the ReFANN to reconstruct the luminosity distance $d_L(z)$ and distance modulus $μ(z)$ from the Pantheon$+$ dataset, with hyperparameters optimized via approximate Bayesian computation rejection and a risk function. This model-independent reconstruction calibrates the Amati and Combo relations using a low-redshift ($z<1$) GRB sample from Fermi GBM and Swift-XRT. The calibrated relations then provide distance estimates for GRBs at $z \geq 1$. Finally, a joint Bayesian analysis simultaneously constrains the cosmological and GRB correlation parameters, ensuring self-consistent uncertainty propagation. Results. We obtain consistent cosmological constraints from two independent GRB correlations. The Hubble constant $H_0$ agrees with SNe Ia values, though potentially influenced by Pantheon$+$ dataset. High-redshift GRBs favour a higher matter density $Ω_m$ than the Pantheon$+$ and hint at possible dark energy evolution.Conclusions. We present a framework that mitigates GRB cosmology's circularity problem, extending the distance ladder to $z \sim 9$ and establishing GRBs as a high-redshift probe.

</details>


### [88] [Forecasting Sensitivity to Modified Dispersion Effects in Pulsar Timing Arrays](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17563)
*Jonathan Grée,Qiuyue Liang,Elisa G. M. Ferreira*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该研究利用脉冲星计时阵列（pulsar timing array）探测到的纳赫兹频段随机引力波背景（stochastic gravitational wave background），通过修正的张量模式色散关系（modified dispersion relation）来检验修正引力理论，并预测未来观测对相速度（phase velocity）偏差的探测灵敏度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 脉冲星计时阵列系统已探测到银河系内的纳赫兹频段随机引力波背景，这为检验修正引力理论提供了新机遇。研究旨在利用该观测数据探测引力波的修正色散关系，并预测未来几年内对特定偏差的测试灵敏度。

Method: 研究聚焦于张量模式的修正色散关系及其对计时残差互相关（timing residual cross-correlations）中重叠减少函数（overlap reduction function）的影响。采用Fisher分析进行全面的相速度不确定性预测，并通过模拟数据研究验证以考虑潜在的非高斯行为，同时考虑了样本方差效应。

Result: 研究提供了未来脉冲星计时阵列灵敏度的观测时间线预测：以3σ置信度探测到相对于光速10%或-1%的偏差，需要约30年的观测时间。相速度不确定性σ_v的预测结果已通过模拟数据验证。

Conclusion: 该研究建立了利用脉冲星计时阵列观测检验引力波色散关系修正的理论框架，并量化了未来探测灵敏度的时间需求。结果表明，对光速微小偏差的显著性探测需要长期观测积累，为修正引力理论的实验检验提供了具体的时间尺度预测。

Abstract: The pulsar timing array systems have reported a detection of a nanohertz-band stochastic gravitational wave background in our galaxy. It is of interest to use this observation to probe modified gravity and to forecast the sensitivity with which certain deviations can be tested in the coming years. In this paper, we focus on the modified dispersion relation of the tensor modes and its effect on the overlap reduction function of the timing residual cross-correlations. We perform a comprehensive forecast of the phase velocity uncertainty, $σ_v$, using a Fisher analysis validated by a mock-data study to account for potential non-Gaussian behavior. We also take into account the sample variance effect and provide an observational timeline for future PTA sensitivity: detecting a $10\%$ or $-1\%$ deviation from the speed of light at the $3σ$ level requires $\mathcal{O}(30)$ years of observations.

</details>


### [89] [Inflation with the Gauss-Bonnet term in the Palatini formulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17742)
*Ali Hassan,Syksy Rasanen*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 在Palatini表述下研究高斯-博内项与暴胀子的耦合，发现其与度量表述不同，不总是全导数项。通过精确求解或近似方法分析三种连接约束情况，发现暴胀子动能修正与陈-西蒙斯项形式相同但符号相反。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Palatini表述中高斯-博内项与暴胀子的耦合，因为与度量表述不同，该项在Palatini表述中不总是全导数项，这可能导致新的物理效应。

Method: 在Palatini表述中求解连接并将其代入作用量：对于空间平坦FLRW时空进行精确求解；对于一般时空使用梯度近似和阶数约化方法。考虑三种情况：无约束连接、零非度量性、零挠率。

Result: 所有情况下，暴胀子动能的主导阶修正与陈-西蒙斯项生成的形式相同但符号为负。引力波部分的修正也呈现类似模式，除可能的零挠率情况外，符号同样为负。在近似有效范围内，与度量表述的差异较小，除非动能项符号翻转或接近翻转。

Conclusion: Palatini表述中高斯-博内项与暴胀子的耦合产生与陈-西蒙斯项类似但符号相反的修正效应，与度量表述的差异通常较小，但在动能项符号翻转附近可能显著。

Abstract: We consider the Gauss-Bonnet term coupled to the inflaton in the Palatini formulation of gravity. Unlike in the metric formulation, the Gauss-Bonnet term is not always a total derivative. We solve for the connection and insert it into the action, exactly for the spatially flat FLRW spacetime, and using the gradient approximation and order reduction for a general spacetime. We consider three cases: when the connection is unconstrained, and when non-metricity or torsion is put to zero. In all cases, the leading order change to the inflaton kinetic has the same form as that generated by the Chern-Simons term, but a negative sign. The modification of the gravitational wave sector also has the same form as in the Chern-Simons case but with a negative sign, except possibly for zero torsion, depending on the coupling and the potential. Within the range of validity of our approximations, differences from the metric formulation are small unless the kinetic term flips sign or is close to doing so.

### [90] [Decay of correlations and zeros for the hard-core model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17858)
*Han Peters,Josias Reppekus,Guus Regts*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文证明了非常强空间混合（VSSM）条件可保证配分函数在参数λ附近无零点，但发现其密切相关的变体不具备此性质，同时VSSM也蕴含谱独立性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 先前研究已证明硬核模型配分函数在参数λ附近无复零点可推出强空间混合（strong spatial mixing），本文旨在探究其逆命题是否成立，即空间混合条件能否保证零点的缺失。

Method: 引入非常强空间混合（very strong spatial mixing, VSSM）这一强化概念，通过将问题转化为由Möbius变换诱导的非自治动力系统分析来证明主要结果。

Result: 主要结果表明，若图族在参数λ处满足VSSM，则每个图的配分函数在该参数附近无零点；同时发现VSSM的密切变体不能保证零点缺失，且VSSM蕴含谱独立性（spectral independence）。

Conclusion: VSSM条件足以保证配分函数的零点缺失性质，但并非所有空间混合的变体都具备此特性，这为理解空间混合与零点自由性之间的关系提供了新的理论框架。

Abstract: In a recent paper the last author proved that absence of complex zeros of the partition function of the hard-core model near a parameter $λ>0$ implies a form of correlation decay called strong spacial mixing. In this paper we investigate the reverse implication. We introduce a strengthening of strong spatial mixing that we call very strong spatial mixing (VSSM).
  Our main result is that if VSSM holds at a parameter $λ>0$ for a family of graphs, this implies that the partition function has no zeros near that parameter for each graph in the family. We also demonstrate that a closely related variant of very strong spatial mixing does not imply zero-freeness. As a consequence of our main result, we moreover obtain that VSSM implies spectral independence. Our proof relies on transforming the problem to the analysis of an induced non-autonomous dynamical system given by Möbius transformations.

</details>


### [91] [Gaussian concentration, integral probability metrics, and coupling functionals for infinite lattice systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17861)
*J. -R. Chazottes,P. Collet,F. Redig*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 该论文发展了一个用于无限乘积空间上高斯浓度不等式的输运-熵框架，证明了在有限体积下相关积分概率度量与耦合泛函的一致性，并建立了马尔顿耦合不等式与高斯浓度之间的等价关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 论文旨在为无限乘积空间 $S^{\mathbb Z^d}$ 上的高斯浓度不等式（Gaussian concentration inequalities）建立一个输运-熵框架（transport-entropy framework），其中敏感性由局部振荡的 $\ell^2$-范数度量。研究关注无限乘积空间中由于结构缺乏可扩展性导致的输运成本特性。

Method: 采用输运-熵框架，分析由局部振荡 $\ell^2$-范数定义的敏感性度量。证明在有限体积下，相关的积分概率度量（integral probability metric）与耦合泛函（coupling functional）的一致性，扩展了经典的康托罗维奇-鲁宾斯坦定理（Kantorovich-Rubinstein theorem）。在平移不变（translation-invariant）设置下，研究相应度量在热力学极限中的收敛行为。

Result: 主要结果表明，相关的输运成本无法由构型空间上的任何度量或成本函数诱导，这是无限乘积空间结构缺乏可扩展性的结果。在有限体积下，积分概率度量与耦合泛函的一致性建立了一个超越度量设置的对偶关系。马尔顿耦合不等式（Marton's coupling inequality）在所有有限体积中与高斯浓度等价，为无限乘积设置提供了新的表征。

Conclusion: 论文建立了一个输运-熵框架，将高斯浓度不等式与输运不等式联系起来。在平移不变设置下，相应度量收敛到 $\bar d$-度量。进一步引入了热力学高斯浓度界（thermodynamic Gaussian concentration bound），并证明了其与涉及相对熵密度（relative entropy density）的输运-熵不等式的等价性。

Abstract: We develop a transport-entropy framework for Gaussian concentration inequalities on the infinite product space $S^{\mathbb Z^d}$, where $S$ is a finite set, in which sensitivity is measured by the $\ell^2$-norm of local oscillations.
  We show that the associated transportation costs cannot be induced by any metric or cost function on the configuration space, due to a structural lack of extensivity in infinite product spaces.
  Our main result proves that the associated integral probability metric and coupling functional coincide in finite volume, yielding a duality extending the classical Kantorovich-Rubinstein theorem beyond the metric setting. As a consequence, Marton's coupling inequality in all finite volumes is equivalent to Gaussian concentration, yielding a new characterization in the infinite-product setting.
  In the translation-invariant setting, the corresponding metrics converge in the thermodynamic limit to the $\bar d$-metric. We further introduce a thermodynamic Gaussian concentration bound and prove its equivalence with a transport-entropy inequality involving the relative entropy density.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 研究未发现支持惰性中微子存在的证据，但为0.5-1.5 MeV质量范围内的活性-惰性混合概率设定了新的实验限制，特别是在0.7 MeV处获得了目前最严格的约束条件。

Abstract: Sterile neutrinos are well-motivated extensions of the Standard Model, introduced to address fundamental questions such as the origin of neutrino masses and the nature of dark matter. Exploiting the precise data reconstruction achieved by the CUPID-0 experiment, we searched for spectral distortions in the double $β$-decay of $^{82}$Se compatible with the emission of a sterile neutrino. The analysis relies on the construction of a detailed background model down to 200 keV, enabling an accurate characterization of the main sources of contamination. Using a Zn$^{82}$Se exposure of 9.95 kg$\cdot$yr, we explored sterile neutrino mass hypotheses between 0.5 MeV and 1.5 MeV. No evidence for a signal was observed in any scenario; therefore, we derived 90% C.I. upper limits on the active-sterile mixing probability $\sin^2θ$, obtaining the most stringent bound, $\sin^2θ<8\times 10^{-3}$, for a sterile neutrino mass of 0.7 MeV.

### [96] [Quantifying the Features of an Amorphous Solid's Local Yield Surface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16905)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Result: 大多数屈服特征可由结合Schmid-Mohr-Coulomb准则的参数化模型描述，参数包括弱面取向（weak-plane orientation）、临界应力（critical stress）和压力敏感性（pressure sensitivity）。屈服特征参数统计揭示了非晶态结构中编码的离散屈服特征群体如何控制塑性流动起始。

Conclusion: 塑性流动起始由非晶态结构中编码的离散屈服特征群体控制，这些特征可通过结合Schmid-Mohr-Coulomb准则的参数化模型有效描述，为理解非晶材料的屈服机制提供了微观基础。

Abstract: In two-dimensional Lennard-Jones glasses, mechanical probing reveals that local yield surfaces are dominated by regions with a positive second derivative of the yield stress with respect to the loading angle. Each feature corresponds to a shear transformation zone and a characteristic non-affine displacement field at yield. Most features are well described by a combined Schmid-Mohr-Coulomb criterion parameterized by a weak-plane orientation, a critical stress, and a pressure sensitivity. The resulting parameter statistics clarify how the onset of plastic flow is governed by the population of discrete yielding features encoded in the amorphous structure.

*Munkyun Lee*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 从几何角度探索多稳态折纸块稳定配置的设计方法，使其能够相互对齐和互锁；从力学角度探索刚度可控的设计方法，通过几何参数确保自支撑和承载能力。

Result: 未在摘要中明确说明具体结果，但研究旨在通过多稳态折纸与块组装的互补潜力，为建筑应用中的自支撑可展开系统提供有前景的解决方案。

Abstract: Origami, which transforms flat sheets into three-dimensional shapes through folding patterns, has inspired the emergence of deployable systems in architecture and civil realms. Most existing origami-inspired deployable systems are based on rigid or curved-crease origami types. However, they inherently lack shape stability and require additional supports to maintain their deployed shapes. These lead to a fundamental trade-off between deployability and shape stability, which remains a major challenge for large-scale origami systems. Multistable origami, in contrast, achieves energy stability across multiple configurations during deployment. This unique characteristic enables it to maintain stable shapes even under external loads. These properties allow multistable origami to achieve both shape stability and deployability, offering high potential for self-supporting deployable systems in architectural applications. However, realizing both large-scale and structurally stable systems using a single origami faces many practical constraints. To overcome these limitations, origami block assembly has emerged as an effective approach to form global systems. This approach enables flexibility in global geometry and mechanical behaviors while offering reconfigurability. These indicate that the complementary potential of multistable origami and block assemblies can provide a promising solution. This study aims to address the challenges of applying deployable origami to large-scale architectural systems by leveraging the potential of multistable origami as modular building blocks. From a geometric standpoint, we explore design methods for stable configurations of multistable origami blocks that can align and interlock with each other. From a mechanical standpoint, we explore stiffness-controllable design methods that ensure self-supporting and load-bearing capabilities through geometric parameters.

Motivation: 环氧聚合物（epoxy polymers）因其多功能特性被广泛应用，但机器学习应用受到复杂三维分子结构、多组分性质以及缺乏整理数据集的限制。现有研究主要局限于模拟数据、特定性能或狭窄组分范围。

Method: 开发了基于高斯过程回归的知识蒸馏（Gaussian Process Regression-based Knowledge Distillation, GPR-KD）框架，使用实验文献数据训练，涵盖9种树脂和40种固化剂。个体GPR模型作为教师模型捕捉非线性特征-性能关系，统一的神经网络学生模型同时学习所有性能的蒸馏知识。

Result: 该框架结合了GPR的可解释性和鲁棒性与深度学习的可扩展性和泛化能力。比较分析显示其预测精度优于传统机器学习模型。通过跨相关性能的信息共享，同时多性能预测进一步提高了准确性。

Conclusion: 所提出的框架能够加速具有定制性能的新型环氧聚合物设计，通过编码目标性能作为输入特征，学生模型利用跨性能相关性，从SMILES表示中提取的分子级描述符创建了物理信息模型。

Abstract: Epoxy polymers are widely used due to their multifunctional properties, but machine learning (ML) applications remain limited owing to their complex 3D molecular structure, multi-component nature, and lack of curated datasets. Existing ML studies are largely restricted to simulation data, specific properties, or narrow constituent ranges. To address these limitations, we developed an informed Gaussian Process Regression-based Knowledge Distillation (GPR-KD) framework for predicting multiple physical (glass transition temperature, density) and mechanical properties (elastic modulus, tensile strength, compressive strength, flexural strength, fracture energy, adhesive strength) of thermoset epoxy polymers. The model was trained on experimental literature data covering diverse monomer classes (9 resins, 40 hardeners). Individual GPR models serve as teacher models capturing nonlinear feature-property relationships, while a unified neural network student model learns distilled knowledge across all properties simultaneously. By encoding the target property as an input feature, the student model leverages cross-property correlations. Molecular-level descriptors extracted from SMILES representations using RDKit create a physics-informed model. The framework combines GPR interpretability and robustness with deep learning scalability and generalization. Comparative analysis demonstrates superior prediction accuracy over conventional ML models. Simultaneous multi-property prediction further improves accuracy through information sharing across correlated properties. The proposed framework enables accelerated design of novel epoxy polymers with tailored properties.
