### [99] [Hydrodynamic Modeling of Odd Nematic Elasticity in Liquid Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16977)
*Zeyang Mou,Haijie Ren,Ding Xu,Igor S. Aranson,Rui Zhang*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究将奇弹性（odd elasticity）概念推广至向列相弹性（nematic elasticity），通过复金兹堡-朗道方程（complex Ginzburg-Landau equation）描述二维向列相液晶（nematic liquid crystals），发现奇向列相弹性可导致畴壁自推进和点缺陷自旋等非互易动力学行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前奇弹性研究主要关注简单软固体，但许多软固体具有结构特征并可能展现向列相弹性或粘弹性。因此需要将奇弹性概念推广至向列相弹性体系，以探索结构软固体中的非互易力学行为。

Method: 通过将二维向列相液晶（nematic LCs）的控制方程重写为复金兹堡-朗道方程（complex Ginzburg-Landau equation），在向列相液晶的流体动力学模型中提出了奇向列相弹性项及其对应的应力项。

Result: 在奇向列相弹性体系中，畴壁（domain walls）变得自推进并伴随双向流动，点缺陷（point defects）能够自旋、发展螺旋模式并诱导涡流。缺陷对的相互作用展现出与活性向列相（active nematics）不同的丰富动力学行为。

Conclusion: 该研究发展了奇广义弹性（odd general elasticity）概念，可进一步推广至其他粘弹性材料，并为操纵向列相液晶中的拓扑缺陷（topological defects）提供了一种新方法。

Abstract: There is a recent interest in studying odd elasticity in soft solids. Current focus has been on simple solids. However, many soft solids are structured and can exhibit nematic elasticity or viscoelasticity. Here we generalize the concept of odd elasticity to nematic elasticity. By rewriting the governing equation for two-dimensional nematic liquid crystals (LCs) in terms of complex Ginzburg--Landau equation, we propose an odd nematic elastic term and its stress term in the hydrodynamic model of nematic LCs. The odd nematic elasticity can be physically interpreted as non-reciprocal interactions between neighboring directors. In odd nematics we find that domain walls become self-propelled and are accompanied by a bidirectional flow, and point defects can self-spin, develop a spiral pattern, and induce a vortical flow. Interactions of a pair of defects show rich dynamics that are distinct from those in active nematics. As such, we have developed an odd general elasticity, which can be further generalized to other viscoelastic materials, and proposed a novel way to manipulate topological defects in nematic LCs.

### [100] [Breakloose suppression in minimal friction models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17076)
*Shubham Agarwal*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了纳米尺度与宏观尺度摩擦系统中"breakloose friction"（起始滑动瞬态力峰）差异的物理机制，通过三种不同加载几何的最小摩擦模型揭示了其出现或抑制的多重物理根源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度接触中常出现显著的起始滑动瞬态力峰（breakloose friction），而宏观系统中该现象较弱或缺失。尽管通常将此行为与破裂前沿（rupture fronts）和过程区效应（process-zone effects）关联，但系统尺寸、温度、驱动速率和加载几何如何控制该力峰，以及其出现或抑制的物理机制仍不完全清楚。

Method: 采用三种具有不同加载几何的最小摩擦模型进行研究：多粒子Prandtl-Tomlinson系统（各粒子独立驱动）、端部驱动Frenkel-Kontorova链（应力沿界面弹性传递）以及均匀驱动FK链（各点局部耦合至驱动平台）。

Result: 相似的宏观起始滑动力峰抑制现象源于根本不同的物理机制：多粒子PT系统中，增大系统尺寸或温度促进局部脱钉事件（local depinning events）的统计失相（statistical dephasing），平滑全局响应；端部驱动FK链中，内部弹性沿界面重新分布应力，延迟滑动起始，并与更高温度或更慢驱动共同实现加载过程中的渐进松弛；均匀驱动FK链中，驱动弹簧刚度控制滑移事件的同步性，从而决定滑动响应特性。

Conclusion: 起始滑动力峰（breakloose peak）的存在与否并不唯一标识单一物理机制，而是反映了局部钉扎（local pinning）、弹性耦合（elastic coupling）和接触结构（contact architecture）三者之间的相互作用。

Abstract: Breakloose friction, the transient force peak at the onset of sliding, is often pronounced in nanoscale contacts but weak or absent in macroscopic systems. Although this behavior is commonly associated with rupture fronts and process-zone effects, how the stiction peak is controlled by system size, temperature, driving rate, and loading geometry, and what mechanisms underlie its emergence or suppression, remains incompletely understood. Here we investigate this problem using three minimal friction models with distinct loading geometries: a multi-particle Prandtl-Tomlinson system with independently driven particles, an end-driven Frenkel-Kontorova chain with elastic stress transmission along the interface, and a uniformly driven FK chain in which each site is coupled locally to the driving stage. We show that similar macroscopic suppression of breakloose friction can arise from fundamentally different mechanisms. In multi-particle PT systems, increasing system size or temperature promotes statistical dephasing of local depinning events, smoothing the global response. In end-driven FK chains, internal elasticity redistributes stress along the interface, delaying sliding onset and, together with higher temperature or slower driving, enabling progressive relaxation during loading. In uniformly-driven FK chains, the stiffness of the driving springs controls the synchronization of slip events and thereby the character of the sliding response. These results demonstrate that the presence or absence of a breakloose peak does not uniquely identify a single physical mechanism, but instead reflects the interplay of local pinning, elastic coupling, and contact architecture.

</details>


### [101] [Mesoscopic Modeling of Dynamic Tetra-PEG Hydrogel Networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17180)
*Pietro Miotti,Lucien Cousin,Mark W. Tibbitt,Igor V. Pivkin*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 动态聚合物网络（dynamic polymer networks）的合理设计需要理解大分子键合动力学（macromolecular bond kinetics）与宏观力学性质之间的关系，但实验方法难以直接测量网络拓扑结构参数如键分布、悬垂链分数和渗透簇尺寸。

Method: 采用混合耗散粒子动力学/蒙特卡洛（DPD/MC）方法构建介观模型，其中聚合物链用有限可扩展非线性弹性（FENE）势描述，可逆交联用莫尔斯（Morse）势建模，蒙特卡洛键交换过程由贝尔力依赖动力学（Bell's force-dependent kinetics）控制。

Result: 模型成功再现了网络的类麦克斯韦（Maxwell-like）粘弹性响应，弛豫时间遵循预期标度关系τ_R ∝ τ_b(p - p_gel)，模拟储能模量与实验流变学数据一致。基于图的拓扑分析可获取键分布、悬垂链分数和渗透簇尺寸等结构参数。

Conclusion: 该介观模型桥接了大分子键合动力学与宏观力学性质，为动态聚合物网络的合理设计提供了补充工具。与永久网络预测的比较表明，动态键交换会影响键分布并延迟系统跨越簇的形成。

Abstract: We introduce a mesoscopic model of dynamic Tetra-PEG hydrogel networks based on a hybrid Dissipative Particle Dynamics/Monte Carlo (DPD/MC) approach. Polymer chains are described by Finite Extensible Nonlinear Elastic (FENE) potential, while reversible cross-links are modeled with Morse potential and Monte Carlo bond exchange governed by Bell's force-dependent kinetics. After systematic calibration against theory and experiments, the model reproduces the characteristic Maxwell-like viscoelastic response of these networks. In particular, the relaxation time follows the expected scaling, $τ_R \propto τ_b (p - p_{\text{gel}})$, and the simulated storage moduli agree with experimental rheology. The mesoscopic resolution allows for graph-based topological analysis, where Tetra-PEG molecules and cross-links are represented as nodes and edges, providing access to bond distributions, fraction of dangling chains, and size of percolating clusters that are challenging to measure experimentally. Comparison with permanent-network predictions further suggests that dynamic bond exchange can affect bond distributions and delay the formation of a system-spanning cluster. This model bridges macromolecular bond kinetics and macroscopic mechanical properties, providing a complementary tool for rational design of dynamic polymer networks.

### [102] [Hexatic Order Coupled with Thermal Noise Produces Bubbles in Two-Dimensional Active Matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17320)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管自驱动纯排斥粒子诱导的相分离是研究最广泛的非平衡相变之一，但二维致密相中气泡的起源仍存在争议。现有解释包括奥斯特瓦尔德熟化（Ostwald ripening）过程逆转或六角畴边界拓扑缺陷等不同理论。

Method: 采用基于粒子的模拟方法，通过引入多分散性（polydispersity）来分离六角畴对气泡尺寸和数量分布的影响，从而明确不同因素在气泡形成中的作用。

Result: 研究发现六角序（hexatic order）是气泡形成的必要条件，但同时也需要热平移噪声（thermal translational noise）的存在。有趣的是，气泡形成所需的热噪声强度可以远小于粒子活性，但不能完全为零。

Conclusion: 热六角畴致密相中表现出的协同运动可能是气泡产生所必需的机制，这为理解二维活性粒子系统中气泡形成的微观机制提供了新见解。

Abstract: The phase separation of purely-repulsive particles induced by self-propulsion is among the most well-studied non-equilibrium phase transitions. However, some notable features of this transition remain open questions, including the origin of bubbles within the dense phase in two dimensions. Various explanations have been proposed, ranging from a reversal of the Ostwald ripening process to topological defects at the borders of hexatic domains. We present particle-based simulations that disentangle the effect of hexatic domains on the bubble size and number distribution through the introduction of polydispersity. While hexatic order is found to be necessary for bubble formation, we also identify thermal translational noise is required for bubble generation. Intriguingly, the magnitude of the thermal noise needed for bubble formation can be remarkably small in comparison with the particle activity but cannot be identically zero. The cooperative motion evidenced within the dense phase of the thermal hexatic domains may may be necessary for bubble production.

### [103] [Rapid Neural Network Prediction of Linear Block Copolymer Free Energies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17391)
*Ian Chen,Alfredo Alexander-Katz*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本研究开发了一个机器学习框架，用于从模拟衍生的能量描述符快速预测线性二嵌段共聚物（linear diblock copolymer）系统的过量自由能（excess free energies），避免了传统Bennett接受比（Bennett Acceptance Ratio, BAR）方法所需的大量中间模拟计算。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自由能是决定聚合物系统相行为和热力学稳定性的关键量，但传统Bennett接受比方法在计算大相互作用强度变化时的自由能需要大量中间模拟以维持足够的相空间重叠（phase-space overlap），计算成本高昂。

Method: 采用耗散粒子动力学（dissipative particle dynamics）模拟自由连接链聚合物，构建包含异质相互作用能、均质相互作用能和键合弹簧能等每链能量统计量的数据集，训练前馈神经网络（feed-forward neural networks）学习这些描述符与通过分层BAR程序计算的自由能之间的关系。

Result: 所得模型能准确复现参考自由能，涵盖多种链长、组成和密度范围，包括训练中未包含的聚合物结构。在直接BAR估计因相空间重叠差而不可靠的情况下，神经网络预测仍与参考值保持一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，基于物理信息的机器学习模型可作为昂贵自由能计算的高效替代方案，为加速聚合物系统的热力学分析提供了有前景的途径。

Abstract: Free energies are fundamental quantities governing phase behavior and thermodynamic stability in polymer systems, yet their accurate computation often requires extensive simulations and post-processing techniques such as the Bennett Acceptance Ratio (BAR). While BAR provides reliable estimates when applied between closely related thermodynamic states, evaluating free energies across large changes in interaction strength typically requires a sequence of intermediate simulations to maintain sufficient phase-space overlap, substantially increasing computational cost. In this work we develop a machine learning framework for rapidly predicting excess free energies of linear diblock copolymer systems from simulation-derived energetic descriptors. Using dissipative particle dynamics simulations of freely-jointed chain polymers, we construct a dataset of per-chain energetic statistics, including heterogeneous interaction energies, homogeneous interaction energies, and bonded spring energies, and train feed-forward neural networks to learn the relationship between these descriptors and free energies computed using a stratified BAR procedure. The resulting models accurately reproduce the reference free energies across a range of chain lengths, compositions, and densities, including polymer architectures held out from training. In regimes where direct, brute-force BAR estimates become unreliable due to poor phase-space overlap, the neural network predictions remain consistent with the reference values. These results demonstrate that physically informed machine learning models can serve as efficient surrogates for expensive free-energy calculations and provide a promising approach for accelerating thermodynamic analysis of polymer systems.

### [106] [Free-Energy Analysis of Bubble Nucleation on Electrocatalytic Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17486)

  <summary>Details</summary>

We find that the activation energy $ΔG_{max}$ decreases with increasing supersaturation $ζ$, following a power-law scaling of $ΔG_{max} \sim ζ^{-2}$, while the critical nucleus radius $R_c$ scales as $R_c\sim ζ^{-1}$. Our theoretical predictions for the critical nucleus radius of hydrogen, oxygen and nitrogen bubbles are in quantitative agreement with experimental measurements. Finally, we present a simple model that couples gas diffusion and electrochemical reaction kinetics to determine the maximum gas supersaturation at a given current density. Our results advance the fundamental understanding of bubble nucleation at catalyst surfaces and provide practical guidelines for catalyst layer design to improve the performance of electrolyzers.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 该机制为调控活性乳液（active emulsions）中的结构形成提供了一条最小化途径（minimal route），通过化学互转化和扩散差异实现了对液滴粗化的有效抑制。

Abstract: Phase separation in passive systems leads to uncontrolled droplet growth, limiting structural control in soft materials and cells. We identify a generic mechanism to arrest coarsening based on chemical interconversion between molecular species with different diffusivities. Sharp-interface theory and simulations show that when the faster-diffusing species becomes enriched inside droplets, composition gradients emerge that oppose mass influx. This transport asymmetry stabilizes droplet sizes even without interaction asymmetries, offering a minimal route to regulate structure formation in active emulsions.

Method: 实验中将粒子置于分为明暗两个区域的竞技场（arena），通过不同光照强度创建交替的亮区（高活性）和暗区（低活性），并改变光照模式的频率。同时扩展了先前提出的动力学模型（kinetic model）来解释观测到的现象。

Abstract: We present experiments on the collective dynamics of macroscopic photoactive self-propelled particles subjected to spatiotemporally varying excitation. The particles move within an arena divided into two regions with different illumination intensities, creating alternating bright (more active) and dark (less active) zones. Under such conditions, the system exhibits a robust migration from the more active region toward the less active region, demonstrating a strong response to external modulation. This response depends sensitively on the frequency of the illumination pattern: at low frequencies, particles follow the changing landscape, whereas at higher frequencies, the response diminishes. We show that this behavior arises from the interplay between the imposed excitation and the intrinsic dynamics of the particle clusters that form spontaneously. To explain these features, we extend a kinetic model previously introduced in [Phys. Rev. ### [110] [Non-equilibrium phase coexistence in conserved chemically active mixtures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17690)
*Florian Raßhofer,Erwin Frey*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究分析了化学活性混合物中，化学反应通过调控粒子输运而非改变热力学相互作用来影响相分离和粗化过程的机制。研究揭示了两种不同的相分离途径，并建立了化学驱动下相共存和粗化调控的动力学调控理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统研究主要关注化学反应通过改变分子间相互作用来影响相分离，而本研究探讨了一种新情景：化学反应调控粒子输运，同时保持热力学相互作用不变。这旨在建立化学活性混合物中相共存和粗化调控的最小且稳健机制。

Method: 研究采用线性稳定性分析（linear stability analysis）和有限元模拟（finite-element simulations）方法，分析不可压缩混合物中热力学相同但扩散系数不同的溶质在驱动化学反应下的行为。在快速化学转换极限下，建立了显式依赖动力学参数的有效自由能理论。

Result: 系统可通过两种不同途径相分离：当相互作用较弱时，通过广义质量重分布不稳定性形成模式并持续粗化；当相互作用有利于相分离时，化学活性可在致密区域内富集快速扩散溶质，从而抑制粗化。研究还发展了锐界面理论，预测了化学驱动下粗化抑制的起始、稳态液滴尺寸和成核条件。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，动力学调控是控制化学活性混合物中相共存和粗化过程的最小且稳健机制。在快速化学转换极限下，系统始终粗化，相共存由显式依赖动力学参数的有效自由能决定；超出此极限，锐界面理论可预测化学驱动下的粗化抑制行为。

Abstract: Chemical activity is known to affect phase coexistence and coarsening in liquid mixtures, most commonly through reaction-induced changes of intermolecular interactions. Here, we analyze a scenario in which chemical reactions regulate particle transport while leaving thermodynamic interactions unchanged. We study an incompressible mixture of thermodynamically identical solutes with unequal diffusivities that interconvert through driven chemical reactions. Using linear stability analysis and finite-element simulations, we show that the system can phase-separate into solute-rich and solute-poor domains via two qualitatively different pathways. When interactions are too weak to induce phase separation, patterns arise through a generalized mass-redistribution instability and coarsen uninterruptedly. When interactions favor phase separation, coarsening can be arrested if chemical activity locally enriches faster-diffusing solutes within dense domains. In the limit of fast chemical turnover, the system always coarsens, and phase coexistence is governed by an effective free energy that explicitly depends on kinetic parameters. Beyond this limit, we develop a sharp-interface theory that predicts the onset of arrested coarsening, stationary droplet sizes, and nucleation conditions under chemical driving. Taken together, our results establish kinetic regulation as a minimal and robust mechanism to control phase coexistence and coarsening in chemically active mixtures.

### [111] [Shear and bulk viscosities of water up to 1.6 GPa and anomaly in the structural relaxation time](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17793)
*Jan Eichler,Johannes Stefanski,José Martin Roca,Isabelle Daniel,Bruno Issenmann,Chantal Valeriani,Frédéric Caupin*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 该研究通过动态和非弹性光散射技术测量了水在高压（最高1.6 GPa）下的剪切和体积粘度，发现剪切粘度增长更快，导致两者比值下降两倍。研究揭示水的结构弛豫时间在约0.5 GPa处达到最小值约1 ps，这与氢键平衡时间相关，源于水的结构异常性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在地壳深处，压力超过大气压一千倍以上，水在这些条件下仍能流动，但其结构和流动性发生显著变化。研究高压下水的粘性行为对于理解地球深部水文过程具有重要意义。

Method: 采用动态和非弹性光散射（dynamic and inelastic light scattering）技术相结合的方法，同时测量水在不同压力下的剪切粘度（shear viscosity）和体积粘度（bulk viscosity）。研究压力范围从0到1.6 GPa，并通过模拟验证了观察到的趋势。

Result: 剪切粘度比体积粘度增长更快，导致两者比值从0到1.6 GPa下降两倍。水的结构弛豫时间（structural relaxation time τ）在约0.5 GPa处达到最小值约1 ps，这与氢键平衡时间相关。与其他液体不同，压力最初会加速水中的弛豫过程。

Conclusion: 结构弛豫时间的最小值源于水的结构异常性（structural anomaly），这种异常性允许水分子局部结构之间最快的相互转换，并产生一系列热力学和动力学异常现象。氢键平衡时间的解释为理解高压下水的行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: Deep in the Earth's crust, pressure exceeds one thousand times the atmospheric pressure. Water still flows under these conditions, but experiences dramatic changes in structure and fluidity. Using combined dynamic and inelastic light scattering techniques, we simultaneously measure the shear and bulk viscosities of water as a function of pressure. The former increases faster than the latter, so that their ratio shows a two-fold decrease from 0 to 1.6 GPa; we confirm this trend with simulations. We analyze our results in terms of the structural relaxation time $τ$. Contrary to other liquids, pressure initially accelerates relaxation in water. Our measurements reveal that $τ$ reaches a minimum close to 1 ps around 0.5 GPa. We interpret $τ$ as a the equilibration time of hydrogen bonds, and propose that the minimum in $τ$ arises from a structural anomaly which allows fastest interconversion between local structures in water, and generates a cascade of thermodynamic and dynamic anomalies.

Abstract: The control of active colloidal particles via optical traps is a cornerstone for research of matter at the micron and nanometer scale. A central challenge in this domain is the derivation of optimal transport protocols that minimize the mean work required to move a particle over a finite-time interval. Here we present a Ritz method in which open-loop protocols are constructed from a global basis of Chebyshev polynomials and optimised by a genetic algorithm. We apply the method to study optimal transport of an active particle, which is modelled as a force-dipole (or a stresslet) near a no-slip wall. The methodology is validated in the limits of zero activity and infinite wall separation, where it successfully recovers the known analytical protocols and the theoretical minimum work. Crucially, we demonstrate that the presence of the boundary breaks the time-reversal symmetry of the optimal protocol found in bulk solutions. This symmetry breaking is shown to be a complex function of the transport direction and the particle's intrinsic activity. Because the presented approach requires only the capability to simulate stochastic trajectories, it offers a robust, principled framework for optimizing transport protocols in complex fluid environments that remain inaccessible to exact analytical treatment.

Motivation: 研究旨在扩展抛物线反射器的设计空间，超越传统抛物面形状。探索更广泛的可展曲面类别对于理解复杂折叠系统的力学行为具有重要价值，特别是在生物折叠系统（如蠼螋翅膀的展开机制）的应用背景下。

Method: 采用离散化框架（discretized framework）构建网格，对应关键的可展曲面族（developable surfaces families），包括广义圆柱面（generalized cylinders）、切线可展曲面（tangent developables）和广义锥面（generalized cones）。同时考察了欧几里得（Euclidean）和非欧几里得（non-Euclidean）折痕模式。

Result: 研究证明在该抛物线反射器系统中，不同构型之间不存在等距变换（isometric transformation）。这一发现揭示了纯粹可展模型的基本局限性，并表明需要引入受控拉伸（controlled stretching）来实现构型间的转换。

Conclusion: 通过允许拉伸适应（stretch accommodation），可以实现不同构型之间的转换，这为建立广义的弯曲折痕拉伸理论（generalized theory of curved-crease stretching）奠定了基础。该框架在理解复杂生物折叠系统（如蠼螋翅膀的展开机制）方面具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We present a novel parabolic reflector system capable of generating a broader class of shapes beyond canonical parabolas. Using a discretized framework, we construct meshes corresponding to key families of developable surfaces, including generalized cylinders, tangent developables, and generalized cones. Both Euclidean and non-Euclidean crease patterns are examined, and we demonstrate that no isometric transformation exists between distinct configurations within this system. This result highlights a fundamental limitation of purely developable models and motivates the incorporation of controlled stretching. We propose that enabling stretch accommodation would allow transitions between configurations, laying the groundwork for a generalized theory of curved-crease stretching. Such a framework has potential applications in understanding complex biological folding systems, including the deployment mechanics of the earwig wing.

</details>

### [117] [Exploring the role of connectivity in disordered system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17447)
*Anjan Daimari,Shivanee Borah,Diana Thongjaomayum*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 该研究通过零温Glauber动力学分析广义Petersen图GP(N,k)上的随机场伊辛模型，发现尽管节点连接方式不同，但在配位数z=3固定的情况下，系统均无临界行为，强调了配位数比节点间连接方式更为关键。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究在配位数z=3固定的情况下，广义Petersen图GP(N,k)中不同的节点连接方式是否会影响系统对外场的响应。这一研究兴趣源于随机图和蜂窝晶格上的随机场伊辛模型在z≤3时均无临界行为的确切解。

Method: 采用零温下单自旋翻转Glauber动力学（single-spin-flip Glauber dynamics），比较系统在z=3随机图与不同连接参数k的广义Petersen图上的响应。同时探索有向GP(N,k)情况并与无向结果进行对比。

Result: 研究发现GP(N,k)上不存在临界行为，这突显了配位数相对于节点间变化连接方式的重要性。研究还比较了有向与无向GP(N,k)的结果。

Conclusion: 在配位数z=3固定的条件下，广义Petersen图中不同的节点连接方式不会导致临界行为的出现，表明配位数是决定系统响应的关键因素，而非节点间的具体连接结构。

Abstract: We study a minimal model of disordered systems, the random field Ising model (RFIM) on a generalized Petersen Graph, GP(N,k). This graph has a connected inner and outer loop, where both the loops consist of N nodes constituting a total of 2N nodes. The parameter k satisfies the condition 1<=k<=N/2, such that any site i in the inner loop has i-k and i+k as its two nearest neighbours, apart from its connection to a node on the outer loop. Thus, each node in GP(N,k) has coordination number z=3, and by varying k different connections between the nodes in the inner loop can be obtained. The objective is to study whether different connectivity between nodes in these graphs affects the system's response to an external field when the coordination number is fixed. This is of interest because critical behaviour is absent for z<=3 on a random graph which has been solved exactly as well as on the honeycomb lattice in the context of RFIM. Using single-spin-flip Glauber dynamics at zero temperature, we compare the system's response with the known case of a z=3 random graph and the generalized Petersen graph for various connectivity k, albeit for the same z. Our study finds the absence of critical behaviour on GP(N,k) highlighting the importance of coordination number over varying connectivity between the nodes. Additionally, we explore the case of directed GP(N,k) and compare it with the undirected GP(N,k) results.

</details>

### [118] [Attractor-Keyed Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17049)
*Natalia G. Berloff*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 该研究提出一种利用物理选择器（如激光器、伊辛机等）决策时产生的高维特征信号，通过线性解码器将选择与内存访问合并为单一事件的方法，从而消除稀疏路由架构中的提取操作，降低延迟和能耗。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 物理选择器（如激光器选择模式、伊辛机稳定于基态、凝聚体占据自旋态）在决策时刻会产生丰富的高维特征信号，这些信号通常比获胜者索引包含更多信息，但常规做法是将其丢弃。研究旨在利用这些被浪费的信号资源。

Method: 当特征信号在多次试验中具有可重复性（stereotyped）且在不同路径间线性独立时，通过校准数据构建单一线性解码器，将特征信号映射到任意有效载荷。该方法仅需对测量的设备响应进行一次奇异值分解（SVD），即可在任务选择前验证能力并限定最坏情况误差。

Result: 运行时误差可分解为两个独立可诊断的通道：解码保真度（由字典条件数σ_min(Φ)控制）和路由可靠性（由信噪比Δ/T_eff控制）。研究给出了完整的误差分解，提供了伊辛机选择器构造，并在三种测量模态的合成散斑特征模拟中验证了预测的标度关系。

Conclusion: 该方法将选择与内存访问合并为单一事件，消除了稀疏路由架构中占主导地位的提取操作。虽然尚无硬件演示，但研究提供了可证伪的四步实验协议。真实设备特征信号是否满足可重复性是核心开放问题。

Abstract: Physical selectors (lasers choosing a mode, Ising machines settling on a ground state, condensates occupying a spin state) produce high-dimensional signatures at the moment of decision: full field amplitudes, multimode interference patterns, or scattering responses. These signatures are richer than the winner's index, yet they are routinely discarded. We show that when the signatures are repeatable across trials (stereotyped) and linearly independent across routes, a single linear decoder compiled from calibration data maps them to arbitrary payloads, merging selection and memory access into one event and eliminating the fetch that dominates latency and energy in sparse routing architectures. The construction requires one SVD of measured device responses, which certifies capability and bounds worst-case error for any downstream payload before the task is chosen. Runtime error separates into two independently diagnosable channels, decoding fidelity (controlled by dictionary conditioning $σ_{\min}(Φ)$) and routing reliability (controlled by the margin-to-noise ratio $Δ/T_{\mathrm{eff}}$), each with a distinct physical origin and targeted remedy. We derive the full error decomposition, give Ising-machine selector constructions, and validate the predicted scalings on synthetic speckle-signature simulations across three measurement modalities. No hardware demonstration exists; we provide a falsifiable four-step experimental protocol specifying what a first experiment must measure. Whether real device signatures satisfy stereotypy is the central open question.

</details>


### [119] [Label-free quantitative imaging of two-dimensional concentration gradients using Fabry-Pérot interferometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17678)
*Taieesa Peshkovsky,Stefan Andreas Schmid,David Taylor,Robert W. Style,Lucio Isa,Federico Paratore*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: RIO（折射率观测器）是一种无标记干涉测量工具，用于微流控系统中折射率和浓度场的定量成像，通过法布里-珀罗微流控芯片实现约1×10⁻⁵ RIU的折射率精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微尺度浓度梯度在物理、化学和生物系统中具有核心作用，但由于浓度变化引起的光学对比度有限，其定量可视化仍然具有挑战性。

Method: RIO采用无标记干涉测量方法，基于安装在标准光学显微镜上的法布里-珀罗（Fabry-Pérot）微流控芯片，使用标准CMOS相机实现高灵敏度二维化学成像。

Result: RIO实现了每个像素约1×10⁻⁵折射率单位（RIU）的折射率精度，通过测量共层流中溶解NaCl的浓度梯度验证了其性能，展示了高时空分辨率的二维化学成像能力。

Conclusion: RIO为分子标记不可行或不理想的系统中微尺度浓度场的定量研究提供了可访问的无标记平台，适用于从聚合反应、酶促反应到细胞信号传导和电化学过程等多种非平衡现象的研究。

Abstract: Concentration gradients at the microscale play a central role in many physical, chemical, and biological systems, yet their quantitative visualization remains challenging due to the limited optical contrast associated with changes in concentration. Here, we present RIO (the Refractive Index Observer), a label-free interferometric tool for quantitative imaging of refractive index, and thus concentration fields in microfluidic systems. Implemented using a Fabry-Pérot microfluidic chip mounted on a standard optical microscope, RIO achieves a per-pixel refractive index precision on the order of $1\times 10^{-5}$ refractive index units (RIU) using a standard CMOS camera, enabling high sensitivity two-dimensional chemical imaging. We Characterize the refractive index resolution and spatiotemporal performance of the instrument and demonstrate its capabilities by measuring concentration gradients of dissolved NaCl in a co-laminar flow. RIO provides an accessible, label-free platform for quantitative studies of microscale concentration fields in systems where molecular labeling is undesirable or impractical, and enables investigations of a broad range of out-of-equilibrium phenomena, from polymerization and enzymatic reactions to cell signaling and electrochemical processes.

### [120] [False vacuum decay catalyzed by black hole in a heat bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17008)
*Bowen Hu,Kohei Kamada,Andrey Shkerin*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究了黑洞催化的假真空衰变，在二维膨胀子黑洞背景下分析标量场模型，探讨了从非平衡态（蒸发黑洞浸入不同温度热浴）的衰变过程，构建了小场激发下的隧穿解和大场激发下的随机激活机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究黑洞如何催化假真空衰变（false vacuum decay），特别关注辐射主导宇宙时期小原初黑洞（primordial black holes）诱导的真空衰变过程。通过二维膨胀子黑洞（dilaton black hole）背景下的标量场模型，模拟四维史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）的关键特征。

Method: 采用二维膨胀子黑洞背景下的标量场模型，该模型能重现四维史瓦西黑洞的许多特征，包括线性化场扰动的离心势垒（centrifugal barrier）。分析从非平衡态（蒸发黑洞浸入不同温度热浴）的衰变，构建小场激发下的隧穿解并计算衰变抑制。

Result: 解析构建了小场激发下的隧穿解并评估了衰变抑制，展示了在相应极限下如何简化为Hartle-Hawking（平衡）态和Unruh态的结果。对于大场激发，衰变通过随机激活（stochastic activation）进行，在模型参数特定区域找到了相关的非热sphaleron构型，并构建了描述隧穿到该sphaleron的半经典解。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解辐射主导宇宙时期小原初黑洞诱导的真空衰变提供了重要见解，揭示了黑洞催化假真空衰变的机制，包括平衡态和非平衡态下的不同衰变模式。

Abstract: We study false vacuum decay catalyzed by black holes. We consider a scalar field model with unstable potential in the background of a dilaton black hole in two dimensions. The model reproduces many features of the Schwarzschild black hole background in four dimensions, including the centrifugal barrier for linearized field perturbations. We study decays from the non-equilibrium state describing the evaporating black hole immersed in the thermal bath with a different temperature. We analytically construct the tunneling solution relevant at small field excitations and evaluate the decay suppression. We show how they reduce to those for the Hartle-Hawking (equilibrium) and Unruh states in the corresponding limits. For large field excitations the decay proceeds via stochastic activation; we find the relevant non-thermal sphaleron configuration in a certain region of parameters of the model and construct the semiclassical solution describing tunneling onto this sphaleron. Our results provide insights into the vacuum decay induced by small primordial black holes in the radiation-dominated era of the universe.

### [121] [The gravitational S-matrix from the path integral: asymptotic symmetries and soft theorems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17045)
*Jack Isen,Per Kraus,Ruben Monten,Richard M. Myers*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究将基于渐近边界条件路径积分的S矩阵表述扩展至引力理论，通过卡罗尔边界配分函数推导出BMS对称性对应的沃德恒等式，从而高效导出领头阶和次领头阶软引力子定理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在将先前发展的基于渐近边界条件路径积分的S矩阵表述扩展到引力理论，以建立边界配分函数与标准S矩阵元素之间的简单关系，并通过渐近对称性推导软引力子定理。

Method: 采用基于渐近边界条件的路径积分方法，定义卡罗尔边界配分函数（Carrollian boundary partition function），在扩展BMS变换（extended BMS transformations）的树图水平下发展该框架，并通过显式图计算验证特定项满足沃德恒等式。

Result: 渐近对称性下的不变性导出了边界关联函数满足的沃德恒等式，这些关联函数与标准S矩阵元素简单相关，从而高效推导出领头阶和次领头阶软引力子定理（leading and subleading soft graviton theorems）。

Conclusion: 在扩展BMS变换框架下，通过卡罗尔边界配分函数方法，可以系统地从渐近对称性推导软引力子定理，其中次领头阶软定理由庞加莱沃德恒等式与领头阶软定理共同确定。

Abstract: We extend a previously developed formulation of the S-matrix, based on a path integral with asymptotic boundary conditions, to include gravity. The path integral defines a Carrollian boundary partition function whose invariance under asymptotic symmetries implies Ward identities obeyed by the associated boundary correlators, which are simply related to standard S-matrix elements. We develop this in the context of extended BMS transformations at tree level. Modulo well-known subtleties associated with poles in the superrotations and corner terms, this leads to an efficient derivation of the leading and subleading soft graviton theorems from BMS symmetry. Our general arguments are verified by explicit diagrammatic computation of specific terms in the partition function, which are shown to satisfy the Ward identities. We also show how, in our context, the subleading soft theorem is fixed by Poincaré Ward identities together with the leading soft theorem.

</details>


### [122] [Kalb-Ramond Topological Term in Majorana Superspace and Kaluza-Klein Spectrum Deformation in Five Dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17262)
*L. A. S. Nunes,C. A. S. Almeida*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在五维超空间中构造了Kalb-Ramond拓扑项的超对称扩展，采用Majorana旋量坐标，揭示了在四维超空间导数处理中不可见的新贡献项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在构建五维超空间中Kalb-Ramond拓扑项的超对称扩展，特别针对具有挠率（torsion）的理论。现有基于四维超空间导数的处理方法无法捕捉到某些重要贡献项。

Method: 采用基于Majorana旋量坐标的N=1、D=5本征超空间形式体系，这是Linch、Luty和Phillips的N=1/2超空间的Majorana基实现。协变导数明确依赖于第五坐标导数。

Result: 该方法产生了两个在四维超空间导数处理中不可见的新贡献项——一个玻色项和一个费米项。费米项本身也是拓扑结构，保持了原始理论的背景无关性。首次在该框架中实现了完全超对称的Chern-Simons-like耦合。

Conclusion: 紧致化后，新的玻色项使Kalb-Ramond塔的整个Kaluza-Klein质量谱发生偏移，偏移量与拓扑耦合常数成正比。这一具体预测在纯玻色和伪超对称处理中均不存在，对Randall-Sundrum膜世界模型中的挠率现象学有直接影响。

Abstract: We construct the supersymmetric extension of the Kalb-Ramond topological term in an intrinsic $N=1$, $D=5$ superspace based on Majorana spinor coordinates. This formalism is a Majorana-basis implementation of the $N$=$1/2$ superspace of Linch, Luty and Phillips, and is particularly well suited to theories with torsion: the Majorana condition is the natural spinor structure in five dimensions, orbifold parity acts directly at the level of the Grassmann coordinate, and bulk matter couplings to the Kalb--Ramond field require no intermediate change of spinor basis. The covariant derivatives of the formalism carry an explicit dependence on the fifth-coordinate derivative, absent in the pseudo-supersymmetric approach of Klein. This generates two new contributions to the component action - one bosonic, one fermionic - that are invisible in any treatment based on four-dimensional superspace derivatives. We further show that the fermionic partner of the bosonic topological term is itself a topological structure, so that the supersymmetric extension preserves the background-independence of the original theory. The identification of the mixed Kalb-Ramond component with a gauge vector, implemented at the superfield level, yields a fully supersymmetric Chern-Simons-like coupling for the first time in this framework. Upon compactification, the new bosonic term shifts the entire Kaluza-Klein mass spectrum of the Kalb-Ramond tower by a factor proportional to the topological coupling constant - a concrete prediction absent in both the purely bosonic and pseudo-supersymmetric treatments, with direct implications for torsion phenomenology in Randall-Sundrum brane-world models.

</details>


### [123] [Finite-$N$ Bootstrap Constraints in Matrix and Tensor Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17364)
*Samuel Laliberte,Reiko Toriumi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探索了矩阵自举（matrix bootstrap）技术如何用于约束有限N下的矩阵和張量模型，以具有四次相互作用的Gaussian模型为例。研究发现矩阵模型的约束不显式依赖于N，而張量模型的约束则随N变化，允许对理论参数空间进行更广泛的扫描。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索矩阵自举技术如何约束有限N下的矩阵和張量模型，特别是理解约束条件如何依赖于模型维度N。这有助于揭示矩阵模型与張量模型在约束特性上的本质差异。

Method: 采用矩阵自举技术，以具有四次相互作用（quartic interaction）的Gaussian模型为例进行研究。通过分析Schwinger-Dyson方程的结构，比较矩阵模型和張量模型在有限N下的约束特性。

Result: 对于矩阵模型，约束不显式依赖于维度N，而是依赖于多迹期望值（multi-trace expectation values）的性质。对于張量模型，Schwinger-Dyson方程的结构允许约束随N变化，从而能够更广泛地扫描理论参数空间，并发现了作为四次耦合函数的两点函数（two-point function）的新约束。

Conclusion: 矩阵自举技术能够有效约束有限N下的矩阵和張量模型，但两者表现出不同的约束特性：矩阵模型的约束与N无关，而張量模型的约束随N变化，这为探索張量模型的参数空间提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: We explore how matrix bootstrap techniques can be used to constrain matrix and tensor models at finite $N$, where $N$ is the dimension of the matrix/tensor, taking a Gaussian model with a quartic interaction as example. For matrix models, we find further evidence that bounds do not depend explicitly on $N$, but rather on properties of multi-trace expectation values. For tensor models, the structure of the Schwinger-Dyson equations allow for bounds that vary as a function of $N$, admitting a broader scan of the parameter space of the theory. In the latter case, we find novel bounds on the two-point function as a function of the quartic coupling of the theory.

</details>


### [124] [W-algebras of the Deligne-Cvitanović Exceptional series and the minimal 3d ${\mathcal N}=4$ SCFT](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17394)
*Thomas Creutzig,Niklas Garner,Byeonggi Go,Heeyeon Kim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种三维场论构造，将中间李代数（intermediate Lie algebras）和相关的C₂-有限（C₂-cofinite）极小W-代数（minimal W-algebras）作为边界代数实现。该构造基于极小三维N=4超共形场论与拓扑场论的耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在为Deligne-Cvitanović（DC）系列中的中间李代数和相关C₂-有限极小W-代数提供统一的三维场论起源。这些顶点代数结构在数学物理中具有重要意义，需要寻找其物理实现。

Method: 采用极小三维N=4超共形场论与拓扑场论耦合的构造。对于与拓扑A-扭（A-twist）兼容的Neumann型边界条件，边界局域算符代数实现了极小W-代数。虽然该边界条件无法变形到B-扭，但全纯-拓扑（HT^B）扭转而实现了中间李代数的水平一仿射代数。

Result: Neumann型边界条件实现了极小W-代数W_{-h^∨/6}(𝔤,f_min)，而全纯-拓扑（HT^B）扭转则实现了中间李代数的水平一仿射代数。这为这些顶点代数结构提供了统一的三维场论起源。

Conclusion: 该三维场论构造成功地将中间李代数和相关C₂-有限极小W-代数作为边界代数实现，为这些顶点代数结构提供了统一的三维物理起源，连接了不同扭转变换下的代数实现。

Abstract: We propose a three-dimensional field theory construction that realizes the vertex algebras associated with the intermediate Lie algebras and the related $C_2$-cofinite minimal $W$-algebras of the Deligne-Cvitanović (DC) series as boundary algebras. The construction is based on the minimal three-dimensional ${\mathcal N}=4$ superconformal field theory coupled to a topological field theory. For a Neumann-type boundary condition compatible with the topological $A$-twist, the algebra of boundary local operators realizes the minimal $W$-algebra $W_{-h^\vee/6}(\mathfrak{g},f_{\text{min}})$. While this boundary condition is not deformable to the $B$-twist, we argue that a holomorphic-topological ($HT^B$) twist instead realizes the level-one affine algebras of the intermediate Lie algebras, providing a uniform three-dimensional origin for these vertex algebra structures.

</details>

The analytic structure of the supersymmetric zeta function, particularly its residue and special value, allows for the computation of the curvature-squared integral of the Sasaki-Einstein manifold and the subleading holographic anomaly. ### [126] [Multiway junction conditions: Jackiw-Teitelboim gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17695)
*Jia-Yin Shen*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该论文系统研究了由JT引力（JT gravity）主导的bulk时空通过共同界面粘合形成的booklet几何结构，完整求解了多路连接条件（multiway junction conditions），将膨胀子（dilaton）配置分为三种不等价类型，并确定了界面形状和膨胀子的显式形式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在系统探究booklet几何结构的性质，这种结构通过将多个bulk时空沿共同界面粘合并施加连接处的引力一致性条件而形成。论文专注于为JT引力主导的booklet提供多路连接条件的完整解。

Method: 通过构造膨胀子解空间的不变量，将所有膨胀子配置分类为三种不等价类型。利用连续等距变换（continuous isometric transformations）将每种类型固定为标准形式，有效消除冗余自由度。逐阶展开约束方程，并联合求解连接条件和连续性条件至次领头阶（subleading order）。

Result: 膨胀子配置被分类为具有吸引、排斥或中性行为的三种类型，每种类型由单一物理参数表征。研究发现，只有当足够数量的bulk携带吸引性膨胀子时，连接才被允许，这一条件由平衡条件（equilibrium condition）定量描述。论文进一步分析了不同膨胀子类型的所有可能组合，确定了界面形状及其上定义的膨胀子显式形式。

Conclusion: 该工作为JT引力主导的booklet结构提供了多路连接条件的完整解，通过系统分类膨胀子配置并消除冗余自由度，揭示了连接条件对膨胀子类型的约束关系，为理解此类几何结构的引力一致性条件提供了理论基础。

Abstract: A booklet is a geometric structure formed by gluing multiple bulk spacetimes along a common interface and imposing gravitational consistency conditions at the junction. We have systematically investigated the properties of booklet structures, constructed the booklet geometry, and derived the multiway junction conditions applicable at the interface. In this work, we provide a complete solution to the multiway junction conditions for booklets composed of bulks governed by JT gravity. By constructing invariants of the dilaton solution space, we classify all dilaton configurations into three inequivalent types, each exhibiting attractive, repulsive, or neutral behavior. Through continuous isometric transformations, each type is fixed to a standard form characterized by a single physical parameter, effectively eliminating redundant degrees of freedom. This process selects a distinguished class of Poincaré coordinates for each type. Expanding the constraint equations order by order breaks coordinate invariance beyond the leading and subleading orders. By jointly solving the junction and continuity conditions up to subleading order, we find that junctions are only allowed when a sufficient number of bulks carry attractive dilatons, as captured quantitatively by a equilibrium condition. We further analyze all possible combinations of different dilaton types and determine the shape of the interface along with the explicit form of the dilaton defined on it.

Abstract: We investigate a recently identified class of six-dimensional supergravities without tensor multiplets whose primitive BPS strings are described by a rational superconformal field theory. Rationality imposes severe constraints on the supersymmetric spectrum of their BPS strings and provides an effective way to study this class of models, despite the absence of a conventional geometric realization within F-theory. We find that, in each model, the rationality constraints are nontrivially satisfied and uniquely determine the elliptic genus of the strings, providing a new consistency criterion satisfied by this exotic class of candidate quantum gravity theories. In all cases, the left-moving Kac-Moody-Virasoro algebra on the string worldsheet is extended by higher-spin currents, corresponding to discrete symmetries of the 2d SCFT. This allows us to determine the global form of the six-dimensional gauge group for all the members of this class of models.

Abstract: We formulate a relativistic hydrodynamic theory for fluids with spin and intrinsic dilation charges. Linear mode analysis reveals a gapped dilation excitation and the freeze-out of long-wavelength sound modes, similar to the superhorizon modes in cosmology. In the nonrelativistic limit, the theory reduces to that of microstretch fluids. Upon coupling to electromagnetic field, we show that the scale anomaly permits additional contributions in the electric current, dilation current, and energy-momentum tensor. Our theory naturally applies to nearly conformal fluids undergoing rapid expansion or contraction.

### [131] [Asymptotics of superfluid Bjorken flow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17985)
*Alexander Soloviev,Michał Spaliński*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 该研究探讨了基于Mueller-Israel-Stewart理论耦合复标量场的膨胀超流体动力学，作为探索夸克-胶子等离子体手征相变的理论框架。研究发现渐近解可表示为包含$τ^{-a\ln τ}$因子的新型跨级数（transseries），描述了初始信息在耗散演化中的稀释过程。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在为膨胀夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）的手征相变（chiral phase transition）探索提供一个可处理的理论框架。通过研究超流体（superfluid）动力学，旨在理解重离子碰撞实验中可能观察到的物理现象。

Method: 采用Mueller-Israel-Stewart理论耦合具有自发破缺$U(1)$对称性的复标量场（complex scalar field）来模拟膨胀超流体。研究聚焦于Bjorken流（Bjorken flow）在晚固有时间（late proper-time）的行为，分析渐近解的形式。

Result: 发现渐近解可表示为新型跨级数形式，包含$τ^{-a\ln τ}$等因子。这些解描述了初始数据信息在耗散演化中的稀释，并保留了对对称性破缺相变（symmetry-breaking transition）的记忆。根据凝聚弛豫率（condensate relaxation rate），系统呈现两种不同的晚期行为：纯阻尼衰减或阻尼振荡。

Conclusion: 该分析的主要物理洞见是，此类阻尼振荡可能被印记在重离子碰撞实验（heavy ion collision experiments）的观测结果中。跨级数解揭示了系统如何保留对称性破缺相变的记忆，并展示了不同的晚期动力学行为。

Abstract: We consider the dynamics of an expanding superfluid modeled by Mueller-Israel-Stewart theory coupled to a complex scalar field with a $U(1)$ symmetry that is spontaneously broken. This is a manageable theoretical setting for explorations of the chiral phase transition of expanding quark-gluon plasma. We study the late proper-time behavior of Bjorken flow in this physical system and find that asymptotic solutions can be expressed as a transseries of a novel form, which contains factors like $τ^{-a\ln τ}$. This transseries describes how the information encoded in the initial data is diluted in the course of dissipative evolution. These solutions retain memory of the symmetry-breaking transition and describe two qualitatively different late-time behaviors of the dynamical variables, depending on condensate relaxation rate: either a purely damped fall-off or damped oscillations. The possibility that such oscillations could be imprinted in the observed outcomes of heavy ion collision experiments is the main physical insight that follows from our analysis.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: These lecture notes contain an introduction to quantum simulation of bosonic systems in the continuum, focusing on weakly interacting Bose-Bose mixtures with competing mean-field interactions. When the values of such interactions are fine-tuned to almost completely cancel the mean-field energy, quantum fluctuations become apparent and dominate the behavior of the system, stabilizing an ultradilute quantum liquid phase. An analogous situation appears in single-component dipolar quantum gases. We review the mechanism that gives rise to this exotic quantum liquid, which can form droplets that are self-bound in the absence of any external confinement, and discuss their properties and dynamics in both the mixture and the dipolar cases. In dipolar gases, arrays of dipolar droplets stabilized by quantum fluctuations can establish global phase coherence and form supersolids. In bosonic mixtures, supersolidity can emerge already at the mean-field level through spin-orbit coupling. We discuss the properties of such spin-orbit-coupled supersolids, comparing them to their dipolar counterparts. Specifically, we focus on their periodic density modulation, phase coherence, and peculiar excitation spectrum, which hosts both superfluid and crystal excitations. Finally, we conclude by discussing open research directions in the areas of quantum liquid droplets and spin-orbit-coupled supersolids, in particular at the interface of the two research topics.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: Linear limit continuation was recently developed as a systematic and effective method for constructing numerically exact solitary waves from their respective linear limits. In this work, we apply the technique to two typical anisotropic harmonic traps in two-dimensional Bose-Einstein condensates to further establish the method and also to find more solitary waves. Many wave patterns are identified in the near-linear regime and they are subsequently continued into the Thomas-Fermi regime, and then they are further continued into the isotropic trap if possible. Finally, the parametric connectivity of the pertinent solitary waves is also discussed.

### [134] [Unstable Slip in Fault Gouge Driven by Temperature and Water](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16921)
*Li Wang,Jie Meng,Dongpo Wang,Gongji Zhang,Helge Hellevang*

Main category: physics.geo-ph

TL;DR: 通过大规模分子动力学模拟研究温度对断层泥中石英-水界面摩擦的影响，发现摩擦系数随温度升高而线性下降，主要受界面水结构热演化控制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 断层泥中微观颗粒滑动是地震成核的基础，但温度如何通过界面水影响摩擦的机制尚不清楚。需要量化温度对摩擦强度、真实接触面积和水层结构的影响。

Method: 采用大规模分子动力学模拟（large-scale molecular dynamics simulations）研究亲水性石英-水-石英界面在300-500 K温度范围内的行为。分析温度相关的摩擦强度、真实接触面积和水层结构变化。

Result: 摩擦系数和摩擦力随温度升高单调下降，遵循近似线性关系μ∝T⁻¹和Ft∝A。加热破坏第一吸附层的氢键网络，降低吸附层密度，减弱径向分布峰，表明界面水从有序强吸附态向扩散弱束缚态转变。

Conclusion: 温度-水耦合条件下的摩擦稳定性主要由界面水结构的热演化控制。界面重构削弱了颗粒间桥接和结构内聚力，促进从结构锁定向水介导润滑的转变。

Abstract: Microscale granular sliding within fault gouge is fundamental to earthquake nucleation, yet the mechanism by which temperature affects friction through interfacial water remains poorly understood. Here, large-scale molecular dynamics simulations were conducted on a hydrophilic quartz-water-quartz interface over 300-500 K to quantify temperature-dependent changes in frictional strength, real contact area, and water-layer structure. Results show that both the friction coefficient and friction force decrease monotonically with increasing temperature, following near-linear relationships of $μ\propto T^{-1}$ and $F_t \propto A$, indicating that frictional weakening is primarily governed by temperature-driven contact restructuring. Structural analyses further show that heating progressively disrupts the hydrogen-bond network in the first adsorption layer, reduces adsorption-layer density, and weakens radial distribution peaks, demonstrating a transition of interfacial water from an ordered, strongly adsorbed state to a more diffuse, weakly bound configuration with delayering and quasi-phase-transition behavior. This interfacial reconstruction weakens intergranular bridging and structural cohesion, promoting a shift from structural locking to water-mediated lubrication. These results suggest that frictional stability under coupled temperature-water conditions is strongly controlled by the thermal evolution of interfacial water structure.

</details>

# cs.CR [[Back]](#toc)

### [135] [Synchronized DNA sources for unconditionally secure cryptography](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17149)
*Sandra Jaudou,Hélène Gasnier,Elias Boudjella,Marc Canève,Victoria Bloquert,Vasily Shenshin,Tilio Pilet,Sacha Gaucher,Soo Hyeon Kim,Philippe Gaborit,Gouenou Coatrieux,Matthieu Labousse,Anthony Genot,Yannick Rondelez*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于DNA的密码学原语，利用合成DNA的随机池作为同步熵源，实现远距离一次性密码本（OTP）加密的无条件安全通信。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 一次性密码本（One-Time Pad, OTP）虽被香农证明具有完美保密性，但需要分发与消息等长的随机密钥且仅能使用一次。传统方法难以实现远距离、大规模密钥的安全分发，这限制了无条件安全通信的实际应用。

Method: 该方法利用包含随机索引-载荷对的复制DNA分子作为共享秘密。通过本地测序和数字化处理，生成用于OTP加密的通用二进制掩码（binary mask），不依赖计算假设即可实现无条件安全。

Result: 实验在东京和巴黎之间演示了该协议，使用内部测序生成了约400 Mb的共享秘密掩码，残差错误率可达到通常的总体解密失败率2^{-128}。二进制掩码的最小熵（min-entropy）符合NIST SP 800-90B标准，与已批准的密码学随机数生成器相当。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了DNA作为远距离OTP的可扩展熵源，能够在敏感环境中实现高吞吐量安全通信。通过连接分子生物学和密码学，基于DNA的密钥分发为全球通信网络的无条件安全开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Secure communication is the cornerstone of modern infrastructures, yet achieving unconditional security -resistant to any computational attack- remains a fundamental challenge. The One-Time Pad (OTP), proven by Shannon to offer perfect secrecy, requires a shared random key as long as the message, used only once. However, distributing large keys over long distances has been impractical due to the lack of secure and scalable sharing options. Here, we introduce a DNA-based cryptographic primitive that leverages random pools of synthetic DNA to install a synchronized entropy source between distant parties. Our approach uses duplicated DNA molecules -comprising random index-payload pairs- as a shared secret. These molecules are locally sequenced and digitized to generate a common binary mask for OTP encryption, achieving unconditional security without relying on computational assumptions. We experimentally demonstrate this protocol between Tokyo and Paris, using in-house sequencing, generating a shared secret mask of $\sim$ 400 Mb with a residual error rate to achieve the usual overall decryption failure rate of $2^{-128}$. The min-entropy of the binary mask meets the most recent National Institute of Standards and Technology requirements (SP 800-90B), and is comparable to that of approved cryptographic random number generators. Critically, our system can resist two types of adversarial interference through molecular copy-number statistics, providing an additional layer of security reminiscent of Quantum Key Distribution, but without distance limitations. This work establishes DNA as a scalable entropy source for long-distance OTP, enabling high-throughput and secure communications in sensitive contexts. By bridging molecular biology and cryptography, DNA-based key distribution opens a promising new route toward unconditional security in global communication networks.

</details>

Abstract: Over the last seventy years, many Finsler-type geometric and modified gravity theories have been elaborated. ### [137] [On the conservation of specific energy and entropy in infinite anharmonic systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17338)
*Gaia Pozzoli,Renaud Raquépas*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有无界经典自旋（unbounded classical spins）的无限、封闭、平移不变、有限范围晶格系统（即非谐晶体），在钉扎（pinning）主导相互作用的条件下，证明了比能量（specific energy）和比熵（specific entropy）在时间演化下的守恒性，并讨论了它们与趋近热平衡的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用与Lanford、Lebowitz和Lieb（1977）相近的假设条件，研究无限、封闭、平移不变、有限范围的晶格系统。关键假设包括钉扎（pinning）主导相互作用，这确保了系统的稳定性。

Result: 证明了在时间演化下，比能量（specific energy）和比熵（specific entropy）的守恒性。同时讨论了这些守恒量与系统趋近热平衡（thermal equilibrium）之间的关系，类似于量子自旋系统中的已知结果。

Conclusion: 该研究成功地将量子自旋系统理论中的守恒性和热平衡结果，推广到具有无界经典自旋的经典晶格系统，表明尽管困难来源不同（无界性 vs. 非对易性），但两类系统在热力学行为上存在深刻的相似性。

Abstract: We work with infinite, closed, translation-invariant, finite-range lattice systems with "unbounded classical spins", also known as anharmonic crystals, under assumptions close to those used by Lanford, Lebowitz and Lieb (J. Stat. Phys., 1977); among other conditions, the pinning dominates the interaction. In this context, we prove conservation of the specific energy and specific entropy under the time evolution, and we discuss their relation to approach to thermal equilibrium, paralleling known results in the theory of quantum spin systems, where noncommutativity, as opposed to lack of compactness, is the main source of difficulties.

### [138] [Generalized Snell's laws for rough interfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17488)
*Christophe Gomez,Knut Sølna*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了具有一般混合特性的快速振荡粗糙界面的波反射与透射问题。通过渐近分析，精确表征了反射场和透射场的镜面反射（specular）与散斑（speckle）分量，并建立了广义斯涅尔定律（generalized Snell's laws）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于分析快速振荡粗糙界面对波的反射与透射特性，特别是当界面波动幅度与中心波长处于同一量级时的临界尺度情况。该研究旨在理解粗糙界面在不同相关长度尺度下产生的镜面反射和散斑分量的形成机制。

Method: 采用基于尺度分离的渐近分析方法，对应傍轴（paraxial）或抛物线尺度体系。考虑临界尺度界面，其中界面波动幅度与中心波长处于同一量级，并分析不同相关长度（correlation length）与波束宽度（beam width）的相对关系对波场的影响。

Result: 当界面相关长度与波束宽度相当时，反射波和透射波中出现随机镜面分量，但无散斑分量。当相关长度小于波束宽度时，出现镜面均匀化（specular homogenization）机制，粗糙界面可近似为有效平坦界面，产生确定性镜面反射和透射锥，同时出现包含镜面锥的更宽散斑锥（speckle cones）。研究提供了散斑图案的两点相关函数，并建立了中心极限定理类型的结果，表明它们可建模为高斯随机场。

Conclusion: 研究结论表明，通过分析镜面反射和散斑分量的形成机制，能够建立依赖于界面有效散射算子的广义斯涅尔反射与透射定律（generalized Snell's laws of reflection and transmission）。这些结果精确表征了粗糙界面对波传播的影响，为理解复杂界面散射问题提供了理论框架。

Abstract: In this paper, we consider the reflection and transmission problem of waves by a rapidly oscillating rough interface that exhibits general mixing properties. Using an asymptotic analysis based on a separation of scales, corresponding to a paraxial (parabolic) scaling regime, we precisely characterize the specular and speckle (diffusive) components of the reflected and transmitted fields. A critically scaled interface is considered, in the sense that the amplitudes of the interface fluctuations and the central wavelength are of the same order. When the correlation length of the interface fluctuations is of the same order as the beam width, random specular components arise in both the reflected and transmitted waves, while no speckle component is observed. Equivalently, the reflected and transmitted fields are essentially confined to the cones formed by the specular components (specular cones) with directions given by the classical Snell's law of reflection and refraction. When the correlation length is smaller than the beam width, a specular homogenization regime emerges. In this case, the rough interface can be approximated by an effective flat interface, yielding deterministic specular reflected and transmitted cones. However, broader cones containing the specular cones appear, within which the wavefields form speckle patterns (speckle cones) whose total energy is of leading order. We provide the two-point correlation functions of these speckle patterns and establish a central-limit-theorem-type result, showing that they can be modeled as Gaussian random fields. These results enable the identification of generalized Snell's laws of reflection and transmission, which depend on an effective scattering operator at the interface.

</details>

*A. I. Komech,E. A. Kopylova*

TL;DR: 该文研究了量子化单模Maxwell场与二能级分子耦合的阻尼驱动Jaynes-Cummings模型，构建了在非正耗散算符和时不变泵浦条件下的收缩动力学半群，并证明了量子光学基本耗散算符的非正性。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本文旨在处理量子化单模Maxwell场与二能级分子耦合的阻尼驱动Jaynes-Cummings模型，考虑一类在产生和湮灭算符中为多项式的广泛阻尼和泵浦类别。

Method: 研究采用构造Hilbert-Schmidt算符空间中的收缩动力学半群（contraction dynamical semigroup）方法，针对非正耗散算符（nonpositive dissipation operator）和时不变泵浦（time-independent pumping）条件。

Result: 主要结果是成功构建了Hermitian Hilbert-Schmidt算符Hilbert空间中的收缩动力学半群，该半群的所有轨迹都是Jaynes-Cummings方程的广义解。作为关键示例，证明了量子光学基本耗散算符的非正性。

Abstract: The article addresses the damped driven Jaynes-Cummings for quantised one-mode Maxwell field coupled to a two-level molecule. We consider a broad class of damping and pumping which are polynomial in the creation and annihilation operators.

All trajectories of the semigroup are generalised solutions to the Jaynes-Cummings equations. As a key example, we prove nonpositivity for the basic dissipation operator of Quantum Optics.

Extension to lower dimensionality fails, as it should, by observing the the triviality theorems used in our proof are not applicable in such cases.

Result: 得到两类解：一类导致场方程成为克莱因-戈登方程（Klein-Gordon equation）的推广，另一类导致典型的非线性无质量解。在平直时空下，该形式恢复了Plebanski模型族和Bopp-Podolsky电动力学作为特定极限。

Conclusion: 这些扩展可能在极端环境中具有现象学意义，如早期宇宙或带电致密天体附近，在这些区域可能探测到与经典电动力学的偏差。

Abstract: Within the general framework of $f(R)$ gravity, we introduce a function of the electromagnetic curvature invariant $f(\mathbb{F})$ that couples minimally to gravitation to ensure a consistent treatment of curvature functions in these theories. We show that one of the solutions leads to field equations that are a generalization of the Klein-Gordon equation while the other leads to a typically non-linear massless solution. Focusing on flat spacetime, our formalism recovers the Plebanski family of models and Bopp-Podolsky electrodynamics as specific limits. These extensions may have phenomenological consequences in extreme environments, such as the early universe or near charged compact objects, where deviations from classical electrodynamics might be probed.

### [143] [The imitation game (r)evolutions: $Q$-star effective shadow from GRMHD analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16995)
*Víctor Jaramillo,Laura Meneses,Héctor R. Olivares Sánchez,Carlos Herdeiro,Darío Núñez,Shuang-Yong Zhou*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文证明稳定Q星（Q-stars）的类时圆形测地线角速度可在非零半径处达到最大值，导致有效阴影形成，使其成为黑洞模拟体（black hole mimickers）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究Q星作为黑洞模拟体的潜力，特别是验证稳定Q星能否产生有效阴影，这一特性此前仅在非稳定解中被研究过。

Method: 对代表性稳定Q星模型进行广义相对论磁流体动力学演化模拟，并采用启发式分析评估有效阴影尺寸。

Result: 稳定Q星确实形成了低密度、低亮度的中心区域（有效阴影），其尺寸与同等质量的史瓦西黑洞相当，且该机制不依赖于超致密性或特殊选择的吸积盘。

Conclusion: 稳定玻色子星家族可作为有效的黑洞模拟体，其有效阴影形成机制具有普遍性，为黑洞替代模型提供了新的可能性。

Abstract: $Q$-stars are a class of boson stars arising in scalar-field theories with interacting potentials, minimally coupled to gravity. We show that, in certain regions of parameter space, the angular velocity of stable timelike circular geodesics around $Q$-stars can attain a maximum at a nonzero radius. Notably, this behaviour may occur for stable configurations. This feature has been argued to produce effective shadows, but so far it has only been investigated for unstable solutions. We test this possibility by performing general relativistic magnetohydrodynamic evolutions for a representative stable $Q$-star model. A low-density, low-luminosity central region is indeed observed to form and persist -- at least until the evolution becomes affected by numerical viscosity. As a proof of principle, this suggests that families of stable bosonic stars can act as black hole mimickers. Moreover, for the model at hand, a heuristic analysis shows that the effective shadow has a comparable size to that of a Schwarzschild black hole with the same mass. Importantly, this mechanism for generating an effective shadow does not rely on the object being ultracompact, or an ad hoc chosen accretion disk.

</details>


### [144] [The Structure of the Continuum Limit of Spin Foams](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16999)
*Matteo Bruno,Eugenia Colafranceschi,Fabio M. Mele,Carlo Rovelli*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究为自旋泡沫（spin foam）量子引力理论建立了独立于具体模型的公理化框架，分析了其连续极限（continuum limit）的结构特性。研究发现强收敛概念必然导致拓扑理论，而通过分布意义（distributional sense）的弱收敛可以构造物理希尔伯特空间（physical Hilbert space），从而为引力路径积分提供精确的物理表述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自旋泡沫（spin foam）方法旨在为规范圈量子引力（canonical Loop Quantum Gravity）提供协变的路径积分表述。由于自旋泡沫振幅通过时空离散化定义，理解理论的连续极限（continuum limit）是该领域的核心开放问题。

Method: 研究引入了一个受阿蒂亚（Atiyah）拓扑量子场论（Topological Quantum Field Theories, TQFTs）启发的自旋泡沫振幅公理化框架。该框架将希尔伯特空间和振幅分配给与三角剖分流形相关的组合和拓扑数据，并通过在三角剖分集上配备合适的序关系，提供了连续极限的精确概念。

Result: 在自旋泡沫振幅收敛的自然假设下，研究建立了一个"不可能性"（no-go）结果：足够强的收敛概念必然导致拓扑理论。通过弱化收敛概念，在分布意义（distributional sense）下考虑连续极限，圆柱体（cylinder）相关的振幅定义了rigging map，从而构造了物理希尔伯特空间（physical Hilbert space）。

Conclusion: 所得连续振幅在物理态空间上作为良定义的分布（distributions）作用，以精确的意义将引力路径积分的这一表述特征化为物理理论。该研究为超越拓扑量子场论（TQFTs）的连续极限提供了系统分析框架。

Abstract: The Spin Foam approach to quantum gravity aims at providing a covariant path-integral formulation of canonical Loop Quantum Gravity. Since spin foam amplitudes are defined through discretisations of spacetime, understanding the continuum limit of the theory remains a central open problem. In this work, we investigate the structural aspects of this limit in a model-independent manner. We begin by introducing an axiomatic framework for spin foam amplitudes inspired by Atiyah's formulation of Topological Quantum Field Theories (TQFTs). In this setting, Hilbert spaces and amplitudes are assigned to combinatorial and topological data associated with triangulated manifolds. By equipping the set of triangulations with suitable orders, this framework provides a precise notion of continuum limit and allows us to analyse its properties independently of any specific model. We proceed then to systematically investigate how the specifics of the limit procedure allow to go beyond TQFT in the continuum. Under natural assumptions on the convergence of spin foam amplitudes, we establish a no-go result: sufficiently strong notions of convergence necessarily lead to a topological theory. Motivated by this obstruction, we weaken the notion of convergence and consider the continuum limit of spin foam amplitudes in a distributional sense, in the spirit of Refined Algebraic Quantisation. Under this assumption, the amplitude associated with the cylinder defines a rigging map, yielding a canonical construction of the physical Hilbert space. The resulting continuum amplitudes act as well-defined distributions on this space of physical states, characterising this formulation of the gravitational path integral as physical in a precise sense.

### [145] [The two shadows of a single black hole: Vacuum birefringence phenomena within Einstein-Nonlinear-Electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17007)
*Marco A. A. de Paula,Haroldo C. D. Lima,Pedro V. P. Cunha,Carlos A. R. Herdeiro,Luís C. B. Crispino*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 研究考虑了一个依赖于两个电磁标量不变量（electromagnetic scalar invariants）的NED模型，分析了光子在该模型中的传播特性。从时空度规（spacetime metric）观测者视角，将光子运动解释为受四力项（four-force term）作用的非测地线曲线。

Result: NED中的光子运动表现出真空双折射（vacuum birefringence），即光子根据偏振状态沿两条不同路径传播。这导致静态NED黑洞可存在两个不稳定光环（unstable light rings），形成双重阴影（two distinct shadows）。基于人马座A*（Sagittarius A*）的观测数据，对NED黑洞的荷质比（charge-to-mass ratio）设定了上限。

Abstract: One of the main features of nonlinear electrodynamics (NED) is the existence of an effective geometry that describes the geodesic motion of photons. A detailed analysis of the properties of effective geometry is of utmost importance for a better understanding of NED theories and their possible imprints on physics, especially in the context of black holes (BHs). We consider a NED model that depends on the two electromagnetic scalar invariants and obtain that the motion of photons in NED exhibits \textit{vacuum birefringence}, i.e., photons can propagate along two distinct paths, depending on their polarization. As a consequence of this phenomenon, we show that static black hole solutions sourced by NED can admit two distinct unstable light rings, leading to the formation of two distinct shadows. Moreover, to explore the potential astrophysical relevance of our results, we also compare them with the astrophysical observations for the shadow radius of Sagittarius A*. We place upper limits on the charge-to-mass ratio of the NED-sourced black hole. We also show that the motion of photons in this context can be interpreted as nongeodesic curves subjected to a four-force term from the perspective of an observer in the spacetime metric, generalizing previous results in the literature for NED models that depend on a single electromagnetic scalar invariant.

### [147] [Scattering of a scalar field in the four-dimensional quasi-topological gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17644)

Result: 灰体因子与史瓦西（Schwarzschild）情况仅有微小偏差，表明散射特性对几何近视界正则化（near-horizon regularization）基本不敏感；准正规模（quasinormal modes）与灰体因子之间的对应关系在高多极数（higher multipole numbers）下足够精确。

Conclusion: 规则黑洞的散射特性对几何正则化不敏感，灰体因子与史瓦西黑洞相似，且准正规模与灰体因子的对应关系在高多极数下保持良好精度。

Abstract: We study grey-body factors for a massless scalar field in the spacetime of regular black holes arising in four-dimensional non-polynomial quasi-topological gravity. We consider two representative metrics that capture the typical features of regular geometries. Using the WKB method, we compute the transmission probabilities and analyze their dependence on the regularization parameter. The grey-body factors are found to deviate only slightly from the Schwarzschild case, indicating that the scattering properties are largely insensitive to near-horizon regularization of the geometry. The correspondence between quasinormal modes and grey-body factors is shown to be sufficiently accurate for higher multipole numbers.

### [148] [Modified Friedmann equations and non-singular cosmologies in $d=4$ non-polynomial quasi-topological gravities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17654)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已知准拓扑引力理论（quasi-topological gravities）能解决黑洞奇点问题，本文旨在探究该机制是否同样能够消除宇宙学奇点（cosmological singularities），特别是大爆炸奇点（Big-Bang singularity）。

Method: 研究聚焦于四维（d=4）非多项式曲率准拓扑引力（non-polynomial curvature quasi-topological gravities），分析填充纯辐射或其他标准物质的宇宙模型，考察其红外极限（infrared limit）行为。

Result: 发现了三种具有正确红外极限且无大爆炸奇点的宇宙演化情景：1) 宇宙从德西特相（de Sitter phase）演化而来，曲率不变量有限但物质密度发散（仅在无限仿射距离处）；2) 反弹宇宙（bouncing universe），需要多值拉格朗日量；3) 渐进闵可夫斯基起源（asymptotically Minkowski origin），类似永恒徘徊宇宙（eternally loitering universe），物质能量密度非奇异且近似恒定。

Conclusion: 准拓扑引力理论确实能够消除宇宙学奇点，提供了三种无大爆炸奇点的宇宙起源模型，其中渐进闵可夫斯基起源模型尤其具有吸引力，因其物质密度非奇异且不进入超普朗克区域（super-Planckian regime）。

Abstract: Quasi-topological theories of gravity are known to resolve black-hole singularities. We investigate whether the same mechanism can remove cosmological singularities. Focusing on non-polynomial curvature quasi-topological gravities in $d=4$ dimensions, we find three generic scenarios with the correct infrared limit but without a Big-Bang singularity, for universes filled with pure radiation or other standard matter. The first scenario yields a universe emerging from a de Sitter phase, a case for which the curvature invariants remain finite but the matter density diverges, albeit only at infinite affine distance. The second one corresponds to a bouncing universe, which requires a multi-valued Lagrangian. The third possibility is an asymptotically Minkowski origin, reminiscent of an eternally loitering universe. The matter energy density for this solution is non-singular even at infinite affine distance and does not enter a super-Planckian regime, but is instead approximately constant for the past eternity.

### [150] [Electromagnetic radiation-reaction near black holes: orbital widening and the role of the tail](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17728)
*Bakhtinur Juraev,Arman Tursunov,Zdeněk Stuchlík,Martin Kološ,Dmitri V. Gal'tsov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该研究分析了带电粒子在施瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）外部均匀磁场中的轨道演化，同时考虑了局部辐射反作用（radiation-reaction）和弯曲时空中的非局域尾部自作用力（tail self-force）。研究发现轨道展宽效应（orbital widening effect）在包含尾部项时依然存在，且对于天体物理中现实的荷质比，尾部贡献可忽略不计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探究带电粒子在弯曲时空（curved spacetime）中同时受到外部磁场、局部辐射反作用和非局域尾部自作用力影响时的轨道动力学。这有助于理解天体物理黑洞环境中带电粒子的真实演化行为。

Method: 研究方法基于DeWitt-Brehme方程及其Landau-Lifshitz简化形式，推导了弱场（牛顿极限）和强场区域中电磁自作用力（electromagnetic self-force）的保守和耗散分量的解析表达式。通过实施向后时间积分（backward-in-time integration）来对比分析三阶DeWitt-Brehme方程和二阶Landau-Lifshitz方程。

Result: 研究结果表明，即使包含尾部项，轨道展宽效应依然存在，且对于天体物理中现实的荷质比（charge-to-mass ratios），尾部项对轨迹的贡献可忽略不计。该展宽效应直接由磁场和辐射反作用参数的乘积控制，并可在牛顿极限下捕捉到。

Conclusion: 研究结论确认了轨道展宽效应是一个稳健现象，即使在天体物理黑洞环境中也能持续存在。同时发现了一个标度对称性（scaling symmetry），表明使用中等参数值的模拟能准确代表现实天体物理条件下的动力学行为。

Abstract: We investigate the orbital evolution of a classical charged particle around a Schwarzschild black hole immersed in an external, uniform magnetic field, taking into full account both local radiation-reaction and the nonlocal tail self-force arising in curved spacetime. Starting from the DeWitt-Brehme equation and its Landau-Lifshitz reduction, we derive analytic expressions for the conservative and dissipative components of the electromagnetic self-force in both the weak-field (Newtonian) and strong-field regimes. By implementing backward-in-time integration of the third-order DeWitt-Brehme equation alongside the second-order Landau-Lifshitz equation, we demonstrate that the so-called orbital widening effect persists even when the tail term is included, and that for astrophysically realistic charge-to-mass ratios the tail contribution to the trajectory is negligible. We further show that this widening is directly controlled by the product of the magnetic field and radiation-reaction parameters and can be captured in the Newtonian limit. Finally, we identify a scaling symmetry showing that simulations with moderate parameter values can accurately represent the dynamics in realistic astrophysical conditions, confirming that orbital widening is a robust phenomenon that can persist even in astrophysical black hole environments.

### [151] [Non-linear instability of the Kerr Cauchy horizon near $i_+$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17911)
*Sebastian Gurriaran*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文证明了在满足特定非线性Price定律型估计的条件下，克尔（Kerr）黑洞内部时空在柯西视界（Cauchy horizon）处存在曲率发散和Lipschitz不可延拓性，从而支持了强宇宙监督假设（Strong Cosmic Censorship）的Lipschitz版本。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法基于Dafermos和Luk的克尔柯西视界C^0稳定性证明，以及Giorgi-Klainerman-Szeftel的非可积形式体系和Klainerman-Szeftel的主时间规范。通过将黑洞内部划分为不同区域并采用适当规范，分析Teukolsky方程的非线性类比，并应用Sbierski的Lipschitz不可延拓性判据。

Result: 证明了相应的最大整体双曲发展（maximal globally hyperbolic development）在类时无穷远$i_+$处存在非平凡的柯西视界（Cauchy horizon）片段，该处表现出曲率发散特性，且时空度规是Lipschitz不可延拓的。

Conclusion: 研究结果在Price定律型假设下，为克尔时空在类时无穷远附近的强宇宙监督假设（Strong Cosmic Censorship）提供了Lipschitz版本的证明，表明时空在柯西视界处存在本质奇异性。

Abstract: We consider solutions of the Einstein vacuum equations which arise from smooth initial data on a hypersurface slightly inside a dynamical black hole settling down to a subextremal Kerr black hole, and satisfying a precise non-linear Price's law-type estimate (which we expect to hold generically). We prove that the corresponding maximal globally hyperbolic development admits a non-trivial piece of future null boundary - the Cauchy horizon - emanating from timelike infinity $i_+$, which exhibits a kind of curvature blow-up, and across which the spacetime metric is Lipschitz-inextendible. Our results thus imply a Lipschitz version of Strong Cosmic Censorship for Kerr spacetimes near timelike infinity under this Price's law-type assumption.
  The analysis relies on the proof of the $C^0$ stability of the Kerr Cauchy horizon by Dafermos and Luk, on the non-integrable formalism of Giorgi-Klainerman-Szeftel and principal temporal gauge of Klainerman and Szeftel used in the proof of the exterior stability of slowly rotating Kerr black holes, on the linearized analysis for the Teukolsky equation inside subextremal Kerr black holes by the author, and on Sbierski's criterion for Lipschitz inextendibility. More precisely, we proceed by decomposing the black hole interior into different regions equipped with appropriate gauges, allowing for a proof of stability estimates and a thorough analysis of the non-linear analog of the Teukolsky equation, from which we infer our instability results.

### [152] [Energy extraction from a rotating Buchdahl star via magnetic reconnection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17928)

Motivation: 本研究旨在探索磁重联（MR）作为从快速旋转的布赫达尔星（BS）中提取能量的机制。BS是一种无视界（horizonless）的致密天体，其自旋参数理论上可以超过黑洞（BH）的极端极限，这使其成为研究高能天体物理过程潜在高效引擎的有趣对象。

Method: 采用科米索-阿森霍机制（Comisso-Asenjo mechanism）作为分析框架，评估快速旋转BS的能量提取效率和功率输出。重点分析由快速磁重联（fast magnetic reconnection）驱动的能量提取速率，并将其与布兰福德-兹纳耶克机制（Blandford-Znajek mechanism）的预测结果进行比较。

Result: 研究发现BS的能层（ergoregion）仅当自旋参数满足β>1/√2时才存在，因此磁重联提取旋转能量仅在此条件下可行。当BS自旋参数超过黑洞极端极限时，能量提取速率显著增加，磁重联的效率远高于布兰福德-兹纳耶克机制。

Conclusion: 磁重联能极大增强从大自旋快速旋转BS中提取能量的效率，使此类天体可能成为比黑洞更高效的高能天体物理过程引擎。这突显了无视界致密天体在能量提取机制研究中的重要性。

Abstract: In this work, we investigate the magnetic reconnection (MR) process as a mechanism for energy extraction from a rapidly rotating Buchdahl star (BS), one of the most compact horizonless objects that can, in principle, possess a spin parameter exceeding the extremal limit of a black hole (BH). We explore the energetics of the BS by focusing on the newly proposed MR mechanism developed by Comisso and Asenjo (the Comisso-Asenjo mechanism). Within this framework, we evaluate the energy extraction efficiency and the associated power output from a rapidly rotating BS. We show that the ergoregion of the BS exists only when the spin parameter satisfies $β>1/\sqrt{2}$. Consequently, the extraction of rotational energy through MR becomes possible only under this condition. Furthermore, we analyze the rate of energy extraction driven by fast magnetic reconnection and compare the resulting power with that predicted by the Blandford-Znajek mechanism. Our results indicate that the energy extraction rate increases significantly when the BS spin parameter exceeds the extremal limit for a BH, highlighting that MR can be substantially more efficient than the Blandford-Znajek mechanism. We demonstrate that MR can greatly enhance energy extraction efficiency from rapidly rotating BS with a large spin, making such an object potentially more efficient engines of high-energy astrophysical processes than BH.

</details>


### [153] [Observational Signatures of Exact Black Hole Solutions in a Dark Matter Halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17986)
*Azalbek Boltaev,Tursunali Xamidov,Sanjar Shaymatov*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本研究推导了嵌入Dehnen型暗物质（DM）晕密度分布的史瓦西（Schwarzschild）类黑洞（BH）的精确解，并分析了其几何、动力学和观测特征。通过研究视界结构、时空曲率不变量、能量条件、测地线行为，并利用弱场（水星、S2星轨道）和强场（EHT、GRAVITY等）观测数据进行贝叶斯推断，对DM晕参数施加了观测约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 本研究旨在探索暗物质（DM）晕环境对天体物理黑洞（BH）时空几何和可观测特性的潜在影响。通过构建嵌入Dehnen型DM晕的黑洞精确解，为研究黑洞与暗物质相互作用提供了一个替代视角。

Method: 首先推导了嵌入Dehnen型暗物质（DM）晕的史瓦西（Schwarzschild）类黑洞精确解。随后分析了视界结构、时空曲率不变量以及DM晕相关的能量条件。研究了DM晕对类时（timelike）和类光（null）测地线的影响。最后，利用贝叶斯推断（Bayesian inference）和马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法，通过弱场（水星、S2星轨道）和强场（Event Horizon Telescope, GRAVITY等）观测数据对DM晕参数进行约束。

Result: 获得了描述嵌入Dehnen型暗物质（DM）晕的黑洞的精确解，并分析了其几何和动力学特征。通过将模型预测与观测数据（包括M87*和Sgr A*的EHT、GRAVITY及联合数据集）进行比较，确定了模型参数的最佳拟合值和相应的上限，从而对DM晕参数施加了观测约束。

Conclusion: 该分析为探测暗物质（DM）晕环境对天体物理黑洞（BH）时空几何和可观测特性的潜在影响提供了有价值的见解。研究结果为理解黑洞与暗物质相互作用提供了一个替代视角。

Abstract: In this work, we derive novel exact solutions describing Schwarzschild-like black holes (BHs) embedded in a Dehnen-type dark matter (DM) halo density profile and investigate their geometric, dynamical, and observational signatures arising from such geometries. We begin by analyzing the horizon structure and spacetime curvature invariants, as well as examining the energy conditions associated with the DM halo. Subsequently, we study the influence of the DM halo on both timelike and null geodesics in the resulting geometry. Finally, we obtain observational constraints on the DM halo parameters by comparing the model predictions with weak-field data from Mercury and the S2 star orbit, as well as strong-field observations from the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT), GRAVITY, and combined (EHT+GRAVITY) datasets for M87* and Sgr A*, employing Bayesian inference and Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) methods to determine the best-fit values and corresponding upper limits of the model parameters. Our analysis provides valuable insight into probing the potential influence of DM halo environments on spacetime geometry and observable properties of astrophysical BHs, offering an alternative perspective on BH-DM interactions.

### [154] [Resonant field emission from noble-metal/graphene heterostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.16997)
*Maxim Trushin*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究展示了石墨烯包覆贵金属的场发射特性，其非单调I-V特性源于通过石墨烯电子态的共振隧穿，为金属异质结构中的可调电子传输提供了实用途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 金属场发射技术支撑了早期真空管技术，但金属中电子传输的可调性有限限制了其应用。本研究旨在探索通过石墨烯包覆贵金属实现可调电子传输的新途径。

Method: 研究结合了从头算（ab-initio）界面参数与薛定谔方程（Schrödinger equation）电子传输的精确解，分析了两种实验相关几何构型：具有平坦悬浮发射极的垂直构型和具有尖锐电极的共面构型。

Result: 石墨烯包覆的贵金属表现出清洁的非单调I-V特性，这源于通过石墨烯电子态的共振隧穿（resonant tunneling），得益于石墨烯的原子级薄度和与贵金属的弱电子杂化。

Conclusion: 该研究为金属异质结构中的可调电子传输建立了实用途径，使其成为空气通道场发射纳米电子学（air-channel field-emission nanoelectronics）中具有竞争力的组件。

Abstract: Field emission from metals underpinned early vacuum-tube technology, and recent nanoscale engineering made field-emission devices compatible with modern silicon platforms. However, the limited tunability of electron transport in metals has restricted their applicability. Here, we show that noble metals coated with graphene exhibit clean non-monotonic $I-V$ characteristics arising from resonant tunneling through graphene's electronic states, enabled by graphene's atomic thinness and weak electronic hybridization with noble metals. Our approach combines ab-initio interface parameters with exact solutions of the Schrödinger equation for electron transmission across the interface. We analyze two experimentally relevant geometries: a vertical configuration with a flat suspended emitter and a coplanar configuration with sharp electrodes allowing for strong field enhancement and gating. These results establish a practical route to tunable electron transport in metal heterostructures, positioning them as competitive components for air-channel field-emission nanoelectronics.

### [155] [Magnetically tunable telecom emission from Er3+ ions in layered WS2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17118)
*Guadalupe Garcia-Arellano,Gabriel I. Lopez-Morales,Johannes Flick,Cyrus E. Dreyer,Carlos A. Meriles*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论分析，揭示了Er³⁺离子在WS₂层状材料中的电信波段发射特性，发现磁场可通过塞曼效应（Zeeman effect）调控发射偶极子的强度和取向，并识别了WS₂作为结合低退相干与光子兼容性的新型量子平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Er³⁺离子具有电信波段的磁偶极跃迁特性，适用于量子通信和自旋-光子接口，但寻找兼具低退相干和光子兼容性的宿主材料仍是一个核心挑战。本研究旨在探索WS₂层状材料作为Er³⁺宿主环境的潜力。

Method: 研究采用时间分辨和偏振分辨的光致发光（photoluminescence）技术，在中等磁场（< 0.2 T）下测量WS₂薄片中Er³⁺的发射特性。基于密度泛函理论（density functional theory）参数化的有效模型计算，分析了Er³⁺在单层WS₂中的能级结构。

Result: 实验观察到当磁场具有面外分量时，Er³⁺发射出现显著变暗、寿命延长和发射偶极子旋转，而面内磁场影响较小。理论分析表明这些效应主要源于塞曼诱导的近简并晶体场（crystal-field）子能级混合，改变了光学跃迁偶极矩的大小和取向。不同厚度薄片的比较测量和局域光学态密度（local density of optical states）的数值估计进一步表明，偶极子与薄WS₂层各向异性光子环境的耦合也起到次要作用。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，层状WS₂是一个可通过磁场调控电信波段发射的平台，这种调控源于晶体场物理和各向异性光子耦合的相互作用。该发现为开发基于Er³⁺的量子技术提供了新的材料选择。

Abstract: Erbium ions (Er3+) provide a telecom-band optical transition with strong magnetic-dipole character, making them attractive for quantum communication and spin-photon interfaces. Identifying host environments that combine low decoherence with photonic compatibility, however, remains a central challenge. Here we investigate Er3+ emission in tungsten disulfide (WS2) flakes, a layered host offering low nuclear-spin density and narrow telecom emission. Using time- and polarization-resolved photoluminescence under modest magnetic fields (< 0.2 T), we observe pronounced dimming, lifetime extension, and rotation of the emission dipole when the field has an out-of-plane component, whereas in-plane fields produce little change. Effective model calculations of Er3+ in monolayer WS2 parametrized from density functional theory indicate that these effects arise primarily from Zeeman-induced mixing of near-degenerate crystal-field sublevels, which modifies the magnitude and orientation of the optical transition dipole moments. Comparative measurements in flakes of different thickness and numerical estimates of the local density of optical states further suggest a secondary contribution from dipole coupling to the anisotropic photonic environment of thin WS2 layers. These findings identify layered WS2 as a platform where magnetic fields can tune telecom emission through an interplay of crystal-field physics and anisotropic photonic coupling.
