### [156] [Spontaneous Polarization Suppression of Exciton-Exciton Annihilation in 3R-Stacked MoS$_2$ Bilayers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17215)
*Tae Gwan Park,Xufan Li,Kyungnam Kang,David B. Geohegan,Christopher M. Rouleau,Alexander A. Puretzky,Kai Xiao*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 在3R堆叠MoS₂双层中，通过自发极化产生的层间激子间排斥性偶极-偶极相互作用，显著抑制了激子-激子湮灭（EEA）过程，为高密度激子体系提供了新途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 二维半导体中快速的激子-激子湮灭（exciton-exciton annihilation, EEA）限制了高密度激子体系的实现，而这对强激发下的高效光电器件操作至关重要。研究旨在探索抑制EEA的机制。

Method: 采用超快泵浦-探测光谱（ultrafast pump-probe spectroscopy）测量不同结构MoS₂的EEA速率。通过建立包含偶极-偶极排斥势的速率限制湮灭模型（rate-limited annihilation model）来分析实验数据。

Result: 3R双层中的EEA速率γ_EEA为(5.03±0.99)×10⁻³ cm² s⁻¹，比单层低约18.2倍，比非极性2H双层低约2.9倍。观测到的γ_EEA,3R/γ_EEA,2H≈0.35比值与激子-激子相遇距离约1.3 nm相符，接近双层激子玻尔半径。

Conclusion: 3R堆叠双层中的自发极化通过排斥性偶极-偶极相互作用抑制了非线性激子损失，为实现高密度激子体系提供了有效途径。

Abstract: Rapid exciton-exciton annihilation (EEA) in two-dimensional semiconductors limits access to high-density excitonic regimes essential for efficient optoelectronic operation under strong excitation. Here, we show that EEA is suppressed by repulsive dipole-dipole interactions between interlayer excitons polarized by the spontaneous polarization intrinsic to rhombohedral (3R)-stacked MoS$_2$ bilayers. Using ultrafast pump-probe spectroscopy, we measure an EEA rate of $γ_{\rm EEA}=(5.03\pm0.99)\times10^{-3}$ cm$^2$ s$^{-1}$ in 3R bilayers, which is approximately 18.2-fold smaller than that in monolayers and 2.9-fold smaller than that in nonpolar 2H bilayers. Despite the higher exciton diffusivity recently reported for 3R relative to 2H bilayers, the reduced EEA rate in 3R indicates a rate-limited regime governed by the close-encounter annihilation probability rather than diffusion. A rate-limited annihilation model incorporating a dipole-dipole repulsive potential captures the observed ratio $γ_{{\rm EEA},3{\rm R}}/γ_{{\rm EEA},2{\rm H}}\approx0.35$ for an exciton-exciton encounter distance of $\sim$1.3 nm, consistent with the bilayer exciton Bohr radius. These results show that spontaneous polarization in 3R-stacked bilayers suppresses nonlinear excitonic losses and provides a route toward high-density excitonics.

</details>


### [157] [Phonon circular birefringence and polarization-filter in Magnetic Topological Insulators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17274)
*Abhinava Chatterjee,Chao-Xing Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文提出了一种由表面声子霍尔黏度（surface phonon Hall viscosity）诱导的声子极化滤波机制，能够在磁拓扑绝缘体中产生界面声子模式，实现声子极化和角动量的选择性传输。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 表面声子霍尔黏度（surface phonon Hall viscosity）作为轴子电动力学的声学类比，在磁拓扑绝缘体中产生新颖的声学现象。本研究旨在探索由表面声子霍尔黏度诱导的先前未被研究过的效应。

Method: 提出了一种声子极化滤波机制，该机制由表面声子霍尔黏度诱导，产生频率低于体模频率的界面声子模式。进一步开发了广义散射框架（generalized scattering framework），研究从平凡绝缘体到磁拓扑绝缘体的声波注入效应，包括正入射和斜入射情况。

Result: 界面声子模式具有特定的圆极化（circular polarization），可作为极化滤波器，仅将匹配极化的声子限制在界面处。磁拓扑绝缘体能够选择性传输一种类型的圆极化声子模式，实现声子极化和角动量的操控。研究还讨论了表面声学法拉第旋转（surface acoustic Faraday rotation）和纵-横模式转换（longitudinal-transverse mode conversion）现象。

Conclusion: 表面霍尔黏度成为工程化轴向声子态（axial phonon states）的强大机制，为基于声子角动量（phonon angular momentum）的拓扑声子器件开辟了新途径。

Abstract: The surface phonon Hall viscosity (PHV)-an acoustic analog of axion electrodynamics-emerges from the strain response of magnetic topological insulators and gives rise to novel acoustic phenomena. In this work, we propose a previously unexplored effect: a phonon polarization-filter mechanism induced by the surface PHV, which generates an interface phonon mode with its frequency below the bulk mode frequency. This interface mode possesses a specific circular polarization and therefore acts as a polarization filter, confining only phonons with the matching polarization at the interface. Magnetic topological insulators can thus selectively transmit one type of circularly polarized phonon mode, enabling the manipulation of phonon polarization and angular momentum. In addition, we further develop a generalized scattering framework to study the effect of an injected acoustic wave from a trivial insulator to a magnetic topological insulator with both normal and oblique incidence, and discuss the phenomena of surface acoustic Faraday rotation and longitudinal-transverse mode conversion. Our results establish surface Hall viscosity as a powerful mechanism for engineering axial phonon states and open new avenues for topological phononic devices based on phonon angular momentum.

</details>


### [158] [Symmetry-Enforced Nodal $f$-Wave Magnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17406)
*Hirschmann Moritz M.,Furusaki Akira,Hirschberger Max*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过引入自旋空间对称性（spin-space symmetries）解决了非共线磁体中自旋极化和能带分裂定义的模糊性，构建了蜂窝双层结构上的巡游电子紧束缚模型，预测了节点结构引起的自旋电导和表面p波磁性诱导的体禁戒Edelstein效应。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在非共线磁体中，交替自旋纹理（alternating spin textures）既可能出现在孤立能带中，也可能出现在具有节点分裂的相交能带对中，这引发了关于p波、f波等磁体应基于自旋极化还是能带分裂来定义的模糊性问题。

Method: 为解决这一模糊性，研究引入了耦合所有能带自旋极化和分裂纹理的自旋空间对称性。针对节点f波磁体，构建了蜂窝双层结构上巡游电子与非共线磁纹理耦合的紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）。

Result: 自旋极化和分裂的解析表达式揭示了其对跳跃和交换耦合的依赖关系。研究预测了由分裂节点结构引起的倾斜诱导自旋电导（canting-induced spin conductivity）。此外，体相f波磁体可在表面诱导p波磁性。

Conclusion: 表面p波特性导致了具有f波各向异性的体禁戒Edelstein效应（bulk-forbidden Edelstein effect）。该研究通过自旋空间对称性框架澄清了非共线磁体中自旋纹理与能带分裂的关系，为自旋电子学应用提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Owing to their relevance for spintronics, electronic band splitting and spin-polarization textures in magnets are active areas of research. In non-collinear magnets, alternating spin textures can arise both for isolated bands and for intersecting band pairs with nodal splitting. This raises the question of whether $p,f,...$-wave magnets should be defined by their spin polarization or their band splitting. To resolve this ambiguity, we introduce spin-space symmetries that couple the spin polarization and splitting textures for all bands. Focusing on the nodal $f$-wave magnet, we construct a tight-binding model of itinerant electrons on a honeycomb bilayer coupled to a non-collinear magnetic texture. Analytic expressions for spin polarization and splitting reveal the dependence on hopping and exchange coupling. We predict a canting-induced spin conductivity arising from the nodal structure of the splitting. Furthermore, the $f$-wave magnet in the bulk can induce $p$-wave magnetism on the surface. This surface $p$-wave character leads to a bulk-forbidden Edelstein effect with $f$-wave anisotropy.

</details>


### [159] [Polarization-Aligned, Spectrally Consistent Quantum Emitters in As-Exfoliated Carbon-Doped Hexagonal Boron Nitride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17440)
*Sofiya Karankova,Yeunjeong Lee,Seungmin Park,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Jin-Dong Song,Young Duck Kim,Yong-Won Song,Hyowon Moon*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固态量子发射器是集成量子光子电路的关键组件，但六方氮化硼（hBN）量子光源存在多步制备工艺、缺陷特异性有限和发射波长重复性差等问题。开发适用于平面光子器件且具有一致光学特性的发射器诱导方法仍是关键目标。

Method: 研究在未经后处理（as-exfoliated）的碳掺杂六方氮化硼（carbon-doped hBN）中识别量子发射器，这些发射器在原子级薄晶格中展现出稳定且可重复的发射特性。

Result: 量子发射器表现出卓越的光谱稳定性（标准偏差7 μeV），发射能量可重复且局限在2.2825 ± 0.0042 eV的窄范围内。吸收和发射偏振的一致偶极子对齐表明内在缺陷具有相同性质。

Conclusion: 未经后处理的hBN中可重复、偏振对齐的量子发射器为可扩展集成提供了多功能平台，为广泛的量子技术应用开辟了途径，显著促进了与平面光子结构的进一步接口。

Abstract: Solid-state quantum emitters constitute an essential building blocks of integrated quantum photonic circuits. Among potential emitter platforms, hexagonal boron nitride (hBN) hosts single-photon emitters in an atomically thin lattice amenable to photonic integration. However, multi-step fabrication approaches, limited defect specificity, and poor emission wavelength repeatability limit the performance of hBN quantum light sources relative to established solid-state architectures. Developing methods to induce emitters that are both suitable for planar photonic devices and that exhibit consistent optical properties remains a key objective. In this work, we identify quantum emitters in as-exfoliated carbon-doped hBN that exhibit both stable and repeatable emission energies together with polarization-aligned dipoles. Owing to the high lattice crystallinity, these single-photon light sources demonstrate exceptional spectral stability with a standard deviation of 7 $μ$eV. The emission energy is reproducible and confined within a narrow range of 2.2825 ${\pm}$ 0.0042 eV. Notably, consistent dipole alignment for absorption and emission polarization suggests that the intrinsic defects are of the same nature. The color centers are observed in as-exfoliated hBN without any post-treatment, significantly facilitating further interfacing with planar photonic structures. These reproducible, polarization-aligned quantum emitters in as-exfoliated hBN provide a versatile platform for scalable integration, offering a pathway toward a broad range of quantum technologies.

### [160] [Strain-driven spin mixing and dark-exciton recombination in a neutral Ni2+ doped quantum dot](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17752)
*K. E. Polczynska,S. Karouaz,W. Pacuski,L. Besombes*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过分析CdTe/ZnTe量子点中单个Ni²⁺离子的中性激子光学特性，揭示了局域应变环境对磁性离子与激子自旋耦合的关键调控作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究旨在探究半导体量子点中过渡金属掺杂剂的自旋-激子耦合机制，特别关注局域应变环境如何影响Ni²⁺离子的自旋态混合及其与激子的相互作用。

Method: 通过测量含单个Ni²⁺离子的CdTe/ZnTe量子点的光致发光光谱，分析应变诱导的自旋态混合特征；采用包含应变取向和价带混合的有效自旋哈密顿量（effective spin Hamiltonian）模拟亮激子和暗激子光谱的磁场演化。

Result: 实验发现局域应变张量主轴与量子点生长方向的错位会重新定向磁性离子的自旋量子化轴，导致低磁场下空穴-Ni²⁺交换相互作用减弱，并在部分线偏振亮激子跃迁周围产生光致发光复制峰；纵向磁场可恢复圆偏振光学选择定则，使Ni²⁺离子的三个自旋投影S_z = 0, ±1得以光谱分辨；暗激子发射出现在光谱低能侧，低场下主要由涉及磁性离子自旋翻转的跃迁主导。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明局域应变环境在决定半导体量子点中过渡金属掺杂剂的自旋-激子耦合方面起着关键作用，为理解和调控量子点中磁性离子与激子的相互作用提供了重要见解。

Abstract: We investigate the optical properties of neutral excitons in CdTe/ZnTe quantum dots containing a single Ni2+ ion. We show that the photoluminescence spectra provide a direct spectroscopic signature of strain induced mixing of the Ni2+ spin states. A misalignment between the principal axis of the local strain tensor and the quantum dot growth direction reorients the spin quantization axis of the magnetic ion, reducing the hole Ni2+ exchange interaction at low magnetic field and giving rise to photoluminescence replicas around the partially linearly polarized bright-exciton transitions. A longitudinal magnetic field restores the circularly polarized optical selection rules, allowing the three spin projections S_z = 0, +-1 of the Ni2+ ion to be spectrally resolved. Dark exciton emission appears on the low energy side of the spectra and is dominated at low field by transitions involving spin flips of the magnetic ion. An effective spin Hamiltonian including strain orientation and valence band mixing reproduces the magnetic field evolution of both bright and dark exciton spectra. These results highlight the key role of the local strain environment in determining the spin exciton coupling of transition metal dopants in semiconductor quantum dots.

</details>


### [161] [Magneto-rotation coupling dominates surface acoustic wave driven ferromagnetic resonance in the longitudinal geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17758)
*Gyuyoung Park,OukJae Lee,Jintao Shuai*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文为mumax+微磁框架开发了声子-磁子扩展，实现了三种表面声波耦合机制，并通过六个基准模拟验证了实现效果，展示了磁旋转耦合在特定几何条件下成为主导驱动机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在扩展mumax+微磁框架，以模拟表面声波（SAW）与磁系统的耦合机制，包括磁弹性应变耦合、磁旋转耦合和自旋旋转（Barnett）耦合，从而更全面地研究声子-磁子相互作用。

Method: 研究开发了mumax+微磁框架的声子-磁子扩展，实现了三种表面声波耦合机制：磁弹性应变耦合、源于反对称位移梯度的磁旋转耦合，以及源于晶格角速度的自旋旋转（Barnett）耦合。

Result: 通过六个基准模拟验证了实现效果，包括SAW驱动的畴壁运动、磁化翻转、磁旋转和Barnett场验证、瑞利波手性导致的非互易SAW-磁子吸收，以及驻波腔中的空间分辨耦合。在纵向几何条件下，磁弹性耦合产生零横向力矩，而磁旋转通道成为唯一驱动机制。

Conclusion: 对于钇铁石榴石（YIG）参数，磁旋转主导的交叉角约为1.1度。通过将磁旋转耦合常数K_mr作为可调参数，绘制了协同性相图，显示仅磁旋转耦合即可实现强耦合（K_mr = 1 MJ/m³时C = 257），避免交叉分裂为13.6 MHz。

Abstract: We present a phonon-magnon extension for the mumax+ micromagnetic framework that implements three surface acoustic wave (SAW) coupling mechanisms: magnetoelastic strain coupling, magneto-rotation coupling arising from the antisymmetric displacement gradient, and spin-rotation (Barnett) coupling from the lattice angular velocity. Six benchmark simulations validate the implementation through SAW-driven domain-wall motion, magnetization switching, magneto-rotation and Barnett field validation, nonreciprocal SAW-magnon absorption from Rayleigh-wave chirality, and spatially resolved coupling in a standing SAW cavity. For the longitudinal geometry (m_0 parallel to k_SAW), we show that the magnetoelastic coupling produces zero transverse torque despite generating a 50 times larger effective field; the magneto-rotation channel provides the sole driving mechanism. The crossover angle below which MR dominates is theta_c approximately 1.1 degrees for YIG parameters. Treating the magneto-rotation coupling constant K_mr as a tunable parameter, we map out the cooperativity phase diagram and show that MR alone can achieve strong coupling (C = 257 for K_mr = 1 MJ/m^3) with an avoided-crossing splitting of 13.6 MHz.

</details>


### [162] [Strongly entangled Quantum Spin Rings driven by Hückel rule](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17854)
*Manish Kumar,Deng-Yuan Li,Zhangyu Yuan,Ying Wang,Diego Soler-Polo,Enzo Monino,Libor Veis,Yi-Jun Wang,Xin-Yu Zhang,Can Li,Jinfeng Jia,Pei-Nian Liu,Pavel Jelinek,Shiyong Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该研究通过表面合成π磁性碳基大环，揭示了量子自旋环中强相互作用导致的非传统反铁磁序和高度简并受挫磁基态，建立了基于Hückel芳香性概念的新型设计原理。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子自旋环（quantum spin rings）是研究非常规磁序和奇异量子相的平台，也是新兴量子技术的有前景材料。传统自旋系统由弱相互作用的局域自旋组成，但强相互作用的自旋环表现出超越海森堡模型（Heisenberg model）的复杂行为。

Method: 通过表面合成（on-surface synthesis）方法实验制备了由[2]三角烯（[2]triangulene）单元组成的π磁性碳基大环（π-magnetic carbon-based macrocycles）。结合扫描隧道谱（scanning tunneling spectroscopy）和多参考计算（multireference calculations）揭示了电子结构与Hückel芳香性规则（Hückel aromaticity rule）的密切关联。

Result: 强相互作用导致未配对电子总数波动和非平凡反铁磁序（non-trivial antiferromagnetic order）。偶数元环的电子结构由4n/4n+2 Hückel（反）芳香性概念主导，而奇数元环则具有高度简并的受挫磁基态（highly degenerate frustrated magnetic ground state）。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了基于Hückel芳香性概念的量子自旋大环新型设计原理（novel design principle），为理解和设计具有特定量子特性的自旋系统提供了新途径。

Abstract: Quantum spin rings represent an intriguing platform for studying unconventional magnetic order and exotic quantum phases, and they are also promising materials for emerging quantum technologies. Conventional spin systems consist of a set of weakly interacting localized spins that are well described by the Heisenberg spin models. Here, we demonstrate that strong interactions between radical centers in macrocycles of different sizes lead to fluctuations in the total number of unpaired electrons and to non-trivial antiferromagnetic order that extends beyond the Heisenberg picture. We demonstrate that the electronic structure of these spin rings is governed by the concept of 4n/4n+2 Hückel (anti)aromaticity for even-membered rings, whereas odd-membered rings possess a highly degenerate frustrated magnetic ground state. The strongly coupled spin rings are experimentally realized through the on-surface synthesis of π-magnetic carbon-based macrocycles, which consist of [2]triangulene units. The close correlation between the electronic structure and the Hückel aromaticity rule is revealed by scanning tunneling spectroscopy and multireference calculations. This work establishes a novel design principle employing the concept of Hückel aromaticity for quantum spin macrocycles.

</details>
